genealogical chart avncient historie onely trewe ſyncere cronicle warres betwixte grecian troyans ſubſequently fyrſt euer cyon auncient famouſe cytye troye vnder lamedon king laſte fynall deſtruction ſame vnder pryam wrytten daretus troyan dictus grecian ſouldiours preſent ſayde warres digeſted latyn lerned guydo de columpnis ſythes tranſlated englyſhe verſe iohn lydgate moncke burye newly imprinted mdlv reader although battayles betwixte grecyans troyans laſte fynall euerſion ye cyty troy hiſſtorye worthye eterne memorye hath paſſed penne ſundry famouſe poetes great clerkes grekes latynes homer vergyle ouyde others whych theyr workes ther came handes moſt men haue therfore hytherto ben holden chiefeſt reporter hyſtorye neuertheleſſe part lye affection towardes theyr countreythemen homer fauourynge grecyans virgyle ouyde troyans partelye breakynge ſayth theyr poetycall fiction hiſtorye ſo peruerted verye trouthe therof theyr dygeſtes maye hope fynde trouthe theyr doynges haue onely laboured tranſlators virgyle homer theyr peculyer vulgare language eaſelye conſydered whome although ſome confeſſe haue learnedlye ryghte well perfourmed theyr enterpryſe therin yet hath ben ſome ſo beaſtly bolde vndertake wtout eyther wyt learning tranſlate ſame hiſtory namelye eanedes virgyle englyſhe vnderſtandynge ſearſe word virgile mēt worke example man ſtudyouſe hiſtorye ſhoulde ſeke fynde ſame doynges wyllyam caxton leawde recueil troye ſhoulde fynde thyncke aſſuredlye none thynge longe tedious brayneles bablyng tendyng end▪ hauyng certayne begynnynge proceadynge therin ydyot follye make ende tyll bydden muche lyke foolyſhe vnſauerye doynges oreſtes iuuinall remembreth wryt booke iuſte volume filled mergentes outwarde ſydes madnes whych wythout conſydered tended purpoſe whych caxton recueil ſo lyſt wyth iudgement peruſe ſhall rather thyncke doynges worthye nūbred amongeſt trifelinge tale barrayne luerdries robyn hode beuys hampton remaine monumēt ſo worthy hiſtory yet hath wanted faythful trew reporter ye hiſtorye daretus phrigyan dytus grecyan curyouſe worthy dedes theyr countreithes lykewyſe preſēt al ſayd warres haue dyligently regeſtred ſame whoſe bokes although iniurye tyme long extant yet laſt beyng founde athene haue ſins dewe conference ben founde hooly agre dyſcourſe ye ſayd warres labores aſwel darete dyte laſte came ſyght handes lerned dylygent guydo columpna hath ſyncerelye pythely digeſted ſame one latyne volume ſo theſe degree hath bene laſte ye diligence iohn lydgate moncke burye brought englyſhe tonge dygeſted maye appere verſe eſtranayle well doynges hathe wythout doubte ſo muche preuayled vulgare language hauynge prayſe dewe deſeruynges may worthyly numbred amongeſt thoſe haue chefelye deſerued tunge verye perfect diſciple imitator great chaucer ye onelye glorye beauty ſame neuertheles lykewyſe hapned ye ſame chaucer leaſe ye prayſe tyme wherin wrote beyng dede al good letter almoſt aſlepe ſo farre groſeneſſe barbarouſneſſe age vnderſtā dinge ſo deuyne wryter bene time wherin kindes learnyng thancked god haue much floryſhed euer anye former dayes within realme namelye dylygence one willyam thime gentilmā laudably ſtudyouſe ye polyſhing ſo great iewell ryghte good iudgement trauail great paynes cauſing ſame ꝑfected ſtamped nowe read ye ſayde chaucer workes vtterly peryſhed ye leſt bin ſo depraued corrupcion copy laſte ſhoulde parte hys meaning haue ben founde euen ſame iniurye almoſt hathe happened wryter pamphlite euerciō troye printed xlii yeares agoe euen tayle hapned dercke vnlearned time ſuche ignoraunce bothe prynter correctour neyther ſhoulde ſeme eyther learned dnderſtandynge engliſhe yt ye ſame worke ſo falſed verſe either lacke foliſhe ſurplus diſplaſinge ye wordes thereby ye ſentence cōſequētlye ye hiſtorye ſo confuſed obſcured moſt place almoſt nothing gathered therof therfore muche meruaylinge hath happened whether lack copy dede otherwiſe yt boke thouly trew ſincere engliſh cronicle ſo worthye hiſtorye whervpon ſo many great clerkes language haue voutſafed theyr trauayles hath tyme whiche deede lacketh haue already doynges ſhewed ſelfes haue ryght good iudgement language bin purged falſyties reduſed nere mgiht conueniēce auctours tranſlation haue therfore taken vpon one ſtudyous ye language countreyth although muſt confeſſe ye leaſt able great nūbre bring hiſtorian lyght ſomewhat truſte perfecte poliſhed inuertyng therin eyther matter ſentence leauyng auctour commendacyon right apperteineth natheles would haue ben withdrawen myne attempte wt myght iuſtly haue recompted wt ſelfe conſyder great enterpriſe vndertaketh goeth aboute brynge perfected handes men ye corrupted labour former wryters howe lyttle thanke gained therby ſhulde neuer haue dared haue beſtowed hereof one penful yncke conſideryng ſo trauaylethe mennes doynges thought nothinge ſelfe therby ſome men iudgmentes hath hād thancke deſerueth ſuch ſhal ſo diſcerne hereof may accompt iudgement like indifferent mās ſhould iudge whych hath purged ouergrowē felde thornes ſtones hath alſo ſowed ye ſame wyth corne ſhuld ye end partaker ye fruytes increaſe therof ſurelye ſo euer ſhall take vpon hym thus trauayle others men labores whether ye lyſt waye ye difficultie thing commoditye pleaſure ſhall enſewe theym deſirous vnderſtande pryueties engliſhe tonge thincketh ſuch one worthy praiſe may ſay iudgemēt trauayle ought thought muche leſſe writeth owne inuēcyō one commend ye quickenes ye witt thother declareth ripenes iudgement hauyng large fielde diſcourſe thother cōpelled withī ye ſtraight boūdes ye writer one may vſe ye frugalitye inuencion wytt thother muſt ſo moderate ſame yt hath greateſt neade therof yet may paſſe lmittes one onely copye muſt peruſed many exāplars loked ouer therin maye choſe ſuch lyketh fantaſye yt ſhal ſeme come nere ye auctours meninge maye moſt pleaſe pleaſure reader therin ſhall compelled put theyr fantaſye yet ſo ſparinglye yt maye neither adde take awaye ſhalbe thereto ledd certaine ſure iudgmentes al thinges eaſie ſo liſt practiſe ſame maye ſone diſcerne thus muche haue thought good ſet wrytynge worke thend reader maye admonyſhed without trewe ſincere engliſhe hiſtoryan lamentable battels deſtinye vtter euerſion auncient famouſe cytye troye alſo preuent malice ſuche ſhal happlye accompte trauayle herein rather raſhe preſumpcyon anye vertuouſe imitacion wel doynge finis 〈…〉 robert braham ¶the prologue tranſlatour myghty mar wt thy ſterne lyght army haſt power ye myght named arte eaſte tyl occident myghty lorde god armipotent ſhininge thy ſtremes rede influence doſt brydell lede chiualrie ſoueraygne patron full hote drye complexion irous woode malencolyke nature brent collerike colour ſhininge like fiery glede whoſe ferſe lokes ben ful drede leuene alighteth lowe downe ſkies iupiter bowe bene thy ſtremes paſſing diſpyteous beholde ſo inly furious thou cauſer art thy fyrie beames werre ſtrife many ſūdrye realmes whoſe lordſhyp cheifeſt capricorne crabbe thy power lorne cauſer art conteke ſtrife loue vlcanus wife whilom yu miſchiefe take helpe onely ſake loue thy bellona dwelleth beyonde cirrha lybye londe vpon ſandes rede helpe great nede ſuccour ſtile dyrecte penne trace correcte whiche barrayne aureat lycoure thy grace finde ſome ſuccoure conuoy thine influence ſtumbleth aye fault eloquence reherſe writen worde helpe mar yt art knighthode lorde haſt manhode magnificence goddes yt arne highe prudence worke texplete ye refuſe maketh clyo muſe ſyſtren pernaſus dwelle cirrha helycon welle renning full cleare ſtremes criſtallyn called fountayne caballyn ſpringeth touche pegaſe helpe alſo thou callyope mother vnto orpheus whoſe dytees ſo melodius werbles reſowninge harpe appeaſed wordes ſherpe bothe parchas furyes infernall cerberus ſo cruell founde coyed alſo bothe beaſt foule tree thy grace helpyng vnto thy golden dewe let lycoure wete dulled breſt thy hony ſwete sugreſt tunges rethoryciens mayſtreſſe art muſciens mine helpe tenlumine wt thy worke beſet cloudes dimme derke ignoraunce making procede theym luſtye ſhall reade herte ſo full drede whan prudent lyſters hereto ſhall take hede makinge ſkill voucheſafe pray full beningly theyr goodneſſe haue compaſſion erre tranſlacion god take highly witneſſe worke hertie lowe humbleſſe toke vpon good entencion deuoyde pride al preſumpcion obey withouten varyaunce lordes biddynge fully pleſaunce hath deſyre ſothely ſayne knighthod reporte agayne worthineſſe ſo ſhall lye eke proweſſe olde cheualrye bycauſe hath ioye great deintye reade bokes olde antiquitye finde onely howe may vertue ſewe theyr ample alſo eſchewe curſed vyce ſlouthe idelneſſe enioyneth verteous buſineſſe yt longeth manhode dare ſayne buſyeth therto ſo fayne haunte bodye playes marciall exerciſe exclude ſlouthe doctrine vigecius thus manfull eke vertuous paſſingly hym write want conning renowne endite much manhode men may ſene witen whō would meane eldeſt ſonne noble kinge hēry ye fourth knighthode well ſpring ſhewed ſtock grewe rootis vertue thus ſett renewe 〈1 page duplicate〉 〈1 page duplicate〉 euery parte tarage ſame lyke father maners name ſothfaſtnes fable called henry eke ye worthy prince wale ¶to ſhall longe ſucceſſion gouerne brutis albion hath bydde drery pyteous fate troye ynglyſhe tranſlate ſiege alſo deſtruction lyke latyn maketh mencion compile guido make could write ſake bycauſe would highe lowe noble ſtorye openly knowe tunge euery age written well language latyn frenſhe ſtorye truthe mys doth eche nacion fine entencion ¶the empriſe anon ginne ſhall worſhyp memoryall tyme maken mencion whan began tranſlation yeare ſothly ſeyne fourtene complete tho father reygne time yeare ſhortly conclude whan xx grees phebus altitude hour whā hath made ſtedes draw roſen chariet lowe vnder wawe bathe beames wawy ſea greſed lyke golde men myght playnly ſe paſſyng bordure occion lucina coloure pale wan colde ariſynge octobre dyght tenchaſe darkenes froſty nyght amiddes scorpion heſperus gan faſt weſter courſe haſte againe morowe gray lucifer nyght voyd away meſſenger called day hemiſpher put affray bright kalēdes phebus vpriſt ſhene ye boundes proſerpin ye quene pluto dwelleth darke region furyes haue theyr manſion tyll ſoone apollo lyſt tarye take ſoiourne sagittarye ¶which time gan prologue behold troye boke ymade dayes olde written auctours v beforne al dede trewe corne fell ſeuered chaffe hande holde ſtaffe truth onely haue compyled vnto fyne begiled necligence thorough foryetfulneſſe ſerpent age longe proceſſe engendred fierſely v aſſayle trouth maken v fayle nere writer minde ſtoryed onely nature kinde true knowing ſhuld haue gon wrake wittes ſcyence put abacke ne elder ſerched ſoughte ſothfaſt pythe impe thought thinges paſſed fordyrked theyr hewe writing refreſhed new aūceters left v hynde make myrrour onely minde ſe eche thinge truly bright cleare glaſſe nere theyr writynge nowe memoryall death wt ſwerde ſhuld haue ſlayne ydimmed ſodayne ſhowres great proweſſe theſe conquerours derked eke brightneſſe fame ſhineth yet reporte name vnto v bokes repreſent without fayninge waye went theyr dayes alyue agayne trouth ſo euer ſtriue counterplede make debate ſouth redde high lowe eſtate without fauour ſo lyſt take hede death clerkes litell drede theyr deſerte beare wytnes tyraunt truthe expreſſe ¶as men deſerue without excepcion lak pris graūt guerdon wherfore ſemeth euery maner man shulde lyfe euer vertue ſake eſchewe amys death playnly clerkes willlyn write except none playne trouth man gone olde time theyr writinge trewe cheryſhed lordes yt thē knewe honoured greatly tho dayes enacted gilt theyr ſayes theyr high renowne māhod prowes knighthod eke theyr worthines trihumphes al eke victory famous cōqueſt fonge glory ¶fro point poynt reherſinge ye trouth without fraude neclygence ſlouth theyr labour theyr beſineſſe elles certayne great worthineſſe theyr dedes bene vayne dyrked age elles would haue ſlayne length yeares noble worthy fame conquerours playnly theyr name dimmed eke letter aureat eke deffaced palme laureat yt wan knighthod ī dayes whoſe freting ruſte newe newe aſſayes eclipſe honour glory highe prowes clerkes memory haue truly ſet dilygent laboure enlumined many curious floure rethorike make v comprehende trouth tho kinde byſied faithfully trauailed agayne age wold haue aſſayled theyr bokes euery thinge yſet key remembraunce ſhet laſteth yet dureth euer one recorde thebe ſo longe agone ruyne deſtruction ye may beholde good inſpection croppe roote right dede stace loke ye may rede howe polynece eteocles brethern two ne could liue peace till thebe brought ruyne maner howe diden fyne death alſo worthy tideus howe edipp teares full pyteous wept eyen drery payne ye ſmokes departed twaine feaſt fyres funerall great stace ye may reden al ſyre engendred brotherly hatred ye deathe cruel mede ¶in ſothe many worthy man lyke mine auctour well rehearſe troye alſo latter yeares diligence theſe cronycleres ye may beholde theyr writinge well ſtrife werre ſiege euery dell right ſo many yeares ſin paſſed whoſe ſtorye yet age hath diffaced cruell deathe mortall ſtrokes maugre death ye may beholde bokes ſtorye fully reherſed newe newe freſhe floure coloure hewe day day quicke nothinge feinte clerkes haue ſtorye ſo depeynt death age weye trouth may make deye ¶al ſome haue trouth ſpared wrytynge playnty declared tolde faythfully tranſformed theyr poeſy vayne fable entencion haue contriued falſe tranſſumptiō hide trouth falſly vnder cloude ſothe malyce ſhroude homer writinge feyned hath full many dyuers thynge neuer guydo lyſt deuiſe thinges done farre anotherwiſe hath tranſformed trouth feyned falſly goddes caſe ¶the worthy grekes helpe warrey agayne troyens ſey lyke lyfely men among theym day day dytyes freſhe gay ſugred wordes vnder hoony ſote galie hyd lowe roote may outward aſpyed grekes alyed therfore theym fauorable much thyng whych commendable theym luſt deine ryght making loue hath loſt ſight gyue pry none deſerued cupide blinde whoſe dome ben obſerued luſt equytye reaſon trouth ſyngulertee falſe affeccion reyſeth ful ofte vayne lauſion man worſhyp deſerueth none falſe reporte thus full many one without merite hath fame blowe wherof another renowne vnknowe ī armes hath ſūdry meruailes wrought whō peraunter ſpeaketh mā nought fauour foſtred thē rightes hindred hathe many worthy knightes ¶ouide alſo poete egally hath cloſed falſhed trouthe yt make men enoſed parte ſhall theym holde miſty ſpeche ſo hard vnfolde entriketh reader ſee virgil alſo loue ene eneyd reherſeth much thinge partie trewe writing except onely liſt ſomwhile trace folowe homeris ſtile ¶and ſyege wrote eke lollius tofore daretus frigens wrote moſt truely fonde ditus eke grekes londe preſent ſene euery dell fill write trewe well eche tunge ſuche conſonaunce theyr bokes variaunce vnto athene brought proceſſe ſerched ſought diligence one cornelius neuewe vnto saluſtius rome yborne dewe tranſlate trace ſewe theſe auctours good auiſement bycauſe ſet entent brefe lefte muche behinde ſtory men bokes finde firſte meninge cauſe originall ginninge roote ſpeciall ne come lande nauy firſte ſparke kindled enuy betwixt grekes theim troye towne cornelie maketh menciowne theyr ſhyppes theyr vytayle grece called ytayle laſſe bokes verifye ¶is named nowe lande romanye numbre kinges duke wēt towarde ſyege one aſſente wynne worſhyppe exercyſe armes onely full knyghtly wyſe abydyng ſe verſion cytye noble illyon maner theyr armure ¶nor ſyege longeſt endure wiſe eche dyd aſſayle often met battayle many worthy loſt theyr lyfe olde hatred wrought vp newe ſtryfe theyr death dateth yeare wrytinge ſo partyculere without fruite compēdious foreſayd romayne cornelius ¶wherfore late comparyſowne auctour ful highe renowne beſyed hym trace ſewe dite daret caſt tranſmewe ſtory worde ſentence foloweth theym ſuch conuenyence effect ſubſtaunce ſame columpna guydo name writing paſſing excellence enlumineth crafte cadence noble ſtorye many freſhe coloure rethorik many ryche floure eloquence make ſounde bett ¶he ſtorye ymped hath ſet good fayth trowe hath pere recken write mattere boke ye may beholde ſe ſaye knelyng kne laude honour excellence fame guydo mayſter vnto thy name excelleſt ſouerayngtye ſtyle wryte matter compyle ſhal folow nere euer may god graunte paye hym haue vndertake ſtorye make prayinge ſhal read ſee erre amende humble herte lowe entencion committing theyr correction therof thanke yt wyn theyr ſupport thus wil begin ende prologue fyrſte boke ¶how ye knge theſſalie named pelleus loſt men diuine puniſhemēt praiers obtained others ca ye reigne land theſalye ynamed ſaloni king called pelleus wyſe diſcrete alſo vertuous guido liſt ſpecifie helde lordſhippe regalye yle gouernour kynge whych people recorde writinge mirundones called tho dayes ouide fayneth ſayes metamorphoſeos ye may rede people ſothfaſtly dede mine auctour maketh mencion brought echeone deſtruction ſodayne tempeſt fyry leuen goddes ſent downe heauē yre without offence ſwerde ye ſtroke peſtilence yle whilom toke vengeaunce like put remembraunce people deſtroyed certayne thunder dint hayle rayne full vnwarely guido liſt deſcriue none left liue lande vyolence eſcape might peſtilence except kinge went alone wood make mone sool ſelfe diſconſolate place ſtode deſolate kinge ronnynge fro complayninge aye fatall woo harmes endure till laſt caſe auenture beſide holt ſawe ſtode tree full great hight large quantitye holowe thee roote coulde knowe ſawe earthe lowe ante crepe paſſing greate plente ſight fell downe kne made prayer panim wiſe goddes humble ſacrafiſe vpon wo great aduerſytee onely mercy haue pytee turne theſe ante fourme man thus gan praye coloure pale wan lande tenhabite ſtandeth deſolate alone awhaped mate comfortles creature releue endure ouide maketh mencion god iupiter herde oriſon hath ſuch routhe leſte anone fulfilleth requeſt might diuine grace made heuen ſhine beningly vnto earth adowne ſodayne tranſmutaciowne ante brought fourme mē anon fete vpright gan gon theſaly ſalue kinge like liege toke theyr dwellinge within citye called tho egee ouide ye may beholde ſe people theyr worthineſſe theyr ſtrength great hardineſſe mirundines ſo longe haue bore name life ye reade may thee ſame ſaincte mathewe called ſo apoſtle ſo much wiſdome prudent aduertence beſy labour wilfull diligence forſeing great diſcrecion ſuppoſe mine opinion fable ante contriued wiſdōe haue ſo much acheued knighthod ſo liſt loke manly dedes throughout troye boke al miſchiefe ſo wel haue theim borne full wiſely prouided toforne fil werre peace ſlouthe reckles ¶but ante eſchewe idelneſſe ſomer ſo full beſineſſe winter comme ſaue colde ſhe fore aſtored hath holde ¶but matter holde ſermon ywill longer make diſgreſſion fable nowe ſoiourne lefte agayne retourne pelleus ferther procede ¶which king forſothe ſtory rede mine auctour liſteh endite hadde wife called tethite whyche twayne platly lee manly man hardy achilles guido liſte termine deſcended ſothely lyne moſte renoumed manhode might amonges grekes beſt knyghte yholde ſothe throughout lande worthines preued hande whoſe crueltye troyens ſore abought merueyles wrought durynge ſyege ye ſhall lere pacyently yf ye ſhall liſt heare ¶this pelleus ſpake aforne brother one mother borne hight eſon ſo ferre yronne yeares luſt hath loſt deſyres ferre cropen age wyt turned dotage bothe minde memoriall furdulled wer dercked ſo veryly diſcrecyon berafte concluſion wherfore reigne land theſalye crowne ceptre regalye hath aſſigned brother queme eſtate royall alſo diademe ¶howe eſon kyng olde myghte longer welde gouernayle cauſed crowne brother pelleus ca ii bycauſe croked lame blinde gouerne loſt wit minde feble celle retentife forderked imaginatife loſt bothe memorye reaſon whiche made hathe reſignacion brother nexte heyre degre nyeſt allye affynytye ſome auctors theyr bokes ſayne youth reſtored newe agayne crafte mede great sorcereſſe renewed luſtineſſe herbys pocions ſubtyl workynge confexions queintiſe eke inſtrumentes wyth charmes enchauntmentes made drinke bokes tolde whych yerde drye olde without abode anone ſhe caſt blome budde woulde begin faſt eke grene freſhe beholde drinke ſhe hathe fro yeares olde eſon reſtored vnto luſty age wyt reaſon eke ſage euer hadde life aforne whiche eſon wife yborne ſonne iaſon name worke whō nature blame ſhe crafte platly conninge spent vpon hooly workynge whan ſhe made hert wil thought crafte behind right nought reken ſhape alſo fayrneſſe ſtrength beauty liuelyneſſe gentylnes wiſe gouernaunce large dalyaunce moſt goodly men coulde knowe porte highe lowe auiſe eke tretable conning god wote able diſcriue vertues myne auctour telleth faithfully beloued ſo olde yonge ye lād ſo honour ſprong yt yet yonge ſlendre age alſo inly grene tendre committed gouernaile pelleus withouten fayle euery thinge ſeruiable diligent chambre table euer childe man vnto lorde al euer glad herte faithful obeyſſaunce cheare yet countenaunce inwarde hearte outward ſhewing vncle againſt grutching hooly hande worthy kingdome riche lande iaſon heritage onely tho yonge age ¶vnto pelleus payne againſt herte falſly fayne ſhewe mente herte kept cloſe yt nothing outſterte like addre vnder floures fayre herte tunge al contrayre benigne ſpeche mening like ſerpent vnder coloure treaſon blente ſhewe goodly vnto allye inward brent hate enuy hoote fyre yet ſmeke couertly malyce yreke man might ſigne eſpie towarde iaſon herte bare enuye meruayle none cauſeles saue dradde encres manhode likely tatteine ſuccede father reigne whiche pelleus vniuſtly occupieth daye day caſt fantiſyeth venim may ſome purſute vpon iaſon fully execute muſeth euery houre time dradde ſe haſty prime folowe chaunge wonte done sodenly chaunge newe mone caſteth wayes compaſſeth ſore vnder coloure alway fell malice gan cloſe hide like ſnake wonted glide venim vnder freſhe floures ſonne right hote ſhoures enuy hotter brent glede till time thought would procede execute meaninge euery dell port lambe herte lion fell double tygre ſlyghtly compace galle breſte ſuger face man hath ſuſpection purueyeth deſtruction neuewe within pretending loue fine gile malice yſhet ſo vnder keye entent man bewreye conceled cloſed ſecre vnder cloke priuye enmitye ſo greued vpon ſelfe angre frette ſo ſore abidynge aye tyll vnto entent finde may leyſur conuenient vpon purpoſe platly procede perfourme fully vp dede wherof iaſon hath full lytell rought vncle ne one thought whoſe meaninge conuenience ſo malice linked innocence grounde ſo deuiſe falſe enuye hatefull couetiſe whiche frette ſo ſore falſly winne croppe roote euery ſorowe ſinne cauſe hath bene ſith go full yore many realme hath bought ful ſore dreadful venim couetiſe ala let beware ſtande caſe ¶to thinke afore haue minde falſhed draweth ende though bide laſt yeare two ende ſothe ſhall ſorowe woo bene falſe enuious hereof forth pelleus tell hath ſo longe ſought vpō thing till brought tydinges newe ſo merueylous aſtoned houſe meruayle tho newly falle beſide troy plage orientalle howe colchos tidinges cam within yle encloſed ram whiche bare fleſe full richly golde richeſſe kept holde great aduice great dilygence man might offence ile gouernour noble kinge worthy warrour oetes hight wiſe diſcrete ſage alſo yronne farre age time bokes deuiſe vnderfonged many great empryſe peace warre much worſhip wonne alſo ſonne vnto ſonne gaue vre honour atteyne theſe poetes liſten feyne touchinge line leue nowe ye greate ram purpoſe treate commit dare well aſſure keping buſy cure cruell mar mighty god werre ſtremys rede ſterre influence deytee ordeyned hath full great crueltee ram kepe bullis full vnmilde braſen fete ramageous wilde fell diſpitous nature wood furious hurte ſlee euer one deſyre whoſe mouthe leuen wylde fyre lyke flawme euer blaſed brenne theim ſtode nygh aobut eke eyen lokes moſte horrible fourneys ſtremes viſyble wolde tencreaſe glorye ram golde wynnen victorie fyrſte muſt force myght vnto oultraunce theſe bulles fyght theim vanquiſhe alder fyrſt make theim humble oxe ſtall ſithe theim yoke ere ye land manhode muſt take hand muſt alſo endure ſerpent huge great ſtature without fauour playnely haue oultraunce eke without wordes mo whiche ſerpent ſhortly tell lyke fende comyng hell ¶full venym cruell hate ſkales harde plate armed ſtande defence brethe werſe peſtilence infecten wolde enuiron eyre eche place repeyre ſo full foule corruption eke ſo dredefull infection deth ſoth ſhortly deuyſe fyne hygh empryſe ſuche wolde quarell take hond ylyke one free bonde coulde bet ſelfe defende conqueſt eke ende myghty ſerpēt ſlawe muſt anone cuſtome lawe ¶out head tethe echeone arrace ſowe theim ſelfe place ox eryd aforne ſeede ſprange wōder corne knyghtes armed paſſynge great myght eueryche redy fyght til eche brother ybrought groūd mortall fate yeue dethes wound ende euerychone ſowfaſtly non liue myght fatall lawe longer tyme lyued fellowe ¶and way dredfull peryllous ſo deſyreth ben victorious paſſe muſt manly endure ſo fall take auenture eſtate excepcion cheſe ſo wyll concluſyon may ſcape fauour ne mede ſo begynneth vyſe wel rede ſtatute kyng may ſo wyll entre aſſaye one hath begonne may cheſe tyll haue loſt wonne yet ſome ram expreſſe fleſe alſo bere wytneſſe nothyng golde great treaſour oetes kynge full hye laboure made kepe incantacions ſorſerye falſe illuſyons ¶that ſpoke realmes fer whiche many put theyr lyfe doubte hye deſyre wyn great treaſoure ſhyt within colchos londe ye haue harde deuyſe whoſe purſuyte roſe couetyſe grounde roote wo myſchaunce vayne reporte theim ſelfe auaunce whiche put theim ſelfe ieopardy without reſcues lykely dye helpe ne ſleyght armes vaile might againe ye curſed charmes ſtronge ſuperſticious many worthy knighthode famous enhaſted vnto deth ala ieoparde liſt liues caſe ¶this laſteth forthe tyll afterwarde byfell pelleus platly hath hard tell great miſchiefes deſtructions colchos wrought ſundry nacions haue purſued thes auntres cōquere tyll pelleus ſo ferforth gan enquere knewe hooly trouth herte anone gan compaſſe myght ſlyght make neuewe iaſon vndertake hye empryſe colchos wende way myght hym beſt ſhende ¶and gan pretende colour freſhe hew ygylte outwarde ſo luſty ſo newe though treaſō hyd within ſawe alſo tyme begyn purpoſe tho fyrſt made queint gan forthwith golde aſure paint gaye wordes ſownyng glorious knowynge iaſon yonge deſyrous vnto ſuche thynge lyghtly wolde enclyne therfore thought wolde fyne playnely worke concluſyon made anone conuocation lordes baronye aboute enuyron lande theſalye aſſemble eſtates eche degree realme within chiefe citee holde counſeyle vtterly caſte therby acheue deſyre faſte ſo courte continued dayes three tyll laſte hyd iniquitie gan rake hath hyd ſo longe ne myght longer forth prolonge venym hyd fret ſo herte ſo ſlye wyſe man myght auerte vpon ſyde mente well treaſon couered euerydell curtined ſo vnder trechery thynge ſo ſlyghtly gan gye pryme face man myght deme worde wolde ſeme chere porte ſygne dalyaunce caſte knyghtly auaunce yonge neuewe lykelyneſſe hye honour manhode proweſſe thentent whiche gan purpoſe man cowde ſpye theffect dyd ſo gloſe texte ſo conueyed flatery people cowde eſpye lyttell nought entent within whiche anone preyſe begyn ſuche honour neuewe wolde ſuche chere began vnfolde tofore theim entencion hath voyded ſuſpection aſſembled place towarde iaſon tourne gan face full louyngly countenaunce chere hym ſayde myght throughout ye court whē maked ſilēce thus worde worde platly ſentence ¶howe pelleus fearynge depoſed brother ſon iaſon worthye valiaūt yonge knight coūſayled vndertake ye perellous almoſt inuincible conqueſt golden fleſe colchos perſwacion vndertoke ſame cap iii coſyn iaſon take hede ſhal ſain ſo inly glad fayne ſo ſurpriſed mirth hert enchaſeth voideth ſmerte conſyder myne inſpection thy youthe diſpoſicion whiche ſhortely comprehende saue vertue nothyng entende vnto worſhyp gentylneſſe manly fredom hye largeſſe veryly whether wake wynke ioye onely thyncke ſelfe holde ſo paſſinge fortunate lande hye lowe eſtate lykely honour flete lyue reſte perfecte quiete thy ſupporte worthy gouernaile whoſe manhode may ſo muche v auayle likelyhod eke ſo moche amende ſoth ſaue v defende agayne al tho deſcryue mali wolde againſt v ſtryue rebell maner waye ſurquedrye pryde werraye worthineſſe aſſured tranquyll aſſaute wolde v ylle perturbe noble ſtate royall agaynſt whome thou arte wall myghty ſhyelde protection thus deme fully myne opynion ¶for thyne age thy wyt thy prouidence thy knyghtly herte thy manly excellence reported ben thyne hye renowne many londe many regyowne rounde worlde aboute circuite howe myght ſtonde better plyte thyne honour lyke founde worſhyp ſo hyghly doth rebounde wolde playnly ſeke nothyng ceaſe coulde helpe thyne honour encreaſe hygh renowne ywys euery houre therupon ſpenden treaſoure hye deſyre withouten fayle entier loue dothe ſo ſore aſſayle nyght daye maye haue reſte ſhall tourne hope beſte tenhaunce thyne honour heauen aboue poole ſterres ſeuen whiche thinge haue awaye eſpyed wyt therto haue applyed meane ſhuld longer dwel dere coſyn ſhall tell ſo manhode ſouerayne thy knyghthode thou durſt attayne fleſe gold conquere thy ſtrength whiche ſpoke ſo fer bredth length home returne body ſaufe ſounde ſo conqueſt myght founde thou acheue durſt hyghe empriſe hertes ioye coulde deuyſe worlde ſothly beſte realme fully reſt thy manhode men wolde v drede wherfore coſyn knyghthode manhede take vpon praier requeſt ¶and trouth take beheſte euer nedeth meyne coſtage wyll ſelfe towarde viage ordaine ynoughe harneyſe araye nought ſhal faile yt may thy paye furthermore playnly enſure ſee thou thy beſy cure hyghe empryſe bryng aboute thou ſhalt feare nother ben doubt daye ſucceſſyon kyng region hooly haue ſceptre regaly wherfore iaſon lyfte vp thyne hertes eye thynke thy name ſhalbe longe recorded throughout ye world wherfore accorded within thy ſelfe plainly ne ſpare thyne entent ſentence declare vvhan iaſon vncle vnderſtāde muche reioyſeth take hand dredfull labour without auiſement nought aduertith menyng fraudulēt priue poyſon vnder ſuger cured howe galle hony lured dercke deceyte cloudy falſe engyne ygylt without vnder venyme wherto iaſon hath none aduertence kynge wende cleane conſcience withouten fraude thyng yment wherfore anon yeueth full aſſent wordes fewe plainely gan ſeye vncles wolde obeye accorded concluſion humble herte hoole entenſyon wherof kynge receyueth ſuche gladneſſe vnneth myght ſame expreſſe ryght faſte dyd beſy paine iourney haſt nedes ordaine aſmoche colchos countrey encloſed inuyron ſea man longe ſtryue without ſhyp thyder may arryue preſence anone dyd call famous argus coulde moſt make ſhyp fyrſt art yfonde ſayle ſea fro londe londe hath wrought ſhyp ſotyl crafte whiche fyrſt euer wawe rafte haue entre argon bare name gramariens yet recorde ſame ſhyp fyrſt meruayle called ſo whiche proudely bare ſayle guydos boke doth v ſpecifye happed forthe nauye ¶whan ready meyne vytayle byde nought wynde ſayle many worthye companye noble byrthe great allye vyage ready gon bothe loue worſhyp iaſon amonge whiche great hercules force myght ſtrength pereles begetten vpon alcmene inly fayre womanly ſene iubiter full longe agone takyng lykelyneſſe amphitrion downe fro heuen deyte rauiſſhed luſt beaute loued herte hole entent two ſothly diſcent came hercules worthy famous knyght moſt renoumed manhode myghte whiche tyme ſo meruaylous excellent ſo victorious ouyde liſte recorden hym ſelue methamorphoſis dedes twelue whiche ben remembred inſpeciall honour memoryall ¶and theim reherſe ordre ye lyſt purpoſe vtterly ſlough antheon eyer hyght many gyaunt myght hath outrayed lymes rude ſerpent hydra ſlough eke pallude serberus hounde bonde ſo ſore hell gate brake made voide venym ye ſtrife vpwarde gaue hym ſuche laxatyfe worlde brethe contagyous infected hath ſo venymous blaſt althinges wold die toke harpyes byrdes archady ſlough centaurus beſtꝭ mōſtruous fyerſe lyon berafte houſe ſayne whan ſlawe ſkynne hath ſtript flawe cruell herte throughe hye renowne golden applys berafte dragone fyrye catte ſlough withouten archadye likewyſe cruell bore laſt ſhuldres ſquare veray myght fyrmament bare ne may reaken paſſynge dedes whiche ben hiſtoryall redeth ouide ye ſhall theim fynd trihumphes maketh mīde thoughout ye world honour fet pyllers gades ſet alexſaundre macedone ye kyng ſo worthy lyuynge rood conqueſt guydo liſt write hooſt proudely viſyte beyonde whiche londe habitable ſea ſayle ſothly conuenable ferre beyonde occian ſhypmen thenſe ſkill sibilles ſtreightes maryners call theſe boundes named hercules hym ſelfe theim ſet markes lette ferther paſſe guydo maketh mynde yet place called fynde saracenica fyne laboure longa saphy recorde mine auctour ¶of matter ſhuld ſayne vnto iaſon wyll retourne agayne haſte doth ready make vncle whan hath leue take towarde ſea hercules yfeare men anone ye ſhall tyme yere whan ſhene ſonne ſphere ſo farre vp ronne fully paſſed gemyny hath chare whyrled vp ſo hye throughe draught pirrous reed made crabbes head manſion ſea royall halowed ſtondyng eſtiuall freſhe appollo golden wayne herde men herte ſo fayne hete ſhroude ſhade vnder theiſe braūches theiſe bowes glade whan phebus beames ſo bryght ſhine deſcended ben right line cauſe eyer reflection full hoote luſty freſhe ſeaſon whan cornes gyn fielde ſede graſſes grene mede fro yere yere ben cuſtome mowe playne caſte leyde full lowe tyll moyſture conſumed awaye holte hethe merye ſomers daye whiche time yonge knyght iaſon hercules forth ſhyp gon theim eke reherſe grekes alſo many luſty man shypped echon royall apparayle whan croſſed vnder ſayle within ſhyp whiche argus made ſo ſtaūche might water lade gan ſayle wynde wyll ſhyp gan breake ſturdy wawes yll vpon ſea ſo daye nyght colchos warde held waye right gydyng courſe lode ſterre ere ſayle coſtes nigh ferre philoctetes alder guide coulde afore ſo prudently prouyde great inſyght caſte afore ſee tempeſt winde lande ſea whan ſhuld trouble ſtormes fall mayſter plainly ſhipman craft choſe gouernour coude warne afore euery ſhour ſhuld fall whan ſterres dyd appere ſpecyally guydo doth v lere philoctetes whiche tho fole moſte ſyght erecte vnto pole aduertence cleare inſpection ſterres conſtellacion whiche artre rounde aboute gone clerkes call ſeptemtrion pole ycalled articus euer one appereth vnto v ryght ſo ſothe loke aryght antarticus ſhrouded ſyght ſhypmen diſcrete wyſe lyſte courſe prudently deuyſe vpon ſea haue ſuffyſaunce ynoughe gye theyr paſſage arthourys ploughe playne direction vnto coſtes euery region helpe nedle ſtone may erre coſtes yt gone maryners diſcrete ſage lyke expert lodmanage ſtraunge coſtes ſayle ferre gynne courſe ſterre ¶whiche arthur compaſſeth enuiron whiche cercle conſtellacion ycalled cercle artophilax knoweth nedeth axe ſhypmen ſterry nyght ſuffyſaunt whan ſee lyght ¶and poetes theſe pooles twayne bokes lyken fayne ditees manifeſt v calixto yonge archadius owne ſonne yſtellyfyed heauen defyed iuno enuye iupiter whan ſhe eſpye ¶for whiche ſhe bere tourned gilte ſhe hath erth mourned till heauen naſon tell tranſlate eternally dwell amonge ſterres ſhe ſtalled vrſa maior clerkes called ſonne worthy fame ¶of vrſa minor beareth yet name▪ ſuche courſe might aſterte philectetes moſte experte ſhypmen euer herde tell▪ cunnynge might beare bell ¶and whan grekes longe fordryue caſte ſaylynge ſea forweried trauayle caſte aryue wolde auayle theim refreſhe diſporte ioye vpon boundes londe troye ¶howe iaſon expedicion towardes colchos caſually felowſhyp arryued territoryes troye meanynge onely whyle refreſhe reſte theim cap iiii vuhan hercules iaſon honde ſhip taken haue londe wt theim eke knightes euerichone fro ſea londe gone sore forweried trauaile ſothe come aryuaile symeonte hauen great renowne litle diſtant fro troy towne glad ſykerneſſe ſtorme tempeſt werineſſe ne mente treaſon harme gyle ſtronde reſten theim awhyle wight hurt maner age yle damage man beaſt euer go abyde daye two theim refreſhe efte repaire wyght offenſyon moleſte greuen wyght vnſtable rule fortune might hath euer enuye men liue eaſe whoſe haſtie courſe vnwarely doth diſeaſe ſhe cauſe god wote cauſeles gery fortune lady recheles blinde goddeſſe tranſmutacion tourne whele reuolucion make troyens vniuſtly wene grekes ariued theim tene cauſe ſuſpicion hath many brought vnto deſtruction full many worthy kinges prince throughout ye world reckened prouinces ſlaundre vnto miſchief brought thinge ala neuer thought cauſe chiefe occaſiowne citye royall towne deſtroyed playnly founde whoſe walles hie betē downe groūd many man many worthye knight ſlayue many lady bright wedowe made dureſſe werre kouthe ſith reported ferre many mayde grene tender age lefte ſole withouten mariage behinde theyr father ala fall ſhulde nought elles yt fortune would shewen might crueltye vengeaunce taking vpon citye ¶alas euer ſo worthy eſtate shuld ſo lytell fallen debate whan gon like ſtaunche graffing litell braunche full ſturdy tree growen vp full ofte clymbeth hye may fall ſofte ſparkes ſight ſmall fyre engendred deuoureth gnat firſt litell hate encauſeth flawme contek debate enuiouſlye ſprede abrode full ferre thus ala realmes mortall werre firſt begonne men may reade ſe ſparke litell enmitye ſtaunched fyrſt whē begōne fire ſo ferre yronne embraſeth hertes ſuch hatrede make brenne hote glede partye cruell tene ther ſtaunche ſherp ſwerdes kene ala conſumeth ſlethe thus fine enmite death though ginning caſuell biding frete paſſingly cruell voyde realmes reſte peace ioye fill whilom worthy troye doth wepe caſe ſodayne euery wight ought complayne litell gilt ſhuld haue ſuche vengeaūce except percaſe goddes purueaunce miſchiefe ſhuld perhappes enſuing cauſe great felycitye troye brought thus vnto deſtruction ginninge occacion mine auctour ſpecified worthy rome edified ſpringe worthy eneas whilom troy whan exiled whiche rome reade ye may ſe worlde head chiefe citye famous paſſing worthineſſe eke whē troy brought thus diſtreſſe ye walles caſt broke adowne cauſe many regiowne begonne many great citye troyan manly man enee ſundrye ſeas gan ſo longe ſayle till fortune came itayle wan lande bokes tellen v eke ſonne aſcanius enee doth line ſuccede land itale iuſtly poſſede ſonne siluius came brute ſo paſſingly famous ſo ſhall fayne whilom land called britayne geauntes māhode wā noble yle firſt began ¶from troye alſo ilke enee came worthy francus lorde hye degre rome tēcreaſe high renowne builded time full royall towne ſothely honour auaunce name made call fraunce thus began vnderſtande name firſt worthy lande anthenor departing troyens began cytie veneciens sycanus within litell began tenhabite land cecile parting sycanus worthy brother called syculus finde reygned yle called cecile eneas forth tuſcy gone tenhabite people right anone cicile naples firſt began full many neopolitane longeth daye ful riche great might ¶and diomede noble worthy knight whan troye fall toures faire howe reygne caſt repayre liege tho began quarell fayne withſtode wt al might maine malyce conſpiraciowne wtheld ſceptre crowne deutye theyr olde aligeaunce denied trouth obeyſſaūce wherfore anone ſo bokes tell folkes went dwell calabre gan poſſede knightes diomede fro troye haue thither ſewed fourme byrdes wer anone trāſmewed circe crafte doughter sonne eyer flee anone gonne called bene ſodore reade amonge grekes byrdes diomede ſome bokes theim liſt beare witnes chaūge made venꝰ ye goddeſſe wrathe yt ſhe worthy knight onely ſhe ſawe one fighte eneas ownely ſonne deare time faughte yfeare diomede darte ygrounde gan ame deadly mortall wounde ¶his mother venꝰ gan anone ſhroud vnder ſkye miſty cloude ſaue tho time fro miſchaunce ſkill venus toke vengeaunce byrdes tourne meyne fourme yere yere fle vnto tombe graue yt yet minde haue cuſtome remembraunce rite holde obſeruaunce exequies theſe byrdes euery chone dayes ſpace thence ne gone moreouer dewe loue grekes platly eſchewe latin ought may betyde preſent anone flee aſide eche bokes v aſſure theſe byrdes knowe onely nature grekes latines kindely aſſonder whan theym ſe yt ſuch wōder vnto wit eſpye cauſes hidde ſuch ſorcerye well wote though wit blent roote falſe enchauntement fayth ought defye apparences ſhewed eye fende illuſion therof thus whan troye towne euerſed brought nought full many citie ybylde wrought ¶and many lande many ryche towne edifyed occaſiowne werre ye haue herde telle whiche declare may dwelle poynt poynt like bokes ſayne iaſon wyll reſorte agayne landed worthy hercules symeonte hauen ches haue tolde reſte comforte elles onely deſporte kyng reygnyng troye towne tyme called lamedowne falſe enuye reported tolde certayne grekes herte bolde londe entre knewe well arayed veſſell newe aryue lycence theym purpoſe done offence likelyhed lande greue pride without loue ſafe conduite haue ſtronde ytake ſuch maſteries land make theyr power maner thinge without regarde playnly thy kinge ¶of eſtate taking tho none hede ſuch ſtraungers great drede men laches neclygence fully wete theyr pretence forth prolonge perill caſte ſodeyne thinge wolde wiſt faſt differred till harme wiſedome ſo men may longe ſuffer abide necligence let ſlide enquere theyr gouernaunce ſpeche dalyaunce eueriche reuelaciowne euery ſtrete throughout troye towne rowning ſome ſpake abrode ſpeche ſo longe abode one ſothely ſowne reported kinge laomedowne ye haue herd wilfullneſſe without counſayle auiſeneſſe haſtely maked hath ſonde wit hardy londe beſide leue preſumption wherfore bad concluſion without abode ſoone remewe finally ſhuld eſchewe compelled maugre ſayeth nay ſo king vpon certayne day haſte hath ſente imbaſſadore vnto iaſon grekes gouernoure nother thought harme villanye innocent companye diſported endlonge ſtronde euer hath ſith came londe charge layd worde worde iaſon ſayde effect euery cyrcumſtaunce ſomme playnly ſubſtaunce ¶how lamedon king troye ſent iaſon commaundyng felowſhippe forthwith depart confines countreith aunſwere ſente ayen kinge ca v wiſe worthy famous renowne mighty king ye noble lamedowne hath vnto meſſage thus yſent theffect ſentement ſothe hath meruayle lande ariuayle bringing grekes fewe haue conduite ſhewe protection playnly licence preiudice magnificence wherfore hath charge layde platly ſayde ye anone without delay without noyſe affraye troye land bondes ye leue caſteth greue better eaſe departe folye liues ieoparte wiſe lacke prouidence againſt make reſiſtence pride wilfulneſſe bolde without auiſeneſſe interrupt high felicitye deſireth tranquilitie holde reigne withouten perturbaūce▪ whoſe parſon made ſuch alyaunce atwene manhode royall mageſtye ſuffer none degre diſquiet maner wiſe wherfore counſayle ye ſemen wiſe take good hede vnto ſeye bidding diſobey ¶leſt ye offende knightly excellence ye ſhall finde experience without feyninge ſothe telle take hede therfore may longer dwelle point point ſith ye wiſe ſage hoole effect meſſage vvhan iaſon herd meſſegere theſe wordes al gā chaūgē chere kept cloſe ſobre countenaūce ireful haſtye greuaunce ne rancoure caughte tale saue face gan waxen pale longe abiding ought would ſayne ſpake worde agayne vnto fro kinge ſent gan diſcloſe ſomme entent vnto folkes ſtanding rounde aboute vnto tho diſcured oute meſſage hole firſt abreyde worde worde thus theim ſayd ¶syrs ſayeth well knowe take hede pray hye lowe lamedone king troye hath ſent v wonderful lenuoye chargyng haſt hye land axeth howe thus vpon ſtronde ariue hadden hardineſſe withouten leue ſe gentilneſſe fredome alite howe like kinge ſelfe aquite vnto ſtraungers entre yle nought god wote litell refreſhe departe anon like ye recorden euerychon hereof bearen witneſſe al ſome ala fredome nowe become ¶where manhode gentilneſſe alſo kinge togither two shulde cuſtome haue theyr reſting place honour yt ſhuld alſo embraſe lordes herte kyngely right manly fredome full might shuld ſtraūgers halfe refreſhe recomfort afterwarde might reporte ¶larges experte manhode gentilleſſe haue founde worthineſſe nobleſſe aught allye fredome eke knit regallye longeth honour kinge ſhulde haue charged firſt thinge worthy liege al might pleaſe haue ſhewed theyr comforte theyr eaſe theyr might theyr buſy cure vnto ſtraungers auenture ſea fordryuen diſmayed comming euill appayed yf caſe ſemblable oether fortune variable ſort hap may withſtande aryued grekes land honeſtly like degre ſhuld v haue receyued lyke longeth vnto gentrye ſith ought eſpye hath fredom honour humanytye one made courte flie choſe diſhonour let worſhip gone ſhall euerichone hath choſe helpe fulfiil power ſhall like ſaye ſothe ſhall founde dede ſhall ſelfe rebounde sith malyce hath worke begonne perauenture ſomer ſonne zodiak hath thriſe gone let truſt nothing doubte ſhall ſerue wt ſuch hath ſought lyue ſhall dere abought albe therof ſet nowe tide lande longer abyde till haue leyſur better ſoiourne worde begā anone fourne manly face ſterne cheare ſodeynly vnto meſſagere fro kinge ſo vnto ſent wiſe ſheweth entent ¶my frende quod haue wel vnderſtād meſſage hoole yu haſt toke hand thy kinge bringen vnto v right nowe vnwarely ſith ſtandeth thus nowe haue meaninge euery dele poynt poynt vnderſtande wel worde worde playnly conceyued giftes haue receyued behalfe great nede remembre take good hede euery thing thou haſt v brought truſte well forget nought ſhall imprinte ſurely minde withall goodly finde great bountie maner thinge within land lamedone kinge welcominge great cheare goodly ſonde thou bringeſt accordinge entent god well wote neuer ment harme vnto playnly domage none maner age vpon goddes inmortall theyr kinde ben celeſtiall vnto recorde mine herte take touching borowes thē make witneſſing ment none offence ne haue taken violence within realme woman childe man ſo thou mayeſt reporte thou fordriuen ſea compelled neceſſyte ariue thou haſt herd ſayne onely reſte v vpon playne without vnto certayne daye afterwarde hold furth way vpon iourney make tarying like thou mayſte recorde vnto thy kinge ſaye eke ſhall time ſe perauenter ſhal mowe thanked whan time commeth v ſome go furth thy way ſay thus brother ¶and anone iaſon peace manly knight worthy hercules whē herd thinge fro point poīt anone brought ſuch diſioynt haſty rancoure ſodeyne ire whiche herte almoſt ſet fyre ſodeynly abreyde abacke hie diſdeyne euen thus ſpake chere aſkoyne vnto meſſengere ſayd felowe nothing feare abydinge well certayne titan bemes reyſe agayne ſhall departe hence ſhyppe gone men ſhall lefte one within lande god forne morowe vpō haue faith borowe longer ſhall holde ſoiourne elles ſhall make retourne morowe early daye dawninge payne reprefe ſo go ſaye thy kinge thre yeare yf god v graunt life maugre grutcheth maketh ſtrife vnto lande ſhall agayne retourne caſt anker ſoiourne take hede therof note well time newe chaunge ſhall folowe prime thē power ſhall ſo large ſtretche ſafe conduit litell ſhall reche ſay platly entent haue vnto maundement ſmall regarde day abyde taking leue ſhalbe ſet aſide bycauſe hath begonnen playe ſhal quite god may tourne ſhall owne ſhame ſpare ſay thy kinge ſame ¶this meſſeger gan agayne replye ſayd ſyr ye may denye honeſte meſſage declare auiſe well ſpare kinges ſonde playnly tell ſo beye liſte go dwell ye may yet cheſe ſo lefe lothe ye haue cauſe wrothe ſit vnto worthineſſe ye take hede waye gentelleſſe manaſſing ſuche arowes ſhete bett thretninge lete kepe ſecret till ye large certaynly parcell charge ſtriue make debate better betimes late ye beware harmes mighte fall parte ſay vnto pytie ye deſtroyed man ſhulde hinder dere worthy perſons maner wiſe likly ben diſcrete wiſe leſt wt wordes nowe greue ſaye take leue nighte ypaſſed ſpringing ye day larke bleſſed laye began ſalue luſty rowes rede phebus chare yt ther freſhly ſprede vpon bordure oriente aurora herte hole entent ſwetenes ſiluer ſhoures bedewed freſhe ſomer floures made roſe wt newe bawme flete ſoote lylye margarete encloſe theyr tender leues white oppreſſed hertes gladnes delite drery afore nightes tene hony ſuckels among buſhes grene enbawmed enuyron eyre longe titan gan make repayre brightnes beames merye reioyſe hemiſperie longe aforne ariſe worthy iaſon full haſty wiſe felowe hercules alſo ycharged haue theyr ſhypmen haue ado hale vp anker theym ready make bad haſte euery man take right way vnto ſhyppe anone ſothnes manly man iaſon thought ſtuffed meyne gin werre troye citye ſhortly conclude egall nombre multitude time werre beginne likely ſhuld wynne victorye tho fewe ſitteth nought man hewe aboue head ouer hye leſte chippes fall eye wherfore troye leue coſtes bliue drewe vp ſayle ſhip began driue winde good goddes fauorable fortune theyr frende though ſhe variable thus colchos ſafe ben ycome vnto lande ſafe ſome ben ariued litell ſpace ſea founde haue ſuch grace neptunus cauſed blyue ſayd erſt colchos aryue yle lytell lande colchos hight ye ſhal vnderſtāde howe royall cheife cyty al reygne moſt dignitye worthineſſe ryches fame iacomtes tho bare name chefeſt ſpeake buylding ſtretes large curyous houſinge therwith dyched well without stronge walled toured rounde huge height aloft battayled ye ryght ſtrongly leſte aſſailed many paleys ſtately royall tho ſeat moſt principall kinge abide better elles time happed called oetes reade full renōmed knighthod manhead well beſene meane like ſitting vnto degre euery landes enuirowne fame ſpredde hye renowne al mighty chiefe citye oetes helde royall ſea riuers freſhe ye water cleane lyke criſtall ſhone agayne ſonne ſhene fayre playnes guydo beareth wytneſſe holſome hilles full luſtineſſe many lake many luſty welle eke mine auctour cā tell full many parke full fayre freſhe ſene many wode many medowe grene ſundry floures among ye herbes meynt theyr ſtalke nature hath depeynt ſundry hewes within eke withoute ſeaſon ſomer came aboute fiſhing fouling hauking eke alſo venery hunting two place right inly delytable corne grayne paſſingly greable plenteous maner thynge men harde birdes freſhely ſyng tyme yere hermonye noyſe ſoote melodye freſhe braunches full delycious reioyſe wolde theſe folkes amerous loues bronde fyred herte efte adawen paynes ſmerte certeynly whan grene vere ypaſſed aye fro yere yere may come month gladnes freſhe flora floures empereſſe cladde ſoyle newe deuyſe noble place lyke paradyſe cere goddeſſe largeſſe foyſon suche plentye gaue vnto regyon fleſhe fyſhe wyne vitaile corne lycour full horne vpon londe ſo gan raine ſnowe aſtates yea high lowe lad life ſoueraiane ſuffyſaunce al nature coulde might auaūce litle yle giftes great lyke toforne ye haue harde treate ther plētie ther habundaūce al might pleaſaunce harte commoditee ſo befell citie iaſon come hercules foloweth al pres full well arayed royally ſayne armes encloſed togyther twayne twain people choſe ye none therwith brawnes bone eueriche theim makyng facion full well complete preportion yonge age good ſtature sadde countenaunce full demure euery wight great pleaſaunce ſe maner gouernaunce yonge ſo freſhe hardy meke alſo one paleys go ſuche chere eueriche hath diſport ſee maner noble porte gentylmanly demeaned people preſe gan euery ſee theſe ſtraungers lyke grekes gyſe demeane ſelfe ſo thryfty wyſe deſire people ne wolde ceſſe aboute gather impreſſe enquere myght newe ſuche royalte ben ſodeynly entred towne thus eueriche wold felowe rowne ſo rude ſtare gaſe gape loke maſe towniſh folke done ſo comonly euery thynge falleth ſodeinly oetes lyke worthy kyng whan harde fyrſt comyng receyueth hooly manere ye lyſt anone ye ſhall vvhan yt king hath ſothly vnderſtāde grekes come lande iaſon alſo borne diſſente blud royall theſalye lykely heyre grace haue againe repeire auentures achyued colchos kynge anone ſea aroſe gentilleſſe haſte may goodly wyſe mete theim waye receiueth cheare benigne vnto anone doth aſſygne offycers tawayte night daye chargynge euery maner waye ſoeuer may eaſe thyng may queme pleſe haue foyſon plente eueryche lyke degree thus commaunded al maner thyng anone noble worthy kyng fredome myrrour many halle many riche toure many tourne many dyuers waye many gree made marbyll graye hath conueyed full eaſy paſe tyll thē brought chambre helde daliaunce anone euery circumſtaunce manly fredome made vnto chere chambre engloſed bright cleare ſhone ful ſhene gold aſure many ymage picture hath commaunded offycers honour thē ſtraungers spyces wyne anon yonge freſhe luſty man iaſon faſt gan lycence kyng declare cauſe comyng fyrſt kyng great royalte aſſended royall ſea clothes golde ranged enuyron cuſtome regyon beholde noble ſyght stondyng aboute many worthy knight many ſquyre many gentylman full well beſene kyng right vnto iaſon ſtondyng preſence commaunded hath magnifycence hercules ſytte downe beſyde iaſon longer lyſte abyde commyng cauſe ſhewe effect wordes fewe saue iaſon fyrſt ere tale began full well auiſed chered lyke man conceyued hath noted wonder well poynt poynt mater euerydell forgot worde ſpeche euen lyke rethoryke doth teache gan tale ſo crafte conueye make ye kyng wold ſeye condeſcende rather enclyne aſſente myght fyne comyng knightly hye empryſe thus word worde ſhall deuyſe right worthy prince preſēt place ſupporte hye grace goodnes moſt excellēt dign pacience fauour benygne diſpleaſe may ſaye ſhewe efte declare wordes fewe fynal grounde cauſe coming ye lyſte whiche ben ſo noble kyng goodly wiſe without offence curteſye gyue aundience requeſt ye diſdayne goodly graunte may atteyne yle may auayle fleſe golde frely aſſayle goddes myne auenture lyſte ordeyne fatall eure lyeth playnly fortune gouerne thynges comune werre peace conqueſt victorye armes renowne glory diſcomfyture bryngyng outraunce lyeth hyndre tauaunce ayen whoſe might mortal mā may cheſe ſo wynne leſe lyfe deth fyne labour ye lyſte fauour gyue leue delaye accorded fully aſſaye lyke ſtatute maketh mencion lyſte make none acception vpon ſyde fauour fynde rytes playnly maken mynde euer fall ſhall vnder fonge lowly beſechynge ye prolonge purpoſe make delaye grace ſette daye myne enterpryſe maye achyeue myne abode ſtant vpon leue saithe one word grauntyng ye leſt haue fyne requeſte ¶and whan kyng herde ceriouſly thentent iaſon ſayd ſo manfully ſtynt alyte kepte hym cloſe whyle tyll laſt goodly gan ſmyle towardes iaſon ſaid vnto hym thus iaſon quod albe thou deſyrous vnderfonge paſſyng hye empryſe counſayle lyke ſhall deuyſe full prudently caſte aforne mortall peryll thou lorne thynge lawe yſette chauntement may ylette remedyed fauour mede deth ſoth ſo taketh hede guerdon platly twynne caſte fleſe golde wyn helpe none manhode fortune ſtreyght waye ſo importune dredefull eke ſo full rage ſaue deth lyeth paſſage victorye palme conquere ſothly iaſon ſhall lere founded olde meruaylous workyng ſtatutes mortall thinge ſore bounde vnder regalye rygour may modifye wherfore iaſon thou thinge attame leſte afterwarde laide ye blame thy leſynge thy deſtruction faythfull herte true entencion warne ſelfe quyte man iuſtely ſhall wyte though thou youth thy wylfulneſſe thy lyfe deſtroye without auyſyneſſe sith iaſon peryllous caſe poynt point haue tolde al ye caſe auiſed put faulte ſurplus frely lyeth thinge ſyth thou mayſt cheſe ſo thou wynne leſſe man iuſtly may arecte lawe mar hym ſelfe ſette mortall man right may duelye paſſe hie lowe getteth none grace goddes lyſte hym ordeyne euer caſte hym darrayne diuers thyng moſt furious drede wherfore iaſon euer thou ſpede haue openly declared hooly peryle fauour ſpared fer ſoth reaſon wyll ryght thou woteſt wel lyeth might declare man lette manhode knightly caſte ſette vpon thing thou haſt herde tell ſhulde longer mater dwell vaine thou knoweſt beware tourneth ball tyme thou getteſt thou lyſte put choyſe word kyng roſe vp anone vpon tyme whan ſhulde gone vnto meate iaſon ſyde ye ſhall ſo ye lyſte abyde time approcheth gan neigh faſt offycers full buſyly caſt make redy buſye cure halle bordes cure dyal hour gan marke phebꝰ ſouthward whirled vp arke hye lofte drewe none tyme kyng gone vnto meate entre halle oetes lordes knightꝭ aboute hym euerichon hercules alſo iaſon ſette meate royall ſea euery lorde lyke degree fyrſte worthy man iaſon aſſygned kynge anone ſytte owne borde hercules ſo great lorde ſette alſo faſte ſyde marſhall longer lyſte abyde aſſygne eſtates ſhulde lyke hye lowe degree ſcaffolde hye alofte noiſe gan loude nothynge ſofte trumpeter eke clarioneres noble offycers full thryftely ſerued haue halle lyke ſeaſon gan tyme fall deyntes may rekened ſothfaſtly foyſon plente kyngly fredom vnto hye lowe fulſomly gan reygne ſnowe ye hall ye manhod praiſed kyng renowne reyſed geſtes ſothly ſey whan hym lyſteth chere feſtey lyke kyng ſo thryfty wyſe deynte man deuyſe feaſt ſolempnitie grekes myght great nobely ſee kyng oetes worthyneſſe reporte therof beare wytneſſe ſo come lyue wante connynge ordre diſcryue euery courſe diuerſitees ſtraunge ſewes ſotyltees day ſerued place haue excuſed thoughe lyghtly paſſe though ordre ſayne mine englyſhe rude eke playne endite ſo hye thyng forthe reherſe kyng ſhewe geſtes nobley ouer hath doughter ſent ſpeciall byd ſhe ſhulde forth anone broughte ſouth though men ſought world thrughout plain aſſure men might founde fayrer creature womanly porte manere demure ſadder chere whoſe beaute lykely fade whan ſhe came grekes glade halle ſoth ſhe walketh vp downe womanhede pure affectiowne make chere vnto theſe geſtes newe thus medea roſen hewe freſhneſſe lyllye whyte entermedled kyndly delyte nature made face ſprede egally white rede medlynge concluſyon ennewed proportion fynally exceſſe none one two one ioyned longe endure empreſſe called nature ſhe made lyke deuiſe beholde paradyſe verye ſoth bothe one olde yonge ſytten hall therto ſhe ſucceſſyon borne heyre regyon father diſcent lyne ſhe abyde dure fyne syth ne ryght ſuccede one heyre male reade alſo boke maketh mencion vnto yeres diſcretion able age maryed withſtondynge alſo eke ſhe beaute womanhede one fayreſt read yet none bothe haue youth let clergy deſyre ſet paſſyngly ſpeciall artes called lyberall expert knowynge beſte vre konne lyſte ſuche woman herde neuer telle helicon ſhe dranke ſo welle tyme none ſemblable founde ſothe ne none ſo hable conceyue ſtudye doctrine nature diſpute termine coude alſo cauſes fynde althinges formed kynde lernyng ſo tyme ſpente ſhe knewe fyrmament trewe courſe ſterres meuynge ſhulde fall ſhe lerned aſtronomye moſte ſhe wrought nycromancye exorſiſmes cōiuracions vſed alſo make illuſyons charmes ſayde ſondrye wyſe rytes diuers ſacrifyſe encens ryches caſte fyre ſhewe thynges lyke deſire gootes horne milke blude whan mone equat ſtode fyfthe ſyxte houſe fortuned lokyng gracious theſe houre conuenient fortunate enchauntement make worke ſundry apparences well ſhe knewe heauenly influence aſpectes bothe wrothe glade ſhe thynges made apperteyne ſuche experimentes whan lyſt enchauntementes coude make wyndes blowe thondre lighten haile ſnowe freſe alſo greue men payne ſodeynely ſhe coude make rayne ſhewe wether liſt haue gaſten men ſodeyne erth quaue tourne daye vnwarely vnto nyght anone make ſonne bryght shewe beames full perſyng ful ſhene golden horne voyde nyghtes tene reiſe ye floodes wt many dredful wawe whā liſt ſhe coude eft wtdrawe eke yonge tree ſere roote rynde afterward make againe kinde luſty braunches blome budde newe alſo wynter floures freſhe hewe aray yerth tapyte hym grene beholde ioye ſene many colour ſhewynge full diuers whyte rede grene ynde pers deyſy ryche perled crowne floures winter made frowne vpon ſtalke freſhly tappere ſodeynely deadly chere coude ſomer winter tourne cauſynge daye myſtes mone olde men ſhe coude make yonge efte agayne ſpronge coude ſhewe head berde ful hore graye crafte ſo ſhe lerede tree wt fruite ſhe coude alſo make bare rinde leafe men ſtare eclipſe mone bryght ſonne naturally theyr courſe yronne apropred mai paſſe tytanes courſe kindly traſe whan ſo meueth vnder clyptik lyne clipſe mott folow auctours liſt diffine diſcription bothe twayne full coniunction ſonne beames red haue dwellyng dragones head mone ſet eke tayle nature maye fayle muſt fall eclyps veary nede ſondry bokes like ye may read bycauſe certayne interfecacions diuers circle reuolucions maked ben heauen alofte whiche cauſen v fayle ofte freſhe comfortable ſtremes v ſhad phebꝰ bryght bemes ſo mone hath made deuiſyon ſodeyne interpoſicion ſyght ſtremes viſuall may beholde yet yſene luſte fully comprehende phebus chaire cheuanſende wonte aforehande ſee great ptholome kyng egypt telleth cauſes within boke compendiouſly bothe eclyps coniunction fall naturall mocion medee though clerke ouyde tencreaſe name vpon euery ſyde lyſt ſuche thynges fable tell though poetes ſpryng well yet god forbede ye ſhulde gyue credence ſuche feynyng ſo hyghe offence sith nature muſt denyed al ſuche affirmyng likewiſe diffyed euery chriſtien ſtedfaſt beleue certainly wolde hyghly greue conſcience wyſe wene agaynſt kynde whiche ſo hye quene wight lyuynge creature shulde haue power plaine aſſure curſed thynges ſuperſticious worke kynde contrarious ¶for god almyghtye iudge iudges hath ſette lawe whiche may falle amonge planettes eternally tendure afore ordeyned eternall cure whiche may clerkes lyſt termine vpon ſyde bowen declyne diſcorde debate eternally yformed create fynger ſapience alway meue intelligence lyke lordſhyp bounde neuer yet eclyps yfounde mone beinge inconiunction haue tolde ſaue paſſyon eclyps tho againſt kinde nature knot tyme lyſt vnbynde whan goddes ſonne ſtarfe vpon roode ſonne lyfe derked good whan heauen erth wt hye compunction haue ſygnes ſhewed lamentacion earthquake light tourned derkenes dead body vpwarde gan dreſſe tombes againe deth liue stone rocke ſonder gan ryue temple veyll kut two ſygnes many yſhewed tho ye wondre token meruailous great worthy dyonyſyous vhiche athene clekes hym write called ſcholes ariopagyte whan ſawe noble famous clerke bryght daye ſodeynely ſo derke although apaynym tho dayes infecte rytes layes moſte chiefe principall phyloſophers reken yet tyme aſtoned mynde sayde platly god kynde suffreth death doubte rounde worlde ſo large shalbe diſſolued ybrought nought ſodayne chaunge haſty thought clergye knewe better ſkyll god may chaungen wyll hath power ſuche coaction vnder whoſe myght diſpoſicion lawe kynde conſtreyned ſoth ſeye poynt poynt lowely obeye euery thynge hym lyſt ordeyne elementes may courſe reſtreyne holy wryt doth witneſſe ye may ſe requeſt worthy ioſue bryght ſonne ſtode gabaon adayes ſpace one degree ſhone shewynge token trewe knyght fynally gyue lyght myght hye proweſſe cruell foon manfully oppreſſe whan fought knight ioſue fyue kinges reignyng amoree longe laſte purſuite chaſe tyll take hye treſpaſſe dempt dead bible tell ſyth god thus hyghly lyſt fulfyll knyghtes requeſt oriſon wonder though paſſyon chriſte ieſu incarnat ſake ſonne beames tho waren blak syth hath lordſhip planettes hym lyſt muſt nedely fall medea though ouydyus fable writeth ſaith thus lyſt name ſo hyghe exalte yet truth ſomewhile doth halte albe ſhe paſſynge ſorcereſſe chefeſt named chauntereſſe ¶i wyll paſſe ouer agayne matere howe ſhe came meate ye ſhall en whan father thus ſent se came anone commaundement ſhe came fynde tofore make beautie ſe men cloſet toke beſt araye tencreaſe euer ſhee maye nature worke royall apparayle theſe woman gladly wyll fayle whā beautie haue plēteuous largeſſe embellyſhe buſineſſe ryche tire vpon euery ſyde ought myſſe cloſe hyde foule ſhall couertly wryed defaute outwarde eſpied ¶but ſhe faire alſo well ſayne porte ſo womanly certayne comynge gladeth halle ioye vnto one ſe maner tho entree father bad take ſee beſyde iaſon hym diſporte womanhede recomforte ¶but oh ala lacked hye prudence diſcrete auyſe inwarde prouydence wyſedome alſo perell caſte aforne truſte amayde tendre yeres yborne lyght vnhappy fonde wylfulneſſe kynge gentylneſſe commaunded hath confuſyon diſhonour deſtruction owne doughter borne heyre alſo ſo womanly fayre ſodaynly downe diſcende conſydered myſchyefe ende ala durſt youth affye make ſytte curteſye ſhe myght caſuell mocion full lyghtly catche haue occaſyon amyſſe ala dyd ſo liſt take better hede therto auerte diſcretion wyſely caſte afore reaſon vnware chaunge womanhed whiche euery wyſe man oughte drede euer yet ſo mad wood ought reaſon coude aright good gyue fayth haſtyly credence woman without experyence nother truſt ſykerneſſe ben ſo double full brytylneſſe harde aſſure vnto longeth nature theyr birth haue alliaunce doubleneſſe variaunce hertes ſo fraile ſo vnſtable namely youthe ſo meuynge mutable ſo clerkes lyſt tendyte albe ſory wryte ſayen chaunge mutabilite apropred ben vnto feminite affyrmed ful ſage ſpecially whyle grene age wexyng whan yt yonge whoſe herte full ſelde accordeth wt tonge trouth inwardely ſought ye ſurplus remnaunt thought men may anone true patron fynde inconſtaunce whoſe flaſkyſable kynde fro meuynge wynde hercules ſtronge binde nother sampſon ſo beleue woman herte make remeue blaſe whyrleth fyre fro flee deſyre tyll accomplyſhe fully delite nature kyndly appetyte kyndly ſeketh ſewen fourme tyl courſe proceſſe may performe euen ſo theſe woman refraine ne ſewe luſte fro man man ceaſe till aſſayed wolde god nature apayed one fourme holdeth content whan boundes hath terme went deſyre ferther procede ſtyll abyte wyll excede example ſortes woman wolde abide one duety ſhoulde holde paide ſtylle abyde faile foting doth ofte ſlyde content vnitee faſt ſewen finde pluralitee nature menynge ſhewed although among ſignes outward ſhewed ofte pretende maner ſtableneſſe vnder hyd doubleneſſe well yreke outwarde eye full harde treaſon eſpye vnder curtyn veyle honeſte cloſed chaunge mutabilitye deſyre kepte full cloſe mewe thyng leueſt ſewe outwarde haue laude declyne wt faynyng fraude ¶wherfore oetes thy wyt barayne thou afore prudence naddeſt ſayne ſhulde folowe vnhappy caſe thou bolde thus ſuffer ala thine owne doughter inly freſhe hewe ſtraunge geſtes entred newe folilye lete dele thrugh thin honor worſhip thin hele loſt haſte ſhe miſchiefe brought ſtraūge lande wt ſorowe thought ſhe ſclaunder thy name miſerie ſorowe ſhame ende made thou left ſole myghteſt well complayn makē dole ala whyle prudent forſyght thou haddeſt grace record aright haue caſt diſcrete purueaunce wyſely weyed meaſure balaūce fraude woman frayltye full ſelde ſykertye latyn guydo doth expreſſe wherfore oetes verye rycheleſneſſe thou haſt one augment thy wo without recure bothe two forgo fyrſt thy treaſure thy doughter deare ſo paſſingly entere eke thyne heyre whē yt ſhe gone ſayth mine auctour ther none thy daye occupye thy royall ceptre thy land gye ¶but worth great prouidēce waker kepyng buſy diligence myghty mar god battayle might helpe defende ought auaile agayne wyt woman ſleyght whoſe fraudes bene ſo huge weyght theym lyſt aye game goeth theyr purpoſe bydeth ſo lief lothe ſo ſlye ſo prudent ſo wyſe ſtorye playnly doth deuiſe medea engyne crafte father hath treaſure raft working ſleightie gyle ye ſhall heare within litell whyle ſhe ſat meate tho tide father next iaſon ſide ſodeynly freſhe roſen hewe ful ofte tyme gan chaungen renew hundreth ſithes litell ſpace bloud goodly face vnto herte vnwarely gan avale therwithall ſhe waxeth dead pale eft anone therto take hede hewe returneth goodly reade ſtill among temblyſhe coloure roſe meynt aye lyly floure though roſe ſome dele gan pace yet ſtill lylye bydeth place till nature made theym eft ayene mete thus colde eke wt ſodayne hete medea ſelfe aſſayled paſſyngly ſore vexed trauayled nowe ſhe brent ſhe gā colde aye ſhe gan beholde iaſon yong ſhe gan deſire loke hym ſo ſhe ſet afyre beaute ſemelyneſſe euery thing ſhe inly gan inpreſſe ſhe ſawe minde thought emprynteth forgetteth nought ſhe conſydereth euery circumſtaunce port gouernaūce ſonnyſhe hayre criſped lyke golde wire knightly loke manly chere countenaunce many noble ſigne face alſo moſt gracious beninge moſt acceptable vnto pleſaunce ſhe thought full ſuffyſaunce without vnto alone well bethynke loke parſone time withouten drede meate drynke ſhe toke litell hede ſhe foode hath loſt appetite loke hym ſhe hath ſo great delite ſo prynted remembraunce loue hath caught ſo newely traunce ymarked fyery brond ſhe may eſcape honde yet eſchewe ſtroke ſpeciall ſhe yolde body hert vnto iaſon platly ſeye euer eft ſhe caſt eye whan ſhe founde leyſer opportune wyſedome ſhe wolde contune loken longe leſt men dempt amys maner theſe woman kept cloſe wonderly ſecre chere man could ſe ſhe ment none occaſyon put theym ſuſpection openly token ſene caſt rather men ſhulden wene encheſon abſtinence ſhe abode thus ſylence onely womanhede honeſt ſhame chaſte drede together herte met whych twayne haue ſo maydē let meate drinke wold ſeme thus wit ſhe made theim deme ſo caſt theyr opynion thus ſhe blent diſcreſcion ſo cheare could euery thinge excuſe gaue fooles matter muſe ¶no chere vnbrideled tyme aſterte one thyng cloſed hert alder chere declared maydens haue ofte ſyth ſpared ſhewe deſyre dede falleth ſo take hede flouren virgynitye theyr youth haue lyberty ſpecyfy theyr hertes woulde kepe theym cloſe bolde ſhewe ſumme theyr ſentence thus medea kepyng aye ſylence ne let worde lippes pace couertly ſobre chere face ſhe ment ſheweth eye ſuch ſorte man could eſpye hoote fyre breſte yreke ſelfe right thus ſhe gan ſpeke ſhe ſothe ſo much good would god yong luſty man ſo fayre ſemely ſight aſſured owne knight moſt pleſaunt entyre berde yſprong ſhining lyke golde wyre wel ylimed compact meaſure well growe heyght good ſtature lyketh euery parte ſo wele aſſent fortune whele ewred ſtandē grace ſemeth vpon knightly face heauen beholde albe therwith herte fele colde yet ſothe may none ala nill pyty leſte knewe entent much trouth hym ment ala taketh maner hede albe brenne doth glede dead dare diſcure ala piteous woful auenture rewful helples mortall paine thus dead dare complayne frende foo chaunce ala find ſome helpe ſuccour caſe trewly nathles ſhall deuiſe nothing meane honeſt wyſe lyke ſhall well openly founde deſyre knyt bound wedlock neuer then twine meaning cleane devoyde ſyn grounded ſet vpon al clenlyneſſe without fraude doubleneſſe clean pure mine entencion lo aye maner condicion theſe woman ſo well fayne ſhewe one though thinke twayne couertly nothing ſayne humble chere face playne encloſe theyr luſtes ſuch ſubtyltye vnder boundes al honeſtye theyr entent though trecherye withal ſurplus ſmothely couered though fayth afore pretend theyr fraude floriſhing defēde ſpeake full fayre word forth blēde doubleneſſe encloſed end yet deceyte couertly yment vnder ſuger fayned cleane entent ſothe exiſtence truſte well al apparence ſhewe one another meane whoſe blewe lightly dyed grene vnder floures depeynt ſtableneſſe ſerpent dareth newfangelneſſe playn ſeme wordes fair gloſed vnderneth theyr couerte wile cloſed thing deareſt theyr paye deny ratheſt ſwearen naye lyketh guydo womē endite ala ſo curſedly would wryte agaynſt theym haue debate right ſory englyſhe tranſlate reprefe theym euyll ſeye leuer theyr loue deye wherfore pray theym take pacience purpoſe theym offence ſo good perfyte euerychone reken trowe one hert trewe though amōg cheſe thē loues newe wayeth wel nothing blame often tyme ſe men ſame muſt puruay thē men thē refuſe yf coulde wolde theim full excuſe ſytteth woman lyue alone ſtore haue mo one praying theim grace hope theim treſpace though makyng ſame guido wryteth oryginall miſſayeth let hym beare ye wyfe ſyt well vengeaunce byte ſo theſe woman hath offended myght ſhuld well amended ſhulde receiue duely penaunce yf died withouten repentaunce diſpeyred ſaluacion ſhulde euer haue remiſſion yf content redreſſe may bene clerkes beare witneſſe trouth alyue meane guido ſhulde ſhryue bytter penaunce playnly ſhulde haue tyme depe ygraue ſhulde remembre platly aſterte repente hoole herte ſo ſpake confuſyon wyll longer make diſgreſſyon matter letteth guydo tell ſhall workynge medee hath lycence father nome chamber alone ycome whan hal withdrawen al ye pres whan iaſon hercules lyke kynge meate badde chambres conueied lad full royally arayed well ſayne euery wall couered certayne clothe golde full ſtately wiſe whyle ye haue herde deuiſe medea chambre gone wherby ſelfe complaynynge euer one gaue iſſue paynes ſmarte ſo ſore hath wounded harte loue hath brought ſo ſodeine rage lykely ſoone aſwage ſothneſſe furious god cupide hath ſuch fyre kyndled ſyde neuer lykly lete violent feruent heate encreaſe gan paine breſt atwyxt twayne great debate ſtronge battayle feruently eche dyd aſſayle contek erne game departed betwixt loue ſhame metynge together vnſet ſteuen albe fielde tho parted euen loue ſoth full hye renowne bolde hardy lyke fierſe lyowne fereful ſpere ſwerd knife hote haſty auntre lyfe eke ſurquidous ſtoute full pryde chiefe champyon god cupyde cauſeth ofte free bonde full many peryll take honde cauſed hath full many man death many one yelden vp breth made ther woundes largly blede peryll loue taketh none hede get hym honour excellence fame ¶but contrary enmye called ſhame lyke coward faynte hertles neuer dare ſene pres lacke māhod draweth hī euer abacke ſo ferd dreadfull wrake like chylde yonge tender age hath nother herte yet corage aſſayle ſo feble myght yet full ofte hath ſtonde ſyghte many louer lete ſpede falſe cōſpiring brother dred drede ſhame allyed one aſſent haue piteouſly denyed vnto loue hert herdineſſe ne durſt worde expreſſe whā loue māhode willeth ſpeake wood fyre breſt reke vpon poynte ſhulde aſſaye shame cometh anone vtterly ſayeth nay cauſeth loue horne ſhrynke tabaſhe chere pitiouſly wyncke cowardly cauſe tho appayre thus ſhame froward like contraire helpe drede loues folke feare doubtleſſe ſo ſhame nought ne kouthe aſwell nigh ferre loue lawes ſhuld often tyme erre winde honeſtye cheyne bondes bridell breake reyne right horſe trayſe large lite nought louers wolde take charge vſe wyll luſt tenſewe al ſhame kept mewe within breſt ſo wight knowe outward porte loue beareth ful lowe ne ſhame clekes haue compiled hertes daunger exiled al ſtraungeneſſe feyned falſe diſdeyne ne ſhame playnly wardeyne theſe woman wrytyng theſe olde without aſſaulte caſtell yyolde nede ſyege layne ſuche caſe longe treaty vayne nature louen proceſſe ¶but nowe ala dread ſhamfaſtnes haue daunted loue full lowe maner made humble port cheare haue eke vyolence manhode put ſylence ben great cauſe morning paine thus amiddes either theſe twaine loue ſhame euen ſo vpon poynt medea ſtode tho great diſioynt ſhe ne may paine endure hoote ſhe brent wofull creature betwixt meane loue ſhame whan loue wolde thing attaine deſyres declare came ſhame anone put doubte redy dread luſt deny thus ſhe ſtode doubtfull ieopardy loue ſhame maner traunce full euenly vphanged balaunce ſhame great loue yet yt well appeared ſyghes ſore ſtormy cruell auenture dread ſhame durſt ſhe diſcure fyre loue hath breſt encloſed whiche full harde depoſed thus ſhe hange amyddes betwene two ſhe ne wiſt beſt tyll fortune double face vnhappely hath wrought get grace whyrlyng whele cauſeth wretch full lowe adowne loute whā beſt wene ſittē hye aloft plaine profe men may ſe full ofte gerineſſe reuolution ſo lady tranſmutacion full ofte time falſe full vnſtable enhaſteth thynges fooles full agreable ende confuſyon vnder ſuger ſhroude poyſon aye fortune maner wretch ſheweth fayre ſemblant face flattery ſhe full beninge eye fully fooles parfourmen entent great miſchefe ſhēt ende crafte teſchewe ſodeyne harme taile doth ſew ryght fell whylome medee gynning grounde aduerſitye ¶for lady called fortune ygraunted hath leyſer opportune ſhewe iaſon hooly herte made wt repentaunce ſinerte daye meredien whan apollo beames ſhene ſouthe plage gan weſter faſt oetes father hath yſent haſte medea com hym anone bad ſhe ſhuld gone vnto iaſon hercules make thē chere amiddes al pres ſhe caught hath oportune ſpace deſyre ſawe eke place father moſt occupied ſhe thought bene eſpyed well apperceiuing great buſyneſſe towardes iaſon anon ſhe gan dreſſe haſte full knightly chere curteys wiſe gan drawen nere towardes ayen ſawe let thus together met mede ſyghing firſt abrayde ſyth iaſon euen thus ſhe ſayd ¶how iaſon helpe medea oetes daughter kynge colchos enamored achieued conqueſt golden fleſe cap vi iaſon quod ſhe thyne hye nobleſſe thy manhode thy gentilneſſe thy perſon aſſembled yfeare thy knighthode firſt requere thy conceite thyne opinion arrecte preſumption doubleneſſe yet inconſtaunce womanhead neither variaunce bolde nothynge ſpare meaninge platly declare without deceyte wordes trewe playn beſeching firſt ſhal ſayne without goodly hede beningnely taken hede pacyently wordes ye lyſte ſaye take beſt entent nothing greue thinges two myne hert ſore ameue ſaye loue gentylneſſe meane clerely expreſſe perſon nothing concele departe profe ye ſhall fele ſemeth firſt curteſye ſothfaſtnes ſith gentrye ſtraungers euery maner wight bounde holde due right maken cheare trewely bycauſe iaſon ſe much manhode ſo great worthineſſe fayne buſineſſe may lyke worde hert ſhe gan ſike ſake ſayd thus ouermore fele full great anoy ſore mened without auiſeneſſe onely youth wilfull hardineſſe fleſe golde getten ye may empriſe euer aſſay perillous playnly achieue verye ſothe ye coulde wene leue doubtles well aſſure finall mede great auenture deathe ſaue report ſhame ye wene getten name end playn ſhall tourne contrayre ginning ſo ſhall fine varye wit man engine force might though neuer ſo expert fight haue armes paſſing exerciſe ye ſleyghtes olde newe empriſe though beſt brethed endure deuiſe armure ſo euer wepen bringe harded ſtele trenchaunt perſing yet laſt whan hath ſought without auayle may right nought ¶wherfore iaſon haue compaſſion youthe pure affection wilfully ye ſhulden thus lorne ben bloode line ſo high yborne certaynly may none ye counſayle take none may helpe eaſe ala iaſon wyll ye appeaſe manly corage caſe yblent counſayle bene obedient durſt ſwere ye ſhuld haue victory ben remembred put memory perpetually knighthod win fleſe golde yonde within yle ſtandes beſide mar gouernour gide wherfore one ſelfe aſſente counſayle fully conſent fewe wordes ſo ye liſt ſpede leue luſt worketh reade iaſon full humble chere anſwered ſayd mine owne lady deare thanke beſt wiſe right thus ferre forthe may ſuffiſe power platly may attayne mine hertes quene lady ſoueraine ye may hooly well enſure life may dure truſteth right well liſte fayne liue dye ſhall luſt reſtrayne owne aſſured man obeye euer without chaunge doubleneſſe liue ſothfaſtnes liſt trewe affection vpon life haue compaſſion gentilleſſe ye liſt haue suche chierte body ſaue good fayth verye due right ybounde owne knight vnto mine ende ſpecially grace ye ſo beningnely liſteth ſelfe counſaile neuer erſt degre ne ſeruice woman heade wordes ful goodliheade owne man liſteth recomforte ſothe ſo reporte thouſande folde pleſaunt neuer erſt merite gat graunt ne deſert requeſt prayer rather frely herte entere lyſt vnrequired woo rewe vndiſſerued ſo trewe enſure vpon fayth faſt ſeruice ſhall vnto laſte parſeuer ſothely ſhalbe ſlouth variaunce thereto trouthe finally ſaye withouten wene fewe wordes right meane liſt fayne flatter delude beheſte deathe ſhall conclude parcas ſhall liues threde rend ſome thus make ende vvell thā quod ſhe ful wiſely hert ye muſt afore conſydre aduerte aduenture ye ſhall take hande prudently perill vnderſtande warely caſt haue full well minde mortall harme tayle behinde well credible leue well impoſſible ginne honour alſo fine thilke fleſe hye power diuine preſerued wyth marcys mighte ſo therfore entreth fight full harde thence eſkape fyery flawme bulles gape bene braſſe trapped leuen ben dread thē lightening ye heauē tofore dint great thonder ſeuered hath full many toure ſunder vnto aſhes man conſume wherfore rede ye preſume ram aſſayle leſt ye laboure
