leſe yet withdraw foote ſith ye may cheſe good aduiſe diſcreſiowne honour ſafe hye renowne ſo ye liſt worthineſſe onely folye haſtineſſe empriſe head procede ye liſt like rede saue ſelfe woo al miſchaūce like ye ſhall mine ordinaunce ye commytte lowely lyſte obeye without fraude ſeye iaſon ther thā ſitting borde medea emprintynge euery worde waxed ire almoſt vnpacient ſayd ala entent counceyle leue empriſe certes foule cowardyſe gyn thynge myght chyeue euery man wolde ſhame repreue eke reporte confuſyon pride preſumption toke whan large hye thynge ſo great charge durſt diſtruſtyng myſchyefe accomplyſhe whan came prefe leuer myne owne lady dere ieoparde put ſelfe one wordes fewe ſmale pyeces hewe rather ſhulde cowardely forſake thylke empryſe haue vndertake ye well knowe leue thus ala let counſeyle plainly caſe ſo euer happe falle truſteth ryght well ſhall none ſhulde cowarde harte fro purpoſe way diuerte without laude lyfe ſhulde lede ſhame eternall iuſtlye mede throughout worlde noted ouer euery lande ſpoke ſpeciall iaſon hath ſo hyghly vndertake wherof feare dare none ende make thynketh ryght well ſhall betide lyfe deth miſchiefe abyde thervpon trouth enſure ſo ferforth lyfe may endure ſhall parfourme haue nowe begon though ſo honor may wonne muſte deth beye wil leue bett deye liue aſhamed cowardiſe ſlouth ſemeth hygh routhe man tappere dare ſhewe head whan hath one honour vyllanede time whan yt name ſlayne euery man ſhulde coueite rather faine dye honour liue wretche though thinge death ſtretche welcome beit ſhall well abyde ſome ſo betyde iaſon quod ſhe ſyth ſtandeth ſo ye algates deſyre haue ought eſpye ye leuer ſhortly dye rather lyue haue ye ſaye ſhame yet erneſt game ſuche monſters vnwarely deale lyke dede hereafter ye ſhal feale therfore meued pytee greatly ſteered ye volunte without aduyſe diſcreſion counſayle elles deliberation lyſt take meruailous voyage youth alſo courage gouerned ben chiefely matere luſte two feare inparded ben ye purpoſe ſewe impoſſyble ye eſchewe ſodeyne death nother free bonde crafte man hath power withſtonde ¶wherfore thinke herte good entent caſt yea yet ye ſhent tourne ſhape remedye suche routhe haue ye ſhulden dye father loue moſt rather ye ſhulde wiſe loſte ſhall offende vtterly diſpleaſe friendes ſo may eaſe ſhall fynde ſuche meane weye leaſt ſe deye caſe thinke gyde ſhall ſette aſyde firſt diſcent ſtocke royall ¶and ouer myne heritage withall lykewiſe honour ſhal put abacke helpe ſhalbe lacke yfounde ſo ye kinde ye lyſte haue mynde deſerue goodly quyte conſyderyng firſt nat alite ſaue lyue ſtant ieopardye peryllous ye ought eſpye ſhall ſo ordeyne crafte atwyxe v twayne parte hope ſhall well vpon poynt ſo may fele faythfully ioye woo ſmarte full accorde body herte deſire ye condeſcend vndertake make therof ende ¶this ſothly ladye ſayde iaſon tho aſſented without wordes mo fulfyll euery circumſtaunce euer thinge may pleſaunce quod ſhe ſaine firſte wt fayth herte plaine myght buſy cure meanyng hole ye aſſure hereafter take wyfe holde kepe terme life dede accorde may wt heſt fyne ſumme requeſte except ye ſhall ordeyne repayre father reigne faithfully ye ſhall lede whan ſo ye ſhall ſuccede death heritage herte aye one lyke corage ye ſhall alwayes founden true cheriſhe chaunge newe like mine eſtate without varyaunce ye lyue haue remembraunce gentleneſſe great nede none aliue may ought ſpede ſo lyueth mortall aſſayle force marcyall dragon bulles yfeare ſo firſt lere hooly manere howe ſhall gye like thinke ſpecifye whan ſo happeth mete againe none may helpe herin certayne caſe whiche platly ye ſhall fynde naught aſke ye ayene kynde sothly quod iaſon al ſhalbe ye deuyſe ſo faith theron aſſure oh goodlieſt creature euer yet ſawe vnto paye fayreſt eke ſoth naye bountie ye ben incomparable death ye ben ſo marciable whyle lyue ſaye fayth myne herte meneth tunge ſayth wyll founde aldertreweſt man life death euer grace pleaſaunt perfourme heſtes graunt fully worke ſaluation ye haue ſayde full concluſyon truely ye bearen lyfe beaute haue ſuch prerogatife paſſyng echone liſt gloſe amonges floures doth rede roſe ſomer amyd leues ſoote vere hath made roote humidyte kyndly aſcende barrayne ſoyle clothe amend winter blaſtes haue ſhakē bare ſote bloſmes freſhly repayre medowes many ſundry hewe tapited bene diuers floures newe ſundry motlees luſtly ſene holſome bawne ſhad among ye grene ¶ryght roſe fayreſt echone ryght ſo hath nature ſet alone ſhe made firſt deuiſe aboue haue pryſe ye bene bounte ſpring welle therto beaute ſothly ye excelle beare life comparyſon ne may made ſo diſcreſcion ye paſſen euery man may ſe finde vnto goodlyeſt euer yet borne without lorne helpe ſuccoure fully deſtitute ne founde refute frō whō al fredom meward doth haboūd paſſingly euer bounde ferre forth ſely life may ſtretche ſake death ne reche vnto might pleaſure bene helpe ſo goodly liſt ſene neclygence ſhuld thing refuſen ye would might reaſon full well merked noted eke wilfull nycetye folylye voyde away grace rage aman chaſe wilfull fortune whan ſhe beninge wherfore nowe hooly reſigne herte body lyfe eke death hande ye laſteth breath othes affirme may parſeuer mine endinge daye trewe ſpouſe haue ſayd ſworne beheſted playnly toforne vpon euery thinge obeye may pleaſe till ſuch time deye ſome ſhuld longer tarye beheſt ſhall neuer varye ¶thus whan medea ſawe ſtedfaſtnes ſuppriſed ſo hye gladneſſe ſo great ioye pleynly herte ſhe voyde euery wo ſmert ſo lowly luſt obeyd ſhe went thus ſhe ſeyde ¶iaſon quod ſhe ſhall well ordayne meane waye wherby twayne may eft agayne leyſure mete ſone perfourme done matterlike entent ſhall made finall ſacrament deſire man ſhall vnbinde though nowe therto may leiſure fīde toward eue ſhall eſkape truſt right well time ſhape right ſecretly may mete yfeare ſhall ſende priuy chambre mine ſhall conuye vnto chaumbre priue wey certayne houre withouten fable entent ſhalbe moſt greable vpon point phebus wt light yweſtred eke dercke night hath wt dimmeſſe ſhadowes black hemiſperye fully ouertake oft giueth fauoure fortune vnto theiſe louers leyſour opportune perfourme luſtes achieue right anone ſhall drawe eue ſhall vnto cloſet ſend euery thinge make ende togither ſhall leyſur ſpeake euerich hertes breake eft declare ſumme haue ſpoken fill good leyſur fully byhete ſhall ordeyne whan ſo v luſt mete ſet time euer ſay nay alway nyght whan paſſed day myghty ioue wyſely ſuccour hence forth wyll hooly whyle lyue wakyng ſlepe ſo ye heſtes kepe iaſon lowly gan enclyne ſayd far man may ymagine wight may clearly comprehende wyll vnto liues ende ſeruaunt trewe faythfully quyte though ſaye lyte fayth ſhalbe nertheleſſe though paynt compaſſe gay proceſſe ſoueraigne hertes quene tyll dead ſhall trewly meane haue trouth whyle haue lyfe mind end ye ſhall hereafter finde theyr ſpeche ende thus make medea ſhope take leue anone amonges preſe firſt father ſyth hercules longer bode forthwith anone haſte ſhe vnto chambre gone vp downe ſhe made many went none meine wetyng ſhe ment caſting wayes purpoſe achieue wittes gan buſyly meue ſhe thus rometh habytacle ſide let obſtacle thinge would ſore greue ſtudy till drewe eue leue complaining wo many thought walking fro ¶the midday hour gone ouerſlide tytan ſo faſt doth chayre ryde day arke eaſt weſt compaſſed fyry ſtedes haue almoſt ouer paſſed orizonte drowen downe ful lowe golden waine man might know hidde fyery beames bright diſcence full farre ſyght hirenes cope myrke euening begon dirke twylight day gan faide heſperus beames glade ben ſo freſhe ſo luſty ſo merye gan recomforte hemiſperye ¶whan thus medea ſelfe alone hyghe deſyre gan make mone ſhe ſo longe abode knyght alwaye accountyng houres nyght full trouble buſye thought hath full ſtreitly ſerched ſought ready waye wel ſetting purpoſe albe ſhe kept full cloſe amyd herte quapping wawe dreade feare tyll hope gan adawe bad ſhe ſhuld ryght mery glad tyll dreade agayne made ſobre ſadde leſt deſyre troubled let thus ſhe abay yſet amyd hope fearfull dreade alſo ſhe ne wyſt beſt ¶for deſyre hygh affection hoote brent opynyon luſt ſhe mete iaſon agaynſt dreade come anone made fearfull leſt ſhe eſpyed ill holpe remedyed onely fortune derke night whych ſhe made full glad lyght recomforted onely thoſe two good hope made glad alſo gan anone caſten deuyſe moone heauē would aryſe whan ſhe horne pale wolde ſhed lyght vpon hylle vale gan acounte caſte well tyme founde quarter paſſed pryme ſhe well knowyng arte ſawe ſoth fourth part mone ſhadde newe lyght paſſed courſe aryght tyme coniunction three ſygnes full computacion dayes ſeuen complete age ¶at time ſhe brennyng rage one darted cupides arowe gan loke beholde narowe euery dore liſten buſely wyght ſhe myght eſpye courte walke go man romyn fro ſore ſhe dradde goynge vp downe whan ſo ſhe herde noyſe ſowne whā ſhe heareth whiſperyng venim ſothly ere wiſhed ſlept faſt bed pytyous lyfe longe nyght ſhe led wtout reſpite though wyght coude knowe till hye mydnyght cockes crowe whych tyme whan al buſhte ſtyl taccomplyſhe remnaūt wyll euery made ſylence cleped anone vnto preſence aged vecke fer yeares yronne ſuch crafte ſo mikle helpe kon thriftly bryng thing afore caſten euery doubte ¶of yeares paſſed olde experyence hath gyue theim ſo paſſyng hye prudence loue ſleyghtes knowe ſhe made dogge bowe medea diſcureth al thoughte fro poīt poīt hath forgat righte nought charged releaſe ſmerte recomforte troubled herte haſte anone vpon waye vnto chambre iaſon conuaye ſhe anone rekles caſe gone hym forthe eaſy paſe ſhe newe lere hath brought ye ſhal heare vvhā cock comon aſtrologere midnight hour wt voyce clere began ſowne buſy payne beate breſte wynges twayne time mynute wyll pace warne place tide ſeaſon night medea awayte vpon knight full ready entre kepe ſhe lyſt full lytell ſlepe ne parcell thought whā iaſō chambre brought without eſpying maner wight ſhe anone conueyeth hym full ryght cloſet haſte ſhe maye full well beſene great ryche araye ſyde ſhe made take ſee firſt al ylke leaſe thre moſt expert caſe ſodeynly tourned braſe olde vecke ſtare vpon mone walked hath theym left alone medea dores faſt ſhet iaſon downe anone ſhe hath ſet firſt finde buſy might chambre ſhe ſet vp light torch great cyerges ful royall aboute pyllers euery wall whych gaue lyghte like ye ſonne ſhene cheſte wrought cryſtall clene firſte ſhe taketh paſſage whych ſhe toke ryche image pure golde full luſty beholde theyr cuſtome rytes olde myghty ioue eterne increat yhalowed alſo conſecrat whych image deuoutly ſhe ought humble hert iaſon firſt ſhe brought made lowly theron take othe vnto laſt lyef lothe ſhuld take vnto wyfe fro daye forthe duryng life herte vnfayned fayth inuyolate cheryſhe lyke eſtate fro till tyme finde ſhe euer floured vyrgynitye myne auctour well reherſe aye kept cleane touche man thought dede neuer amys ſhe herte hooly gyuen vnto iaſon euer mo anone hath put hande vnto ſwore fully ye haue heard ſaye requeſtes without delaye kepe thē aye life may laſte oh ala ſoone ouercaſt heſt fayth wt aſſured fraude flatterye • ured couertly innocence trewe meanyng diligence euer ſhe deuyſe deceyued falſhed man though ye trouth apparent aboue yet doubleneſſe ſo ſlyghly ſhoue though ſothely allyed trewe meaning ſo yt nothinge eſpyed vnder fayre chere faining fallaces might ſhe haue wrought ī caſe thā thy ſake ceptre regallye lordes eke alie forſoke one toke hede pitye goodly hede loſte friendes good fame iaſon ſaue fro ſhame yet moreouer forſoke heritage borne ſo hye parage ſhulde haue ſucceſſion heyre diſſent region womanly ſhe wolde quite yfeare ſhe hath ſet mite one houre ſhe hath forſake vnto ſhe hath holy take truſt thou ſhouldeſt haue kynde rich honour ſhe hath ylefte beynde exyle hath choſe gone kynne ſely mayde alone ¶alas wepe thyne vnkyndeneſſe hath ſhe fro death fro diſtreſſe preſerued yet thou takeſt none hede ſhuld haue died ne ſhe thy read thy conqueſt ſhe cauſe may ſhortly clauſe write bountie briefly comprehende effectually perfourmed ende wordes fewe ne may tolde thrugh yu haſt riche fleſe golde manly conquered withouten doubte vnlikely haue brought whan thou helpe tho deſtitute thine comforte refute thou maieſt denye erthly honour ſhe gan defye conſerue heuineſſe eke father hath richeſſe enpeyred pitie whoſe example woman may well lere ſhuld faith truſten man ala medea ſo mykle ſterres aſtronemye yet ſawe ſhe afore deſtinye loue hath put ſo gouernayle al crafte ne myght auayle ſlowe calculation caſte afore conſtellation birthe eke wofull fate rekleſhed ſhe ſawe late ſuppoſe connyng fallyble doubtles ſemeth incredible ſhe wiſte toforne piteouſly ſhe lorne ye ſhall ſe hereafter haſtely ſtory teacheth befell iaſon medee fyrſt ye ſhall maner holly ſee ſhe gan wirche ſwore ſame night ala ſhe hath forbore maydenhead great pitie yet ſhe mente naught elles honeſtye ſuppoſe ſhe went haue wyfe touchyng holde ſtrife yet one thing dare afyrme ſayne ſo meaning theſe twayne ne one wonder fer atwene ſhe truely gan meane honeſte thynkyng outrage like maide innocent age perfourme fleſhly falſe delight acheue fylthy appetite wrought euery thing entent contraire ala ſhe tho ſo debonaire truſte vpon curteſye acquite gentery haſtely rewe vpon ſmarte woman ben ſo pytefull herte wyll gladly ſhewen petie miſhappe ſe man fall ſaue lyfe rather ſhoulde dye ſo medea ſhortly ſeye caſtyng peryll ſhall fall deſyres luſtes holy obeyeth full might ſo longe almoſte night hath courſe rounde gone whiche tyme thus ſpake iaſon lowly ſayde lady time aryſe ſoone wyll pryme ye may ſee well day beginneth ſpringe may howe byrdes ſynge prayinge beſte wyſe ſhall worke ye lyſte deuyſe ceriouſly euery thyng diſpoſe beſeche goodly freſhe roſe myne enterpryſe bring vnto ende erſt fro henſe wynde saue thincke firſt treate maner ye ſhall countrey lete grece repaire agayne whiche lande great felicitie truſteth wel nothyng adrede reygne ſhall lede conqueſt ſo wynne wherfore pray goodly begynne ſhall worke haſt may good fayth anone wil daye ¶to ſhe ſpake ſaying ye ſhal myn owne iaſon vnto deare ſelfe concluſyon aſſented ful affection wittes hole herte enfourme ye ſhall aſterte euery daunger lytell yle ſo ye lyſt bide whyle vp ſhe roſe haſte ſhe maye cofer treaſour laye wēt anone brought hōde ryche ymage ſyluer ſhe fonde ſothely meruaylous entayle whoſe power vertue auayle effectually entent agayne magik enchauntement ſyt force sorcerye made ſo aſtronomye houre choſen equat none clerkes olde full long agone whilom whā flouring ī age vſed make ſuch ymages kyng called thelomee ſo iaſon wylled hath medee beare ymage hym pryuely ye haue herd worke effectually euery thynge ſhe dyd aſſygne ſhe toke hym medycine made maner oyntment hym enoynt brent riche precious thā bawme agayne malyce eche fire flawme ſhe toke hym anone ryche rynge wherin ſet ſtone vertue venym deſtroye ſyde myght hym anoye ſtone furthermore might yf man coude beare aright within hand next ſkyn encloſed ſtrength ſyght ſhuld depoſed theim would gaſen beholde ſo euer hand holde ſuch vertue infallyble ſtorye ſayeth inuyſible ſtone theſe prudent clerkes call achates moſt vertuous founde ſothly cecile ſtone whylom wrote virgyll venus eneas ſente firſt whan cartage went ¶and ſhe iaſon toke certayne byll wrytten lyke boke iourney myght much auayle bad wyſely ne fayle bethought graciouſly ſpede firſt ſcripture rede ram touche wyſe charging eke afore hye empryſe humble hert great deuocion knelyng ſaye oryſon vp downe wrytten bill praying goddes lowely fulfyll requeſt mercy haue pitye miſchiefe ſaue chiefe ſocoure toke hym vyoll lycoure bad manly without feare drede come vnto bulles reade hym caſt knightly eſcape faſt ſeeth theim gape theyr golles lycour caſte hym nede lytel theim gaſte theyr iawes togither ſhall glyewe ſyde ſhall eſchewe bide luſt hym lyſt conſtreyne doubtles maugre al theyr buſye peyne ſhall theim daunte therwt make ſo tame hym liſt earneſt game myght theym make louten encline theym bowen backe chyne lycour ſhall theyr iawes ſo coharte lyghtly ſhall ſundre parte offende noyen wight whē ſhe thus ſayd vnto knight euery thynge gyue inſtruction playn doctrine informacyon ſhall ſcape daungers take hede worke auyſely ¶and thus agreyd thought ye beſt parte men theyr reſt awaked drewe towardes daye well ſawe morowe graye leſt men theym ſuſpiciō hye prudence diſcrecion atwene twelight rody morowe toke theyr leue wt ſaint iohn ye borow oft kyſſyng louers whē twinne ſo went ſhe left within beyng hope mete agayn ſome daye iaſon faſt euer maye gan ordayne iourney achieue thought would anō go take leue wyſe wtin litel whyle maner rude ſtyle purpoſe ſothly ſpare ſupporte playnly declare vvhan rowes rayes rede eſtward v full early gonnen ſprede euen twelyght dawnynge larke cuſtome gynneth ſing ſalue heauenly laye luſty goddeſſe morowe graye meane aurora afore ſonne wonte tench • ſe blacke ſkyes donne derkeneſſe dymmy night freſhe phebus cōforte light brightnes beames ſhene ouergylt hye hylles grene floures eke agayn morowe tyde vpō ſtalkes gā playn theyr leues wide whan iaſon companye toward kynge full faſt gan hym hye fonde lyke eſtate ſceptre hādeful pompous elate hye ſee regally sittyng full kyngly amid cheualrye lordes enuiron ¶at • tyme yonge champion vnder vowe ſtanding ram ſterne face tofore kyng cam beſechyng hym magnificence ſame day graunt lycence hys armes make mo delayes concluding playnly aſſayes daye felde found achieue lyke bound olde beheſt poynt declyne life death till parfourme fine holy auntres fleſe belonge kynge requyryng lōger prolōge goodly graūt fine empryſe kynge ful ſobre wyſe conſydering ſumme demaunde iaſon ſpoke ſayd ſhall commaūd requeſt perfourmed haſt albe quod ful ſore agaſt wylfulneſſe thou ſhulde deſtroyed leſt men thy death arected vnto therupon would blame ſet royall power ne let thy manly youth ſuch ieopardy ſothe great vylany preiudice eſtate name afterward men ſhould put ī blame falſe reporte wrong opynyon withſtode thy deſtruction ¶wherfore rede yu yet bet auyſed counſayle let diſpyſed better honoure certayne thy country repayre againe wilfully take hande mortall thyng man may withſtād rede fully myn aduiſe take hede therto ſyth ye wyſe leſt thou repent late yf ſo thou wilt algate thy purpoſe holde rede almyghty mar praye thy ſpede gyde whatſoeuer ſhal befall eke praye goddes safe ſound thy body reſtore ſome thou getteſt ¶and whan iaſon thus herd kyng diſmayed ſtoned thyng knyghtly wiſe reuerence thankyng highly royall excellence grace beningnytye vpon death hym lyſt haue pytye fully concluding touchyng battayle nother rede counſayle wyſe purpoſe ſhould withdrawe lyke ſtatute playnly lawe right ſo far forth fortune wyll hym eure ſo beſyde auenture settyng aſyde euery feare drede platly ſayd wyll procede parfourme hath vndertake ydle mo ſkylles make allege againe iaſon full openly plaine touching ye ſurplus dredfull thing departyng thus ſayd kyng audience tho lordes ſo hereafter fall ſo euer malys theron muſe worlde fyrſt excuſe goddes platly acquyte though deye ye nothyng wyte ne man ſhall arecte ſkylle worke freely wyll agayne aduice hye prudence lyfe death preſence hooly herte neuer flytte vnto goddes fortune commytte lyſt ordayne againe whoſe wyll ſhall neuer plaine ne ſhall put blame ſo betide honour ioye ſhame thyng thus ende make tyme leue take tho ſtande one one toke hande wyſe forth gan hym dreſſe anone thyncke expreſſe vvhan titan wt feruēt hete drawen vp dewe fro leues wete towarde myd morowe diffine vpon houre whan clocke nine iaſon full manly full like knight armed ſtele cherefull glad lyght gan dreſſe hym forth hap euer fal ſayd dieu vnto feres boote vpon ſtronde lone whan came londe water veſſell lafte fyrſt remembryng crafte medea circumſtaunces ſhulde kepe obſeruaunces euery thing well mynde anone full manly fynde ſhope forth went knyghtly paſe toward bulles forged wer braſe point whan iourney gan medea wexed full pale wan ſore agaſt nothing might glade ruthe ſee wo ſhe made ſo teares chekes twayne full pyteouſly gan deſtylle rayne fordewed wedes blake aye ſorowe ſhe made ſake lyke woman fearefull doubte armes ful māly brought ſobbe ſyghe ſhe peace leſt haſt ought rekles fro point point ſhe bad life ſhe hath hym lad ¶and ſe ſhulde defende gan anone greces aſſende touret hye pynacle ſhe myght haue tho none obſtacle lettyng nother haue ſyghte hym owne choſen knight euer amonge wordes ſhe brake ſtoundemell thus ſelfe ſhe ſpake ¶o thou iaſon ſouerayne hertes heale thou ought knew wo fele sothly trowe ſhulde aſterte trewe thy hole herte god praye iourney leſte may tyme tournen beſt kepe ye ſaulfe ſounde euery membre yefe might fully remembre taught ſame fourme euery thynge fully perfourme day thine honour anaunce ſe hole pleaſaunce certes iaſon fylle ought amiſſe fare well helth worldly bliſſe fare well mirthe ſolace welfare fortune grace one harte ſuffiſaunce ¶lo gouernaunce firſt fro ye time lande hath nome firſt whan thether come bulles fell diſpiteous caſte fyre flawme furious fro mouthes wonder large huge againe whiche chiefe refuge hym ſaue brent enoynted oyntement body kept damage thilke fyre ſo full rage ſmokes darke full horrible whiche eſcape almoſte impoſſyble man eſtate without comforte counſayle medee whoſe doctryne iaſon ſo worke ſcaped miſtes darke ſyre blaſes blake eyre ſo cloudy hath make hym made ſo diſcrete ſage vertue onely thilke ſame ymage whych necke bare wherby ſo prudent ſo ware ye bulles haue moſt feerſly gaped hath theyr malyce ſo auyſedly ſcaped enfection theyr troubled eyre hath vanquiſhed diſpeire effect agayne foule fume would man vnto death conſume ymage ful preſeruatyfe diffend ſaue lyfe ſurely kepe drede ful ofte ſythe wrytte rede vertue thilke ſame oryſon vnto hym full protection fell therby diſtreſſe rather ſykerneſſe preſerue mortall caſe toke lycoure vyall therwithall full lyke manly man one toke bulles nought forgat ſo warely caſt therwtal theyr iawes cloſed faſt vertue ſo mightely englued ther hath vtterly eſchewed hole enfection ſmoky leuen whē eyre gan clere al ye heauen ye myſtes waſted toforne māly hert raught hath horne ſterne bulles vyolence drew forth defēce yo • keth ſo maner plough made go paſe vp ſo eare londe lyſt ſo buxom fonde ſoyle ſmothe bare playn redy made bearen grayne renges tourned vp ſo downe tho theym rebellyowne humble meke redy deſyres playnly fulfyll ¶and iaſon lyke champyon gan enhaſte towardes dragon beaſt ryght great mōſtruous foule horrible deadly venimous armed ſcales large thicke breath perillous wicke eayre peſtylence venim ſuch vyolence full deadly eke mortall throte iſſued al flawme fyre fournes mouthe lyke leuen downe ſouth eaſt wont tempeſt ſmite right ſo dragon ſothely wite mouth flawme blaſed wherof iaſon lytell firſt amaſed hert dreadfull thynge whā remembred ringe feare dread layd aſyde gone ringe ſet ſtone ful ryche noble right vertuous whych teacheth great yſydorus mine auctour alſo finde moſt comenly cometh ynde muſt kept chaſte wonder cleane colour ſurmounteth euery grene whoſe vertue venym deſtroye withſtand may anoye dragon ſerpent adder ſnake ſpecyally ſo betake yholden oppoſyte worme euen agayn ſyte without abode ſothe may cheſe venym force muſt leſe ſtronge vyolent rage ſtone doth ful great damage whan hath vertue blyue peces ſmale gynneth ryue ſelfe abydeth whole whyle land called cecyle worme yt bufo beareth ye name men malice make tame venym vtterly expreſſe take quil mine auctour beareth witneſſe whā wyll worke large ende ſtone ſet line right agayne wormes heade holden tyll deade ſothly vertue nature venim laſt may endure preſence ryche ſtone finde bufo ryght anone myght therof bruſteth euē twain onely kynde mā may reſtrayne goddeſſe called nature whych next lorde al thyng cure hath vertue gyue herbe gras ſtone whych man knoweth ſelfe alone cauſes hyd cloſed hande wyt man vnderſtande openly myght workyng ſo iaſon vertue rynge ſton yt might hī moſt auaūce hath dragon brought vttraunce fonde maner reſyſtence hym wythſtand force diffence neyther venym none ſtryfe wherfore hath beraft lyfe manly wiſe fielde outrayed iaſon full glad well apayed hath wt ſword ſpēt many ſtroke layde hym men newe oke bryght ſkales ſo hard dure well vnneth ne might endure hym dyſmembre ſmite head anone ſtede ſede gan tethe head arace right forth ſelfe place gan ſowe right men corne vpon land eared aforne whych fede ſprāge wonder grayn bright armed knyghtes ſtanding ye playn anone wt ſharpe ſwerdes groūde eueriche gan hurt wounde tyll eche felowe hath cruelly yſlawe theyr fate fynal lawe none theim ſhuld vyctorye death reioyce memorye yfeare thus haue made ende iaſon gan wende vnto ram dylygence fonde power defence maner ſtryfe rebellyowne mightely ram draweth downe ſet hand vpon eueryche horne ſlewe firſt hath ſhorne fleſe golde ſo paſſyng ryche world ther treaſour lich maketh delay take boote haſt may roweth forthe yle hercules meane whyle vpon bryncke many mo abode iaſon till ydo euerychone finde blyue onely ioye aryue gan thanke theyr goddes gracyouſly hath yfall fleſe hath ſo knyghtlye wōne ſhone cleare ſomer ſonne brought hym vnto lōde feares abydyng ſtronde whan apollo dayes arke ye weſt almoſt yronne marke faſt gan downward drawen declyne wawes full watry gan ſhine yet paſſed occian iaſon come many manly man coferes preſence kinge acheued euery thynge longeth conqueſt ram oetes ſoone euer cam make hym chere outward hath hī pained albe herte ſothely fayned full ſory withouten dread exployte happye ſpede iaſon fleſe hathe wonne lyke ſothe feyners koune theim lyſt craftely compace ſhewe outward faythful meanyng face albe venym cloſed hole within meaning maner ſyn ryght ſo kyng wyth loke forhead clere made vnto iaſon outward right good chere gan hym ſpeake wordes fewe frendly head many ſygnes ſhewe though conqueſt hole euery dele poīt point like wonder well full glad ſo fortuned vnto ende hath ſo contuned ioyeth ſpeche countenaunce fortune lyſt ſo far forthe auaunce paleys gan fayre conueye daye daye ful rychely feſteye albe nothing done herte le felt full great ſmerte treaſour deſpoyled ſo hath ryche fleſe forgo domage confuſyon thus great dyuyſyon atwirt chere meanyng thoughte oft fareth yt dewlye ſought many man meanyng falſe double calme couer ſo trouble hyghe malyce hyd deſyre rake falſly wycked couert fire ful hote brennynge inwarde enuye wel hym cowd theim eſpye knewe theyr meanynge falſe fraudelēt ala ful many innocent deceiued wote meane namely ſuche trouthe wene euery cheare men theim make innocence beſt take wyſe thynke well ryght ſo certayne iaſon euery dell hath take gre ye kyng hath wrought aduertyng ye grutchyng thoughte doubtles tho ſat king full ſore ram hath loſt euermore hath vtterly yſayne thoughe ſtill grutche therin gayne fynally neceſſety tyme might none playnly ſawe may cheſe algate fleſe muſt leſe whether lyef lothe fayneth chere though wer wroth onely gentilneſſe ſigne outward grutching doth expreſſe daye daye verye curteſye cheareth iaſon companye whych tyme aboute enuirowne euery partye regyowne people came ſtaren gaſe vpon ram maſe loke wonder deme thē lyſt whoſe dome lytell tryſt oft varie tourne fro wyſely taketh hede therto comon people chaungeth phane day wexe morow wane doth mone ſo flaſkeſable truſteth thē ſhall finde thē full vnſtable ſome glad iaſon ſped ſo wel ſome ſory lyke neuer adell ſayd wōder myght agayne dragon bulles fyght agaynſt force marte yle alyue might aſtert ſayde perauenture craft wrought dyſcomfeture charme ſome ſorcerye thus eche theyr fanteſye gan deme hym longe daye laſt bout makyng delay ful glad lyght medea downe deſcēdeth chambre outwardly pretendethe sadnes chere ſhe nothīg ne knewe nought could men cōceiue hew ſecret meaning ſo hath ſhe womanly demened eke ſo prudently ſhe auoyded diſcreſcion fanteſye ſuſpection man coude working deme nothyng well ſhuld ſeme porte cheare cauſe whi ſo proceſſe drewe pryuely towarde iaſon ſhe lere ſecretly ſhe bad ere wyſe ne leue chambre come eue matter hadden treat ſhal knowe leiſur whē mete ſo anone entred night sole hym ſelfe without torche lyght medea hath waye take ſhe abode ſleples ſake wonder deuoutly deſyryng geſſe treate ſome holyneſſe touching matter contemplacion ſhe ſmitte ſuch deuocion freſhe venus holde memorye alone oratorye openly ypocrytes praye dyuers angel ioyning waye people commended haue night ſo diſpended vayne glorye none laude ſelfe thynkyng fraude secretly ilke twayn alone without light eyther ſonne mone long nyght haue led wythout reſt thought beſte ſpeake ſlepe till pryme caſt leſe tho time thus nyght together diſpende dull comprehende obſeruaunces ſuch relygyous prolyx workyng compēdyous demeth ſelfe ye get well ye wote euery faculte ſo hath knowyng experyence men wyll hym rather gyue credence wherfore ſaye ye wyſe whych ſo rude man deme thyng namely paſſeth knowing alſo wyt fordulled myne imagynatyfe deme practike ſpeculatyfe wherfore paſſe let ouer ſlide forthe thynke ye liſt abide playnly tell iaſon medee whych accorded aſſented ſhe ſhould grece wēde goeth ſhortly ende vnwyſt father euery wyght saue alone hath trouth plyght trewe well wo vnto laſt mo ¶how iaſon conqueſt medea felowſhyppe retourned agayne theſalye cap vii whan iaſon iournee full rychely lyke vnto degree refreſhed colchos kynge withall might lykynge moneth paſſed gone grekes aſſented one purpoſed hath ſhortly yf might medea ſtele away nyght takyng wt hym great treaſour ye rych fleſe ful aſſent alſo hercules ¶but medea thou haſteſt faſt thou ſlawe wyſely caſt ſhuld befall yu thy iourney toke miſchiefe forſoke falſe eke vnkinde othes wherof fynde thou eue morowe thy fatall chaunce thy pyteous ſorowe wepteſt gan thy ſelfe rende tyll death made wofull ende vaine maken reherſayle wote nothynge howe might auaile howe iaſon vnkynde none receyued hath penam tallionis goddes diſnaturelneſſe miſchiefe wretchedneſſe made eke ende though cruell hate felle mar loo mortall fate theſe twayne made ende ſo ſuppoſe lyke writeth guydo gynnynge vertuous ende foloweth full contagious ala yf hadde taken hede aforne miſchiefe forlorne wyll afore miſchiefe ſe may eſchewe haue aduerſitie ende platly deuyne euen lyke right medicyne auayleth whan ſycke dead may helpe ſtomake head lectuarye emplayſtre pocyon receite confection herbe ſtone lech knowe whan corp layde earth alowe ¶or whan beaſt tourned careine myne auctour ſayth veyne recure ſeken halowe ere leyne ſalowe veryly fantaſye helpeth doth remedy thynge perfourmed due date vertue hath thā whā cometh late right ſo caſe veryly ſemblable worldly truſt falſe full mutable caſte peryll tyll falle ſtede ſugre ofte taſteth galle blended luſte tho preſent future ſlouthe necligent theim ne lyſte afore miſchiefe caſte tyll ſnare englued faſte prouyde graceles full indiſcrete wilfully richeles caſte peryll tyde ſewe luſt reaſon goeth aſide befell whylom two medea iaſon alſo ¶but ſo euer iaſon fynde playnly harme alone ſhe great damage fynall ſmerte lacke wyſedome ſhe ne wolde aduerte ſhuld fall whā ſhe iourney toke father folyly forſoke ſyth ſhe wrought wylfulneſſe without counſayle auyſeneſſe lyſt harmes bewayle lyte nought myght auayle let alone complainyng damage well wote touchynge paſſage take good plyte mone haſtyneſſe ſhe began ſoone cheſynge houre fortunat ſhe alone frendes deſolate colchos forſoke ſhyp gon haſte byddynge iaſon hercules companye comyn theſalye without tarying forthwith worde yentred ben within ſhyppes borde cauſe wynde good euery thyng tho luſte ſtode thus aſſented ſtale awaye nyght treaſure catche myght ladde plente vitayle forthe anone began ſayle many coaſt many ſondry yle towardes grece meane medea glad good chere iaſon ſyttynge yfeare hercules gentylneſſe comforte buſyneſſe al faynyngly maner ſake theſe louers full queynte make tyll haue hooly pleaſaunce luſt fulfylled vttreth varyance iaſon preued vtterly hath forſaken full vnkyndly medea paine ſorowe wo guydo ne wryte wordes mo maketh none mencion bycauſe trowe myne opynyon ſorowes ende euery deale reherſed full openly weale methamorphoſeos writē full plaine naſo recordeth certayne death heuyneſſe percell eke vnkyndneſſe iaſon telleth playnly howe medea hath ſonnes ſlowe lyke father viſage telleth eke put moſt rage falſly hym excuſe loued called ceruſe eke piſtelles ſo taketh hede deadly ſorowe may beholde rede howe ſhe trouth aboughte ſore medea ye gete boke auenture wyll nowe buſy cure hooly tourne ſtile iaſon werre made lamedon like guydo openly deſcribed grece aryued firſt whan iaſon hercules alſo ylonded many mo within land reygne theſalye kyng pelleus chiualrye caſte hym playnly wyll fayle mete neuewe ariuayle whan mette countenance chere made outwarde hoole entere ſoueraygne gladneſſe knighthode highe proweſſe renowne manlyhede expleyte good ſpede fortune encreaſe name hath cauſed ſo noble fame colchos honour repayre albe chere vtterly contraire entent euer came agayne face hole playne welcomed hym al againſt herte full ſore aſtoned euer aſterte auentures colchos peryllous retourned ſo victorious couertly treaſon hyde delaye gan ſette aſyde iaſon chere full benyng heritage fyrſte gan reſygne septre crowne kingdome ye leſte perfourme ſumme beheſte like aſſured bonde iaſon toke honde gan vncle full lowe manere firſt thanke herte entere ¶and ful knightly gan pray goodly wolde ſaye mattere fret herte ſore daye daye encreaſyng euer beſechyng hym graunt hym audience touchyng wronge vyolence done vnto hym whan harme ne ment troye lande colchos wente ſaye kynge troye towne within bondes region whan myne great aduerſitye winde wether fordryuen ſea v refreſhe lande dyd aryue purpoſe hym ſtryue reſt v wo lytell whyle forth anone go ſothe maner harme ne thought vnkyngly malyce ſought agaynſt v fynde occaſyon byddyng haſte voyde region notwithſtanding come peace lyke brother knoweth hercules vnto wyght doyng diſtreſſe wherfore praye hygh nobleſſe purpoſe condiſcende whiche platly fynall ende ſette full concluſyon hooly worke deſtruction lyke auowe whan thenſe went ſo ye goodly lyſte aſſent one ſtrongly ſpare maugre myght troye fare may fynde fauoure v refreſhe golde treaſure eke curteſye v ſtrength alſo cheualrye ¶and pelleus without abode anone matter vnderſtode aſſented herte wyll alſo voyage theim go worthy regyowne kynges duke lordes renowne accorded one ſaieth naye go theim helpe may iourney chiefe ſolicitour hercules worthy conquerour ¶and haſte retenewe make towarde spartos hath way take whiche yle grekes pertinent fully obeying commaundement whiche pollux caſtor eke alſo worthy kingꝭ mighty brothern two fynde tyme gouernours bare crowne like noble werreours brothern alſo vnto eleyne poetes lyketh fayne iupiter deyte vpon leda begat three beautie dyd excelle eleyne lyke bokes telle conceyued tyndarys yle vnto londe ioynyng cecyle therfore ſome fynde ſhe yle called tyndaris byrth lyſt endite forthe thyncke hercules wryte hath beſought theſe noble kingꝭ twain mighty hande buſy payne graunte wende troye warde ſhortly ende aſſente ſaye one nay power catche may againe tyme lyſt aſſygne hercules chere full beninge thanked behyght forth wente haſte might toward meſſene ſtronge mighty londe within whiche noble king fonde knightly man worthy thelamon lorde prynce region armes one manlyeſt lyue egall beſte whan knew hercules com ioye hath hym armes nome receyued maner thynge lyke ſat worthy kyng whan wiſte ſothly mente without anone dyd aſſente hym gone troyens greue hercules goodly toke leue hym enhaſteth theſalye agayne pelleus telleth hym certayne howe hath ſpedde beſechynge hym alſo haſte may letter ſende lordes call aſſemble worthy knyghtes thrughout lād yt nigh ferre suche knewe yt experte werre alſo counſayle ſage wyt yronne age force without experience whan manhode mente ſapience loketh well may double auayle longe haue vſed trauayle lyke playnly ſuppoſe may helpe moſte iourney diſpoſe vnto age experience wytte youth force hardineſſe ſytte whan one entent fully accorded worken aſſent quarell grounded vpon ryght thrugh helpe grace yt hath treble myght thē nede drede ſpere wt ſhelde knyghtly wyſe holde feilde knighthode fame glory armes conqueſt victory aſſured vpon multitude manhode ſo grace lyſte conclude ¶therfore let v auenge wrong firſt right make ſelfe ſtronge efte force manly ſhewe knyghtes choſe taken fewe ſo auoyde encombraunce numbre ſo ſhall foe beſte encombre hercules hath ſayde kyng pelleus tho right well apayde thought counſaile righte good hercules without abode great haſte meine gon prouince called pilon whiche duke noble fame fynde neſtor name full renowmed ſtronge chiualrye eke kinred allye hercules ſame bloud whan plainly vnderſtode purpoſe hole cauſe coming graunted hym without taryinge go hym ſelfe hym voiage worthy baronage ready agayne certayne daye hercules faſte euer maye repaired ayen theſalye gathered holy nauye lordes full redy apparayled well enarmed rychely vitayled ¶and pelleus hath taken fyrſte ſea euery lorde lyke degree yſhypped ready gon hercules alſo iaſon beheſtes manly fulfyll towardes troye citie ſpylle ſothly fynde abyde vpon wynde ¶nowe iaſon hercules prynces grece aſſembled aduenge ye vncurteſy done theim lamedon expedicion towardes colchos cap viii vvhan ſote ſtormes apryll vnto roote full lowe gan deſtille luſtye licour many holſome ſhoure reyſe vertue hyghe vpon floure phebus aſcendyng ſphere breſt ſmote beames cleare ram full colerike halowynge veer equinoctiall whan mayes kalendes entren ſothe zephirus ſwete breath ſmothe tendre braūches enſpireth doth ſpryng euery buſhe freſhe bloſomynge hylle water reuolued ſnowes whyte yt phebus hath diſſolued bawme vapoureth vp lofte eyre herbes ſofte rote vertue colde wynter hydde hath full myght force ykydde erth herbe euery tree shade braunches humiditee arayſed ſonnes heate moyſter raynes ſwete whan ſiluer welles ſheden ſtremes ryuers gylte ſonne beames newe greene againe largeſſe ſhad vpon euery playne nightingale wodde ronge full amorouſly welcome ſonge luſty ſeaſon freſhe deſyrous namely hertes whiche ben amorous whan ſea calme blaundiſhinge fro trouble wynde wawy boylynge tempeſt ſure eſcape ſame ſeaſon grekes forth ſhape towardes troye erles duke kynges ſhyppes ſtuffed wt maner thynges werre myght moſt auayle ryght anone began ſayle whan redy without abode eche ſhyppe water rode whan winde luſt gan blowe ioye ſe go rowe whiche made thē haſt ſpeden waie ſhort tyme comen ben troy hauen called symeonte whan phebus fer vnder oriſente weſtred men myght hym ſe grekes byn paſt peryll ſea caſt ancrees thynking beſt ſhippes ſame night reſte ye morowe whan larke ſonge worthi grekes ſo māly ſo ſtrōge began lande haſte myghte troye grounde tentes pighte afore towne great dylygence ne founde maner reſyſtence whyle ſette good awayte euery ſyde leſte deceyte tyll houre ſonne bryght morowe ſhade rody lyghte amyd fielde vpon euery tente whiche tyme one aſſente grekes aſſembled euerychone byddyng kynge anone iaſon fyrſt hercules many worthy beyng preſe ben tente pelleus ycome whā theſe lordes grece al ſome aſſembled place met eche degree ſet pelleus whan al whiſt ſtyll right thus began ye ſentence wyll ¶o noble worthy hye eſtate lowe whoſe knightly fame throughout ye worlde yknow reported fer ſhineth ſonne grekes yet neuer thynge begonne ne victorye ende ye lawrer ſo fer men may wende crowned ben thei toke hād suche thier happe ſe lande ¶wherforeye lordꝭ moſt worthi renowne ye remembre kyng lamedowne wronge yt vpon wrought whan harme none ne thought muſt quit ſhortly ende come ſtroie ſhende wherfore anone haſte may lette v ſet without delaye fyrſt rede taken hede thre thynges moſt helpyng nede ¶firſt aduyſe good diſcretion defence good ſaluacion prudently wardes make none oures miſchiefe take ylke daye lacke prouidence ſeconde diligence might hole entention labour full diſtruction come foe ſelues glory ¶and thirde may victorye inioye platly laſte ouer ye maye afore well caſte knighthode hardineſſe may vanquiſhe ſhal ſo hye richeſſe conquere poſſeſſyowne knowen troye towne plentie ſhalbe founde golde treſour doth paſſingly habounde ſhyppes ſothly wene receiue ne ſhall mow ſuſteine habundaunce yonder within ſo citie wyn god v graunte ſo wyll ¶and alſo faſte kynge ſtyll noble knight ſtronge hercules preſence worthy preſe said counſaile highely cōmende wyſe begynnynge preyſed ende effecte purpoſe brynge counſayle mornynge tofore diſcured byn daye v arme haſte maye fielde payne deuyde mayne twayne tone ſhall kyng thelamowne gouernour hye renowne kyng pelleus ſhall haue gouernaunce wiſely theim ſaue ſelfe iaſon brother shall ſecretely go vnder citie ſonne ſhynes buſhaile thicke vynes ſhall v hyde kepe v full koye lamedon kyng troye anone may may eſpye grekes cheualrye citie yſſue anone v fyght venge hym fone whan cometh ſhippes warde neſtor duke ſhall firſt warde mete hym caſtor ſhall alſo whan ſeeth time knightly haue ado helpe neſtor nede thirde warde pelleus ſhall lede whyles ye thus occupye iaſon ſhall v faſte hye vnto citie vnwiſt echone doubte ſhall wyn anone doth counſayle auayle trouth ye may fayle conquere citie yonde tofore ſome ye gete ¶and accord wt al ſtrēgth might enarme theim ſtele yt ſhone full bryght againe ſonne morowe whan riſeth wrought hercules deuiſeth ¶of battaile betwixt grecian troians wherin troyans diſcomfeted kinge ſlayne citie taken raſed deſtroyed ca ix kyng lamedon whan herde tell cōming liſt longer dwel went many noble knighte flouryng youth deſyrous fyght tho mighten armes beare coude ſhote handell durſte ſpere ¶and whan aſſēbled fielde eueryche armes depeint vpon ſhilde brouded bete vpon coote armure lamedon buſy cure set ordre wardes maketh fielde forth waye taketh towarde grekes lyne right fully purpoſynge abide fight ware thē behynde aduerteth caſteth mynde great ſleyght treachery ſhape coude eſpye forthe wente wardes ſet grekes anone hath met herte bolde aſtoned duke neſtor firſt ſturdy wall whoſe manhod neuer foundē lacke full knightly vpon horſe backe herte men knightes eke gan preſe many worthy greke lamedon ſturdely mete whiche tyme felte full vnſwete frounter many manly man ſharpe ſperes firſt together ran eft ſwordes ſharpe kene ygroūde thilke daye geuen many wounde met thus euery ſyde thrugh plate maile woundes bledde wide baſenettes riue ye crowne noyſe ſtrokes eyre gan ſowne blode tho ſhad new grene ſoyle chaunged hath hewe dyed playnly red vpon whiche full many man lay dead many worthy loſt lyfe certainly mortall ſtryfe grekes diſcomfyted echone ne caſtor ſocoured anone folke troy ſo manly haue bore many knight grekes ylore caſtor entreth bataile knightes ſo ſore aſſayle worthy troyans yt ſpere ſhielde grekes agayne recouered haue fielde many one lieth ſlayne vpon grene thrugh girt body wt ſharpe ſperes kene troye mortall ſtoure driue backe tyll came ſocour haſt worthy lamedowne whiche entred like wodde lyowne made waye vpon euery ſyde made ſwerde glyde deth ſo manly hym bare well vnneth none dare abyde ſtroke rydynge vp downe made waye enuirowne renges hath foen ſoughte dai ī armes meruailes hath wroute manhod worthines grekes hath brought ſuche diſtreſſe ſwerde flyen death marciles ſo many ſleeth ſlaughter grekes wer confuſe tyll pelleus came reſcuſe irous wood fall rage thought wold ye great pompe aſwage troye ſo dyd anone vnhorſeth many one felly ſlough ſtode aforne many harueys hath yt daye torne made ſheldes ryue ſonder beholde wondre til lamedon people ſawe go backe pelleus brought ſo wracke wherof herte felte full great payne beſeching efte repaire againe kyth might like men endure ſo fielde made recure tyll duke neſtor knewe lamedowne amid fielde kynge troye towne right anone without abode agaynſt hym full great pace rode whan kyng firſt eſpye hye diſpite rancour enuye knightly wyſe gan tourne againe nothynge agaſt hye diſdayne yrons herte enbolned pride horſe fyerſly ſmytyng ſyde ye pricke ran red bloud forth neſtor like wood rode anone ſpere brake full knightly kept horſe backe full delyuerly againe quite ſpeare full ſharpe whette byte thrugh ſheld breſt gaue ſuch woūde fro hors felde hī groūd whiche fall kyng nothyng ferde vpriſe ayene knightly drewe ſwerd angre fret hym herte rote vnhorſed fyghte muſte fote wherof partyfull confuſe tyll one cedar came reſcuſe made knight ye ſelfe ſame yere yonge freſhe luſty noble chere syttyng tyme noble ſtede whan gan take hede ſaw kyng foote miſchiefe fight gan forth pryke haſt might toward neſtor ſpere hytte ſadell made flytte downe ground afore kyng lamedon anone full lyke champion recured vp hymſelfe defendeth many ſtroke eche ſpendeth ſharpe ſwerdrs kene byte eueriche gan foyne ſmyte tyll lamedon diſpyteous chere face raſed viſer ſtrype one ſinet ryche cercle baſenet large perle goynge enuyrowne creſte fyerſly beate downe whyles neſtor thus afore hym ſtode face depeint bloud certainely ſoth conclude grekes great multitude reſcued lamedowne ſlayne faſte bore downe vnto earth amonge horſe feete caſtor thought ne wolde lete helpe behelde yfeare yrouſly toke mighty ſpere cedar ſpake late gan ryde pricke deadly hate came toke doubtles troyan knight called segnerides coſyn cedar whan hath ſene courſer rode anone bytwene ſpere ſmote caſtor ſo ſtroke broken two caſtor withouten areſte hath ſpere amyddes breſt segnerides gyue mortall wounde lykely neuer ſounde wherfore cedar caught hath ſuche enuye anone fell melancolye diſpyte boylynge herte segnerides beholde ſo ſmerte maugre grutcheth amiddes ye fielde myght caſtor toke ſhelde vyſer rancour rage wounded hym amyddes vyſage eke horſe fro hym alſo caughte ſquier manfully raught certainely ſtode ſuche diſioynt worthy caſtor poynt haue taken troye tho foote muſt haue go ne pollux many manly knyght mo vii hundred ſtele armed bryght rather come caſtor reſcue whiche ſo ſore gan ſewe maugre caſtor fond force reſte enemy hōd horſe reſtored hym agayne pollux certayne anger feruent ire agayne troians rancoure ſet fyre al one vpon theim ſet mode fortune met troian knight called eliatus armes yonge freſhe deſyrous wonder ſemely yet tendre age kinges ſonne alſo great cartage neuewe eke vnto king lamedon pollux hath like fierſe lyon without compaſſion pytye mercye within renges ſlayne ful cruelly lamedon whan gan take hede inwarde dole felt herte blede whan hym ſawe point vpon deathe full pyteouſly yelden vp breathe vpon playne lay beforne whiche anone made ſowne horne time came riche araye seuen knigh tin haſte may vpon deathe auenged merciles theyr great crueltye grekes haue confoūded lyeth one dead another woūded might hold tacke mortally made theim go abacke gan tourne theyr confuſion fynally daye wyth lamedon triumphe fielde ygone saue ala towne anone vnto king came meſſengere hath tolde wt ful piteous cheare grekes haue citye take ¶then ſe wo tho make would haue made piteus herte bliue dole ſundre riue ſore gan within ſelfe mourne wiſt partye may tourne weuer abiding longe afore ſawe mighty grekes ſtronge citie another hooſt behinde almoſte wo went minde ſodeynly backward behelde toward citye ſawe come felde firſt hercules iaſon theyr ſleyght wonnen ye towne haſt cruell hercules mighty giaunt force pereles lyke lyon wood diſpiteous tygre ramage furyous gan newe theim troye aſſayle ſworde perce plate mayle laboure full mate feynt longe fight werineſſe atteynt came luſty freſhe grene force might ſuſtene rode among theim yonder cruell wiſe ſeuered theim ſonder put theim hooly high miſchaunce rule gouernaunce kinge oppreſſed al dole wardes deſtytute ſole miſchiefe left infortunate comforte fully diſconſolate hercules full diſpiteous loke ſharpe ſpores ſtede felly toke cruelly rode forthe lamedowne earth fierſly bare downe vpon haſt might downe horſe ſodeinly alighte mightely rent baſenet ſwerd ſharpe grounde whet smote head grace caſt forth ſelfe place amonge horſe cruel violence without pytye reuerence arage raught horſe agayne like lion renning playne bare ſlough ſo cā weye many troyan yt time made deye like ſhepe forſkatered wide deſtitute gouernour guide ne reade ſhortly conclude grekes double multitude gan theim enchaſe death ful blyue wel vnneth left one alyue felde haue ben day victours triumphe like conquerours citye toke waye rende adowne wall ſparre rafter treaſour rich towne toke anone theyr poſſeſſyowne euer grutche lefe lothe found plainly wt gothe temple great violēce goddes doyng reuerence ſpoyle without dread feare vnto ſhippe euery thing beare mercyles croked olde lame theyr ſwerdes made cruelly tame childrē ſoukyng theyr mother breſte kill ſley withouten areſt yong maydens wepyng diſtreſſe full gentyl borne great ſemelyneſſe theym led may excuſe theyr freſhe beaute falſly miſuſe waſte bren conſumen roūde aboute brake adowne ye wall exyone kinges doughter dere ſo paſſingly entere life meane lamedon meke bening condicion hercules hath anone take dreadful pyteouſly gan quake delyuered vnto thelamowne entred firſt towne gift receyued hath gree bycauſe ſhe ſurmounting beautee treated would like kinges doughter ſhuld ſyth hath wonne victorye worſhip owne glorye hauing regarde highe degree ſhuld rather knightly honeſtee knighthode wedded therfore sith ſhe blode ſo gentill bore falſe luſt agayne goodlihead vſed beautye womanhaede diſhoneſtly ſuch ſinfull wiſe royall blode lyke high empryſe doctrine nature right like nurture gentil knight conſydered fyrſt birth kinrede grene youth eke maydenheade good ſo fayre ſo womanly therto kinges doughter byrth ſhe alſo haue wed coulde haue ſhame thelamō ſothe thou blame errour thy gouernaunce kindled ful highe vengeaunce hote ſparke enuye ye world ye fire gan multeplye like quenche hete hatred olde bren lete newe flawme ſo taketh hede ſmoke dread ſtorye hereafter ſhall knowe whā towne brēt brought ſo low bothe toure wall wt ye ſoyle made playn nothing ſtode might ſein vtterly grekes theym oppreſſe makyng waſte like wyldernes ¶for good treaſour ryches infynyte many iewell full pleaſing delyte theyr ſhippes towne lede ſhorte tyme homeward ſpede treaſour ſtuffed habūdaūce good ſawe wether ſtode wynd alſo theyr luſt gā ſaile thē home lad yong exione many mayde mo troye grece go ſayling forth within litell ſpace eſcaped fro ſea grace vnto land aryued merely whoſe commyng grekes vtterly ioyfull theyr good ſpede ſpecially guido reade theyr ſhyppes wt golde treaſour lade wherof herte wexe wonder glade outward ſo well thē borne ouerthrowe haue ſo fewe ylorne theyr meyne thanke theyr goddes al grace theym fall wt ye treaſour yt haue home brought full many pore made vp nought throughout yt lād ſuch habūdaūce much good ſo great ſuffiſaunce wight among theim nede many day bleſſedfull lyfe lede yeare yeare reuoluciowne theyr manhod theyr high renowne theyr honour ran round world theim toffende many lāde hath doubte theyr knighthod ſo wyſe vntill ſtorye laſt agayne deuiſe matter ferther procede fauour goodlyhead wil reſt lytel ſpace thā vpborne wt ſupporte grace taccompliſhe vndertoke ende firſt boke make quakyng hand dreade onely feare ſhall reade leſt ye ala haſty mocion ne haue compaſſyon pytye routhe vpon rudeneſſe lowly beſechyng gentilceſſe mercye onely nigh ferre ye finde fayle erre correcte ye flyt grace hooly commit ¶the tranſlatour complaineth miſfortune troians loſſe theyr city liuely deſcribyng tykle eſtate fortune gouernaunce beginning ſame chapyter ſecound boke perſewing matter ſayd hiſtorye ca x enuious ordre fortunat meninge worldly thynge falſe flikerynge nil ſuffer v preſent life lyue reſte without werre ſtryfe ſhe blinde fikel vnſtable courſe falſe ful mutable ſitteth higheſt ſhe cā downe encline whē leaſt weneth bring hym ruine awaytes gladly ben ſodayne face parted twayne shewe moſt hole whā ſhe leſt tryſt well deceytes wiſt engine trappes knewe courte euery daye newe ſothe well affirme dare mortall man may life beware ſhe vneuen peyſing balaunce counterfete fayned countenaunce lo • ing playn cheare flatterye vnwarely blere mannes eye begile ſothe face blandiſhing ſmothe ſhe hath frō high degre made low full falſly ſmile make mowe yet ſomewhyle moſt varyaunt hewe vnto ſome pretendeth trewe ſhe whylom ſome fauorable ſome falſe like deceiuable reiſe one bring another downe falſe lady tranſmutacyowne ſome ſhe giueth renowne victorye doth theym floure honoure glorie ſome ſhe appayre falſe fame giltles perde put man blame ſome ſhe goodly beninge diſdeyne ſhe alſo malygne agayne make hym lowte lowe frō ſee ſhe great kinges throwe theim auayle high toures ſhe plonge worthy emperours hyll hye proſperetye vaile like aduerſytye ryche empriſhe rancoure dyſdayne eft pore ſhe enhaūce agayne falſe goddeſſe eyen blinde set one afore another goeth behinde doth one renne maketh another halte one ſhe high rich exalte plonge pouertye man may haue ſecurytye ſome ſuger hony ſhe diſtilleth ſome ſhe bottel fylleth bytter gall mirre aloe thus lady wilfull rechles ſhe froward peruers hath ſeller drinkes ful diuers ſhe ſome fraude falla miniſtreth piment bawme ypocras ſodeynly ſoote paſt cuſtome giue caſt conclude falſly fine bytter eyſell egre wine corroſynes fret perce depe narcotikes cauſe men ſlepe thus ſhe theim aproche ſwete bitter broche thus reygne quene varyaunce whoſe ioye alwayes fineth miſchaunce truſteth ſhe ouercaſt deceyue playnly laſt eſtate ſoeuer double lady mutabilitye se example king lamedon ſhe hath brought confuſion litel cauſe thing nought crueltye hath deare abought wherfore reade euery man take hede gin quarell nede litell fyre vnder aſhes reke may kindled breake ſuch flawme men may apeaſe beſt ſuffer moſte ſhall haue eaſe therfore ye kynges lordes euerychone make myrroure lamedone well ware violence vnto ſtraungers none offence whan come fer region ne ſuffer theim none oppreſſion within bondes haue wrong owne though ye ſtrong mightye eke among liege another daye perauntre may befall ye ful lytell thynke ſodeyne caſe thus may ye aquyt ythanked another place auenture ye may fayle grace therfore ye may ſuch eſpye theym good cheyre curteſye prudently conſyder witt lorde gentilneſſe ſyt euery ſtraunger goodly haue nothing may honour ſaue refreſhe frely diſporte may good reporte whoſe cōtrary hath much wo wrought afore time ſo well ſought firſt troye thus vtterly deſtroyed people ſorowe wo acloyed lad exyle farre theyr cytye lyuing thraldome captiuitye exyone ye haue herde tell led grece thelamon dwell whō guido cā teache take ſo great vengeaunce wreche eyther parte trouthe heare great routhe boke ye may hereafter rede ceryouſly ye liſt take hede gladly aye reuoluſyon fatall thing diſpoſicion enuyous alway meynt wo world ſo go truely may aduert thought value thyng nought mortall cauſes werres firſt begonne strife debate vnderneth ſonne meued firſt ſmall occaſyon cauſed great confuſyon man harmes halfe endite cauſe deare inough mite eche one redy deſtroye man litel ſtryue brother blode vnkynde greatly drede ala ne take better hede olde troye newe ſmal encheſō trouth knew fynally brought deſtruction olde bokes make mencion many worthy many noble knight slayne felde dureſſe fight kynges prynces ſiege ben deade whā attropos lyſt breake theyr liues threde tel miſchiefe wo want connyng fele alſo pen quake tremble hand lyſt lorde dradde ſea lande whoſe worthines thrugh ye world doth ſprede rude makyng ſhal beholde reade whych colour full naked bare mercye ſpare diſdayne liſt haue pytye feare tremble ſhuld ſe ¶but onely mercye yt doth hert embraſe byd preſume fully grace seyng hym moſt vertuous good mercye annexed vnto royall blode prince longeth nigh ferre aye fore ryght pytye preferre ſupport high nobleſſe ayene ſtyle dreſſe wryte forth ſtorye newe troye ordre ſeryouſly mine auctour latyn guydo wryt praying ye reader wher wordes miſſit cauſyng metre halte lame correct ſaue blame let hym wayte haue curyoſytye sith rime englyſhe hath ſkerſytye ſo dull certayne ne guido enſewe clerke curyous man whych latyn hath rethoryke set ſo wordes cā lyke ſewe ſtyle tranſlation worde worde like conſtruction maner gramariens like ſtile rethoriciens toke ſtorye tranſlate clio came late ſuch craft hath great experience leue wordes folowe ſētence trouthe metre ſet alſo aſyde arte tho guide reduce whan went wrong taking ſmall hede eyther ſhort long trouth lette curioſite making metre purpoſyng much varye dyuers contrarye vnto guydo diſcordaunce conforme fully ſubſtaunce onely meanyng conclude one albe ne waye gone ſewe floures eloquence peyntyng haue none excellence ſundry hewes noble freſhe gay ryche coloures byggen ne may muſt procede ſable blacke ennuyng ye fynde lacke axe mercy fro twyn fauour nowe begyn haſte ſtile forth right directe erre pray correct ſame tyme whē troye towne deſtroyed yt king lomedowne alſo ſlayne crueltye hercules tofore cytye ſonne ſtorye telleth v heyre ycalled priamus wonder manly diſcrete eke prudent time troye abſente ſo father loſt hath ſo lyfe tyme hecuba wyfe ſonnes aboute caſtell laye knightes get may hath theym mightely werreyed father falſly diſobeied vnto hym rebell wonder longe albe priam ſautes huge ſtronge theim aſſayled oft many ſyth ſtrength like knight kyth get armes worſhip honour theim daunt like conquerour caſt fully departe day day life gan ieoparte tofore walles preue mighte many baron many worthy knight flowing yet luſty bloude age flouryng knighthode aſſautes ſuch maner ſtrife firſt auenture life herte men lyſt behind dread death ſothly find afore caſtell hygh thyck ywalled wife hecuba called pryam ful worthy degre fiue ſonnes yonge doughters thre ¶of whych eldeſt hector called alſo fer phebus compaſe naturall daye cercle goeth fer hym withouten doubte reported renowne name worthyneſſe noble fame like bokes ſpecifye roote ſtocke chiualrye knighthod ſoueraygne floure ſours well worſhip honoure manhode dare well expreſſe patron myrrour high proweſſe ginning grounde yfeare wonder benynge lowely cheare diſcrete alſo prudent vertuous dedes actes merueilous remembred ben ſo long gone alone excelled euerychone olde auctours reade ye may finde knighthod yet makē mynde ¶the next brother called parys nature gaue deuys ſhape fourme beautye ſemelyneſſe recorde excellent fayrneſſe time withouten dread ferre paſſed reade eke full manly knight moſt vſed ſo ſhuld fight hand beare mighty bowe ſuch archer man coud knowe none might foūd ſeke fer nere ſhoting might hardely pere founde whan alexſandre called alſo ¶the third ſonne hight deiphobus worthy knight chiualrous armes ful great renowne man high diſcreſciowne wife coūſail min auctour ſayeth thus ¶the fourth brother called helenus sad diſcrete highe prudence alſo man great ſcyence renommed therwith ſpecyall al artes called lyberal theym full experte ryght ¶the fyfth ſonne worthy knyght freſhe luſty yongeſt theim ſayeth guido troylus men call manly man valyaunt battayle fearſely hote fomen aſſayle one beſt time yfounde called hector ſecound manhode throughout troye booke within werre ful oft vpon toke knighthode many high empryſe ſtorye lyke ſhall deuyſe ¶and boke like wryte vergile poete olde wt ſoueraintye ſtyle king pryam alſo hecuba ſonnes two recorde vergelius one named pollidorus priamus grene youthe ye cominge grekes kouth troyewarde haſte anone golde treaſour many ryche ſtone hath ſent forthe beſyde vnto kinge ful great truſt haue kepyng till tyme ſawe concluſyowne ſhuld befall towne eke fine werres ſhoulden take vpon theym grekes tho make thilke kyng falſe couetyſe treaſour ye haue herde deuyſe whan ſawe fortune varyaunce toward pryam vnhappy chaunce lyke tyraunt murderer alſo childes throte made cutte two full crueltye made men burye priuelye man might treaſon vnderſtond beſyde ſea depe vnder ſtrond ¶the ſonne alſo reade vergile called fayre ganimede iupiter hath foreſt hente vpon daye huntinge wente bare vp aboue ſterres clere heauens made butlere eternally hym wonnen ſtede hebe owne daughter dere ¶the fyrſt doughter kyng pryamus hoote creuſa ſayeth vergilius eneydos ſothely ſhe wedded vnto eneas eke ſtorye ſayeth enee wonderfull natyuytye father fynde doubtles tyme called anchyſes hym begat venus goddeſſe ſuch fayrneſſe wyght could neuer yet ſe man paſſyng beautye ſtorye touchyng workyng shall declare many wonder thyng ſo great loo vergyle hath giue eneydos booke worſhyp enee compyled hath like ye may ſe knyghthood many ſtrong batayl hym acheued wan itayle full long time royall towne troy brought confuſiowne conqueſt yf ye lyſt take hede poete ye may ordre reade armes wrought al age comyng alſo cartage fro troywarde within litell al ye may behold great vergile ¶another doughter alſo founde kyng pryam birth ſecound called caſſandra ful great ſadneſſe maner diuinereſſe eche arte experience thynges future fully preſcience tell afore ſhall betide fame ſprang coſtes wide kept chaſte aye virginitye eke prayer honeſtye led life deuocion rite religyon pagyniſme vſed tho dayes obſeruaunces keping layes ¶the third doughter hight pollicene yongeſt ſtil mayde cleane kept ſelfe honeſt lawe vnto time pirrus hath ſlawe ſhape fortune neuer nature wrought beholde fayrer creature eke fynde noble kynge alſo hadde thirty ſonnes boke ſaith mo hardy armes noble founde called ſonnes naturall exceptinge neuer one worthy knyghtes manly men echone name ſo lyſte knowe ſhall fynde wryte vpon arowe ſtory eueryche begynnyng fyrſt eldeſt brother ¶and while pryam ſyege laye tofore caſtell gette may therabout hath many way ſought wofull tydynges vnto broughte grekes haue taken troye towne ſlayne father worthy lamedowne citie olde foundaciowne full piteouſly tourned vp ſo downe worthy lordes gentle men echone taken ſlayne ylefte one lyue grekes crueltie ruyne ala citie exion owne ſyſter dere lad exyle eyen cleare ¶wherfore kyng herte aſtoned ſo ſorowe niſt ſodayne wo gan hym ſo conſtrayne ſobbeth wepeth mortall payne thought herte wolde ſondre breſte hye diſtreſſe myghte haue reſte teares gan ſelfe deſtylle deye fynally wyll ¶and fortune ſo falſly varye drery herte gan bytterly warye ſhe hym ſo deceyuable inly cruell vnmercyable diſpyteous ſo ſterne face vengeable ſo deuoyde grace enuy raged thought hath hir worſt mali hī wrought felly ſhewed ſhe myght worlde neuer wight ſo wo ſuppoſe maner age reaken harmes damage whiche anone euer maye haſt chaungeth ryche araye tryſte heuy deadly face pale aſtoned mortall tale deſyre haue dead countenance enclined head lyfe lad clad blacke ſodaynly ſyege brake wolde tho lenger abyde folke anone gan ryde pyteouſly gan likwiſe wt morne toward troy attones efte returne ¶and whan hath cyty founde plaine ſoyle euen wt grounde hye walles whylom thicke longe ybeate downe made ſo ſtronge toures paleys pryncypall buildyng ſo excellent royall famous ryche great nobleſſe founde tourned wylderneſſe people ſlayne ſyſter ladde awaye wo ne wyſte ſaye conſtraynt aduerſytie harmes wyll cured time right fully ſure vpon ſyde foūde might recure wherfore nought ſobbe wepe fro breſt wt ſyghes ſought full dede broken pale dead viſage thus ala furious rage full pyteouſly hooſte without reſpite continued dayes three tyll laſte darke ſkyes blacke gan wo partye ſlacke tempeſt ſome deale gan withdrawe wepynge blādyſhe gan ye wawe whan floode wo ouer paſte ebbe ioye folowe muſt haſte ſorowe euer wolde hertes ſhende terme euery wo muſt ende though frēdes mē may wepe wayle deth teares may avayle wherfore kyng care hath ſought waye citie repaire caſte hym fully wolde ſo make vertue neceſſytie manfully tene whan eyre gan wexen clene myſtes cloudy ſorowe ſome deale adawe gan morowe heuyneſſe derke nyght chaced awaye ſonne bryght newe ioye aye fyne wo muſte gladneſſe whan ſorowe ygo ſo pryam certayne ſpace whan ſorowe gan lyte lyte paſſe wyſedome pytious ſmerte gan prudently plucken vp herte eyen wawes gan clere anone wroughte ye ſhall ¶howe pryam ſonne lamedon ſuccedynge father buylded cytye agayne cap xi ſorowe aſwaged ſyghes olde longe proceſſe lyke tolde worthy kyng called pryamus herte nowe ſo deſyrous vpon playne ſo waſte wilde ſtronge towne newe buylde deuyſe cytie edifye ſhall aſſautes vtterly defye enmyes mortall foone riche toures walles harde ſtone aboute countreyes enuiron made ſeke euery regyon ſuche workemen curyous wyt inuentife caſtyng meruaylous ſuche coulde crafte geometrye ſotyll fantaſye euery ſuch good deuyſour maſon hewer crafty quarreour euery wryghte paſſyng carpenter may founde eyther ferre nere ſuch coulde graue groupe carue ſuche able ſerue lime ſtone reyſe wall bataylyng creſtes marciall ſuch connynge head alabaſter white read marbell grey pullyſhe playne make ſmothe vaynes grayne ſente alſo euery ymage entayle euery portreyour coulde wel drawe wt colour peynte hewes freſhe yt worke feynte ſuche coulde wt countenaunce glad make ymage wyll neuer fade counterfeate mettall tree ſtone ſotill worke hym pygmaleon appollo whiche bokes tell ymagerye excelle crafte workyng curyous tombe made kyng daryus whiche alixſandre dyd heyght reyſe men ſhulde fame preyſe conqueſt perce went thus priam euery mayſter ſente eche caruer curious ioyner make knottes wt many queynt floure ſette creſtes within eke maiſters toke charge deuyſed haue ſettynge ſcyte holſome eyre delyte ¶and ſoyle defouled ruyne walles olde made playne lyne workman gan citie founde full mightly ſtones ſquare rounde worlde none vnto lyche workemanſhyp buylding riche crafte curyous maſonrye termes ſpeke geometrye wherfore muſt ſette ſyde certaynly neuer redde enclide maiſter foundour worke ſquare compaſſe kepe meaſure leuell lyne rude clearely diffyne diſcriue worke euery parte lacke termes longyng arte dare well trouth affyrmen worlde ne neuer pere vnto citie write ſothe boke maiſter guydo dothe myghte proſperitie hyghe honour felicitie aſſaut perpetually contune rayſed worſhyp neptune named troye tho toforne like firſt grekes lorne length therof ſhortly conclude three dayes iourne lyke latitude neuer erſt herde make mencyon ſuche nother foundacion huge compaſe ſuch largeſſe counte ſo paſſyng fayreneſſe edifyed luſty ſyghte read walles heyght two hundred cubytes marbell grey magecolled without ſautes aſſaye make pleaſaunt delyte amonge marbel alblaſter whyte meynt walles rounde ye towne make ſhewe within eke without freſhe ſo ryche ſo delectable alone incomparable city mortall man sawe euer yet ſyth world began corner euery wall ſette crowne golde ryche ſtones yfrette ſhone full bryght againe ye ſonne ſhene euery towre bretexed ſo clene choſe ſtone ferre ſonder beholde wonder therto citie compaſſed beaſtes beares lyon tygers bore serpētes dragon hertes eke brode horne elyphauntes large vnicornes bugle bulles many great gryffon forged braſſe coper laton cruelly ſygnes face vpon foon made felle menace barbycans alſo bulworkes huge afore towne made hyghe refuge nede ſhulde early eke late portekoles ſtronge euery gate aſſautes nede take charge locke thycke brode large al ye gate wel wrought ſhyning braſſe eke within mighty ſhytting yren barres ſtronge ſquare rounde great barres pytched grounde huge cheynes forged diffence whiche ne wolde breake violence harde theym win euery houſe buylded within euery paleys euery manſyowne marbell throughout towne crafty buildyng working moſt royall highte euery wall sixty cubytes grounde accounted none yt hath ſurmoūted citie one hyght aliche ſoth pore ryche harde hye eſtate lowe houſe paleys ſonder knowe egally tymbre ſtone theyr houſes reyſed euerychone yf ſhuld reherſen corne knottes craft maſonry freſhe enbowīg wt verge right lynes houſyng ful backewines ryche coyning luſty tablementes vinettes ronning caſementes though ye termes engliſhe wolden rime ſhewe theim haue time ne yet language picked none tell ſotyll ioynyng ſtones howe put ſtede mortere ioyntoures coper gylte full clere make ioyne leuell lyne amonge marbell freſhely ſhyne agaynſt ſonne whan ſhene lyght smote golde burned bright make worke gliſter euery ſyde towne ſtretes large wyde crafte ſo prudently prouyded workman ſette ſo deuyded holſome eyre amyddes myght enſpyre erely morowe deſyre zephirus ſo comfortable nouryſhe thinges bene vegetable tyme yere throughout euery ſtrete ſugred ſauour luſty ſo ſwete moſte pleaſauntly eyre gan ſmyte citezeynes onely delyte breth recomforte whan lyſte walke theim ſelfe diſporte thrugh towne wt crafty purueiaunce great auiſe diſcrete ordenaunce compaſe caſt ſquared ſquyers pulliſhed marble vpon ſtronge pyllers deuyſed longe large wyde euery ſtreate fronter ſyde freſhe alures luſty hye pynacles moūſtryng outward coſtly tabernacle vauted aboue lyke reclynatoryes called deambulatoryes men walke togithers twaine twaine kepe thē drye happed rayne ſaue fro tempeſt winde thundre lyſt ſhroude thēſelfe vnder euery houſe couered lead many gargoyle many hydous head ſpoutes thorough pipe aught ſtone worke canell raught voydyng fylthes lowe grounde thorough grate made yron perced roūd ſtretes paued bothe length brede cheker wyſe ſtones whyte reade euery crafte maner man lande deuyſe reken kyng pryamus hye diſcreciowne ordeyned hath dwell towne ſtreates ſeuered yonder eueryche ſet ſonder myght commoditie eche hymſelfe worke lybertye ¶goldſmythes fyrſt riche iewelleres ſelfe crafty brouderers weuers alſo wollen lyne clothe golde damaſke ſatyn veluet ſendell double ſamyt eke eueryche clothe men lyſte ſeke smythes alſo coulden forge wele pollaxes ſwerdes ſperes ſharpe ſtele dartes dagger mayme wounde quarelheades ſharpe ſquare ygrounde alſo crafty armerers maker bowes alſo theſe fletcher ſuche coulde make ſhaftes playne eke dyd buſy payne werre make alſo trappures baners beate royall cote armures diuers standardes penouns fyelde freſhe gaye getouns euery crafte may reckened tell ſhortly citie towne ſo ryche excellent myddes large ryuer went cauſynge full great commoditie whiche twayne hath parted citie courſe full ſwyfte wt freſhe ſtremes clere hyght xantus guydo doth v lere rede vpon flode eche ſyde many mylle ſtode whē nede graine corne grinde ſuſteyne ſtorye fynde ryuer eke fyſhe full plenteous deuided workemen curious craftely caſtynge ſouerayne courſe ſtremes might attaine areche guydo doth coniecte arch ſtronge courſe reflecte condite pypes large wyde withal certayne meanes artifyciall tho made full purgacion ordure fylthes towne waſſhyng ſtretes ſtode rowe gutter earth lowe citie fylthe yſene cauell ſcoured ſo clene eke deuoyded ſo ſecrete wyſe man myght eſpye deuyſe engyne fylthes fer nere borne awaye courſe ryuer couertly euery thyng coured wherby towne vtterly aſſured engendryng corruption wycked eyre infexion cauſe ofte vyolence mortalitie great peſtilence example flode made tybre rome wrought eneas whiche alſo departeth rome two myne auctour ſaith note ſo tenhabite royall chiefe citie kynge pryam hath eche countre made ſerche hole entent prouinces adiacent borowes townes ſmales vyllages ygathred maner age thropes folkes full dyuers ſuche vacant diſpers troye regyowne made hath entre towne great multitude yonge olde tenhabyte ye haue herde tolde thoſe afore foreynes hath troye made citezeynes full diſcretly lyke founde whan gan people abounde kynge priamus hye affectiowne buyldyng myghty towne hath harte caughte fantaſye newe cytie magnifye put remembraunce fully caſte ſome obſeruaunce myghty mar ſterne ferſe hewe ſpecially certayne playes newe horſe foote many ſondry wyſe gyue men knyghthode excercyſe eueryche put aſſaye iuſtes lyſtes alſo tourney preue force whā happe mete play founded firſt crete lande hye lowe eſtate martys honour dedicate palaſtre wake nyght play men taſſaye might foote many ſotyll poynt ſome naked enioynt wynne pryſe dyd full entent founde clerkes full prudent cheſſe playe moſte gloryous whiche ſo ſotill ſo meruaylous harde matter diſcryue though man ſtudied lyue ſhall aye fynde dyuers fantaſyes wardes makynge newe inparties therin ſo great diuerſytie fyrſt founde citie ſyege lyke ſayth guydo iacobus de vitriaco contrary opynyon lyke maketh playnly mencion affyrmeth full aduyſe philometer philoſopher wyſe vnto kynge ſtynte crueltee foūde firſt playe made caldee grece thence ſent alſo troye great auiſement playe founde firſt dyce table caſtynge chaunces deceyuables cauſe haue byn full ofte great debate one founde fortunate wynne whyle fauour chaunce ware ſodeyne varyaunce vnhappely put cleane backe folke ſtode vpon wracke loſſe plonged diſtreſſe reyſed haue haſte hye rycheſſe gladneſſe one rage deuaunt haſarde paſſage one haue ioye nother ſuffreth wo lyke bone ronnen fro hundred ſyth daye varye blandyſhing contrary man aſſured ioye ¶and firſt alſo read troye ſonge red many freſhe comedy dities called ben tragedy declare ſhortly ſentence bothe two fynall difference ¶a comedye hath gynnynge pryme face maner complaynynge afterwarde endeth gladneſſe dedes onely doth expreſſe ſuch pouerte plonged lowe ¶but tragedye ſo lyſte knowe ſtyll begynneth proſperitie endeth lykewyſe aduerſytie doth alſo conqueſt treate ryche kynges lordes great mighty men olde conquerours fraude fortune ſodeine ſhoures ouer caſte whelmed glory whylom thus halowed ye memorye tragedyes bokes maken mynde red ſonge fynde ¶in theatre ſmale aulter amyddes ſette halfe circuler eaſt cuſtome directe vpon whiche pulpet erecte therin ſtode auncient poete reherſe rethorykes ſwete noble dedes hyſtoryall kynges prynces memoryall theſe olde worthy emperours great empryſe eke conquerours gate martes hye honour lawrer grene fyne labour palme knighthod diſſerued old date parchas made paſſen fate ¶and chere face pale ſtyle enclyned gan tourne tale ſynge looſe full mortally ſtroke attropoſe tell alſo worthy head ſodeyne breaking liues threde piteouſly made theyr mortall ende thrugh falſe fortune yt al ye world wil ſhende fyne worthyneſſe ended ſorowe hyghe triſteſſe compaſſynge fraude falſe treaſon ſodaine murder vengeaunce poyſon conſpyryng fretyng falſe enuye vnwarely dydden dye renowne mighty fame hatred ſodeynly made lame honour dawnward gā decline miſchiefe vnhappy fyne fortune vnſwete tolde red poete whyle pulpet ſtode deadly face deuoyde blode synging ditees muſes rent amyd theatre ſhrowded tent came men gaſtfull cheres diſfygured face viſeres playing ſygnes people ſyght poet ſonge hath heyght maner diſcordaunce atwene ditees countenaunce ¶for lyke lofte dyd expreſſe wordes ioye heauineſſe meaning chere beneth theim playing poynt poynt alway anſwering triſte glad heuy light face ychaunged ſodeyne ſyght craftely coulde tranſfygure conformyng chante plure ſynge ſodaynely wepe well coulde obſeruaunces kepe done apryll may whan bloſmes new buſhe hey floures freſhe gynne ſprynge byrdes wood ſynge luſt ſuppryſed ſomer ſonne whan theſe playes troye begon theatre halowed yholde thus rytes tragedyes olde pryamus worthy kyng began matter tell bvt wyll forth ſtorye wryte matter boyſtouſly endyte pryamus paſſyng dylygent ryght deſyrous inwardly feruent ſo myght amonge workes bylde palays ryche hall whiche ſhulde choſe chyefe dungyon royall ſee ſouerayne manſyon whan gan worke approche made builde hye vpon roche aſſure geometrye longeth art trebled ſeuenth parte fynde myght experience meaſure hole circumference lande alſo playnly eke conteyned within ſtronge wall creſt place loweſt vpreyſed full ſyxe hundred paſe builded marbell ful royall ful ſtronge many ryche ſtone amonge whoſe toures reyſed vp ſo hye lyſt greces vp aſſende might ſe inſpection fayre boundes many regyon prouinces ſtode rounde walles within wrought beryle cleare cryſtall ¶and high amiddes noble ylion ryche paſſing foundacion whych clerkes yet theyr bokes prayſe kyng priam made hall rayſe excelling beaute ſtrengthe latitude according lengthe marbyll outward wall tymbre noble ſpeciall halfe cedre reherſe remnaunt ryche heban moſt able dare ſpecifye ſtone ioyne craft carpentrye tymber haue ſoueraynte tel heban tree lyke bokes ſothely finde cometh ethiop ynde blacke geate wyll waxe anone whan korne harde ſtone euermore laſt wil endure corrupt water moyſture hall diffine ſtones ſquare leuel line paued full great dilygence maſonrye paſſyng excellence aboue reyſed ſee ful curyouſly ſtones perre called chiefe pryncipall reygne ſeate moſt royall tofore ſet great delyte borde heban yuerye white egally yioyned ſo clene worke ryft yſene ſeſſyons made euery ſyde onely ſtates ordre deuide eke hall conuenable eche partye dormaunt table yueree eke heban tree euen agayne kynges royall ſee partye therto contrayre yrayſed many crafty ſtayre high hall ſyte ryght lyne oppoſytr pured metall ſtones clere brede length full rych aultere ſtode fygure vyſage maſſy golde wonderful ymage honoured high ſeate onely name iupyter great ¶and ſtatue huge weyght fyftene cubytes compleyt heyght crowne golde high vpon heade heauēly ſaphyres many ruby redde fret enuyron ſtones inde amonges medled fynde whyte pereles maſſye large rounde moſt chefe dirkeneſſe confound carbuncle ſet kyng ſtones recomforte gladden hall enlumine black night freſhenes ruddy light value therof ineſtymable ryches playnly incomparable ymage diuiſion ſhape proporcion heade foote ſo mayſterly entayled poynt workmā hath failed parfourme crafty excellence priamus dread reuerence honoured hath aboue goddes miſchiefe clepe call hole affection ſoueraygne truſt chefe deuocion hope alſo affyaunce welth ioye aſſuraunce welfare proſperytye hath committed deyte wening herte wonder ſykerly aſſured miſchefe therby diffended eche aduerſytye holde reygne high felicitye honour contynually ſhyne iupyter power diuine hym hath protection truſt full opinion thus worke ende achyeued wherof pryam ioye full releued citye noble ilion hath fully brought vnto perfection lyke entent whā therof began thus pryam king worthy man full many day newe troye lyeges lad lefe ioye hym leue royall ſete soueraygnly reygning quyete procedyng forth ſo ye liſt heare vnto effect anone matere ¶how king pryā ſend anthenor grece haue reſtored ayen ſiſter exion ca xii hateful harme moſt dred kindled ſo longe ſparke olde hatred roote debate grounde enuy yre newe flawme hertes fyre grayne malyce cauſer offence rancour ruſted impacyence haſt newe made feſtred ſores ſmert whan thou art one raked herte diſdayne mercye mayſt lete man whyle lyue quyete delueſt vp malyce manyfolde debate newe buryed olde falſly quyckeſt ſtrifes reſtore enuious ſerpēt ſlayne yore felly hath addre enuyous reſt awaked pryamus venim ſo perſyng ſo ille made wery lyue lyfe tranquille meued hym iniquitee vpon grekes auenged peace held reygne lyeges ioye ſouereygne without anoye perturbaunce ſerpent hath wyth newe remembraūce without aduyſe diſcrete areſte hote flawme kindled breſte olde enuye freſhe rancour meynte lykly neuer queynte pryam nowe entenciowne caſt compaſſeth reuoluing vp downe howe ſtrong ryches meyne noble mighty newe citye habundaunt ſhortly conclude plentye multitude men armes chyualrye ſtered haue fanteſye ala whyle vnhappy chaunce dead take vengeaunce vpon foon fyre hote enuye brent inward melancolye standing purpoſe yt man chaūge may domages auenged ſome day iniuryes yt thei haue wrought ¶and tyme ſought purpoſe moſt conuenient anone hath lordes ſent knightes called euerychone come haſte excuſed one namely theim hygh degre obeying humylitye bydding hooly made delay come echeone agayne certayne day ſonnes alſo tho preſent hector except tyme abſent ſtronge mighty regyon panomye ſubiection kinge pryam held worthyneſſe amende thinges redreſſe hector gone panomye certayne cauſes iuſtifye reaſon thought beſt ſettle theim quiet reſt aye ſo iuſt ſo prudent well aduyſed ſo pacient ſo demeaned gouernaunce lothe vengeaunce might eaſy wiſe treate reforme thinges ſmall great lothe noble worthy knighte haſte execute vnright cauſeles rygour condempne full worthy ſolempne kinge priamus lordes great ſmall within troye held court royall lyſt coſt ſpare ceryouſly meaning declare ſee lordes enuyron gan ſhewe hertes entention ¶o worthy lordes aſſembled preſent faythfull trewe herte entēte well knowen diſcrecion great domages foule oppreſſion ye grekes
