golde ſtore plenty ynough none indygence shoulde haue power hym offence vnto vowe make quod anthenor platly vndertake golde good thou ſhalt haue ſuffyſaunce treaſour paſſynge habundaunce thou ſhalt ſykerneſſe thy kyn excelle rycheſſe thou delyuer lyke myne axynge palladyon whych thy kepynge behote thou mayſte truſt bonde ſhalbe ſecree leſt hyndrynge thy name ſo thou dreadeſt ſhame eſclaundred ſo foule deede ſhape ſhall thou nede drede agaſte maner wyſe ſuch waye ſothe ſhall deuyſe man ſhall ſuſpecyous thy perſon engenyous deme amyſſe matter goth well ware lothe diffamed ſo foule thynge knowe therof aſſentynge maner towne shoulde haue ſuſpecyowne let let leuer deye ſhall therfore caſte wey honour ſaue ſo thou shall go quyte ſaye vtterly neyther ſhall beholde ne perceyuere thefte ſtande hole clere euer fall without ſhame vlyxes ſhall beare blame dede thefe alſo men ſhall ſaye ago engyne ſleyghty wyle traynes falſe guyle hath ſtole awaye palladyowne temple leaſynge towne fynally durynge lyue men ſhall hym falſhede deſcryue gylte arreten offence thou onely innocence throughout worlde iniquytye shall excuſed platly go free nedeth tarye mattere come attones lo thy golde thou ne ſhalt longer delayed ſith thou ſeeſt difficultye parte perle reprefe shame dread ſlaundre miſchyefe delaye take thinge hande firſt prieſt gan withſtande full myghtely ſayde nothinge nother prayer manaſinge golde good ne maner mede ne would aſſente ſo foule deede thus anſwered pryme face ofte ſith happeth men purchaſe gifte good ſpeake wordes playne trouth pouerte might neuer attayne mede falſhed maye conquere tytle ryght men trouthe lere gyftes great hertes enclyne golde maye ſtele marbyll mine prieſtes herte hath ſo depe graue anthenor ſhall purpoſe haue poſſede palladion falſe engyne conſpiracion prieſt called tonaunte falſhede myght beſte auaunte relyke fro temple rente vlyxes anthenor ſente towne haſte might ſeruaunt ſecretly nyght wherof troians mortally diſmayde treaſon fynally outrayed wrought prieſt couetiſe blent falſe anthenor beinge aſſente ¶howe grekes made horſe braſſe wherin men armes vnder colour peace brought troye whych vtterly deſtroyed euer cap xxxv oh troy ala wel mayſt yu morne wepe complaynyng wt hertye ſighes depe falſly defrauded palladyon put euer poſſeſſyon ¶oh mighty goddes yt worlde gouerne euerything might cōſerne ryght dewtye trouthe falſhed maye togither ſe euery herte purueyaunce toke ye prieſt vengeaunce traytourſly inyquytye golde good betrayſhed cytye troye ala without recure ſhall emforth ſuer place ſtande ſykertee syth holyneſſe ſo hygh degree maye infecte corrupt mede euery herte ought quake drede ſe ala falſe ypocraſye prieſtes ſhould worlde exemplefye good doctryne perfection make ſo ſoone tranſmutacion double entent ſodainly varye doubtles sanctuarye pollut founde conuerſacyon naked bare deuocyon ſhynynge theyr parfyte light ytourned derkeneſſe vnto nyght vnto place ſhall men go take example ought certys roote ground euerydele couetyſe ſo loke wele whych grayne ſo farre yſowe ſo lyſt aueryce knowe amonge prieſtes ſhall ratheſt fynde therwythall made blynde theyr eſtate maye ſe ſotheneſſe degre gredyer rauynous worldly good couetous prieſtes catche maye gone ſyth many daye theyr breſt fyxed roote couetyſe whych ſyt ſo ſoote man maye arrace remewe theyr tayle euer doth ſewe falſe worme mother noryce myſchyefe euery yvce golde nowe ſo ſhynynge ſo bryght perſynge eke ſo clere lyghte prieſtes ſteemes blent ſothneſſe theyr entente couetyſe receptacle poſſede eke tabernacle theyr herte aye ſo gredy embrace aueryce hath dwellynge place mid breſt vice vyces cauſeth vertue rather fall abyde ſo ſupplaunte recorde take prieſt tonaunte treaſour anthenor hath ſolde ryche relyke holde palladion troye towne haue gathered vp aboute enuyron riche poore throughout citye golde ſyluer huge quantytye floure whete paye theyr raunſom whych ſumme entencion made kepe wyſely conſerue temple longeth mynerue purpoſynge one affectiowne citezyns throughout towne hopinge therby fare bet vpon daye aſſygned yſet apollo theyr panym wyſe solempnelye make ſacrafiſe ſlaughter beſtes wt encenſe bloude whych daye pryeſtes ſtode compaſſe rounde aultere gan kyndle cole bryght clere vpon aulter playnly reade offer vp beaſtes deade flawme great leuen apollo ſtellyfyed heauen offer moſt laborous fyrſte ſacryde fyre ne would brenne lyke deſyre flawme vp aſcende alofte albe aſſayed full ofte ten tymes yet ne would aye queynt ne myght ſe nought ſmoky reſolucions horryble blake lyke exalacyons newe lyme meynt water colde heat queynt might maner wyſe lacke fyre theyr ſacrafyſe aye found wonder obſtacle nexte myracle theyr aulter gan ſprede entrayles beaſtes deade queme apollo wt flawme bryght faire came anone downe ayre royall egle full perfynge loke clawes offerynge vp toke entrayles lyinge enuyrowne deſcence makynge ſuch ſowne none ſo hardy herte manhode aſtoned ſtode ſuppryſed nerfe euerye vayne meruayle caſe ſodayne egle abydynge ouer towne full hygh gan ſore towarde grekes enhaſtyng might theyr ſhyppes ſodaynly alyghte entrayles beaſtes egle let clawes fal wherof troyans toke hede diſmayed wyth mortall dreade ſygnes haue clerely comprehended theyr goddes greatly offended agayne towne fyre went would put doute ſure meruayle mente caſſandra haſte ſente fully haue declaracyon therupon playne expoſycyon ſhe tolde theim platly dreade quenchynge theyr fyres red vnto demonſtracion yre indygnacion ¶that apollo hath troye bore bloud ſhed achylles temple ſlawe vengeably murdred ydrawe without maner reuerence honour done excellence apollo beynge preſente phane plate adiacent deſolued pollut wyth bloude wherfore ſhe ſayde ſhortly good went proſeſſyon herte contryte deuocyon tombe achylles nyght onelye fette theyr tapres lyght sacred fyre brennynge wake fully purpoſe aſſente make mordre ſatiſfaction whych fyre none occaſyon shall quenche flawmes holde none aſſault ſtormye windꝭ wyttes ſought entrayles egle broughte therupon gan togyther rounde til calchas euery thing expowne vnto theym full gan aſſure fine auenture conclude ſhould vpon theyr welfare bad alſo coſte ſpare perſeuer herte ſtable fortune theym ſelfe enhable theym counſaylynge theyr buſy payne solempnelye haſte ordayne certayne offrynge borne felde fayre pallas criſtall ſhelde make ryche ſacrafyſe ſtorye ordre ſhall deuyſe byſhop calchas wyth locke hore traytour forſworne ſyth go ful yore falſed hath trouthe allyaunce clerkes haue put remembraunce theyr locke letter olde newe exemplefye man vntrewe though yeares paſſe faſte awaye ruſt ſclaunder lightly wyll deye fret therof ſo corroſyfe laſteth full many mannes lyfe full harde arrace awaye whoſe venym full ſelde made allaye reporte therof blowen perfection workemanſhyppe tolde afore ſiege ſothly gan fine cyte brought ruyne grekes myght wall ſtrōge bete downe large thicke longe yeare made menciowne lyttell afore takynge towne kinges echone came fro ſo ferre alyue lefte mortall werre ſaw priam couenaunte vnto grekes vtterly made graunt haſte poſſible paye raunſowme toke leue went towne fyrſte fynde kynge phylomene lad body quene pantaſillia home countre ful richely buryed ij thouſande knightes kinge brought vnto troye fyrſt comynge mo fyftye home ladde woman quene hadde thouſand ſtorye ſayth certayne foure hundred home agayne thus fro troye gone morowe nexte priamus anone lordes rode towne accorde confyrmaciowne peace fynall vpon outher ſyde ¶and fyelde grekes hym abyde ¶and grekes firſte ſwore dyomede troye takynge lyttle hede othe condicion cured aboue vnder falſe treaſon syth grekes tho ſwearynge ne bounde ſelfe maner thynge ſtande ſpecyall holde kepe generall poyntes hole engreſſed thilke treate dan anthenor grekes helde traytour fraudulent whiche full double entent meynt treſon ye haue herde toforne whiche obſerue onely ſworne fraude othe wordes playne aduerſaryes take trayne excludynge meanyng ferre peace face herte werre openly confirmed hande inwarde treaſon aſſuraunce bonde though venym cloſed wt wall hyd knoweth certaynely clerkes teache ſwereth falſely ſpeche flouryſhynge outwarde fayre coloure deceyue whiche ende full dere abought founde fully reuerſe ſpeche dede ſo dyuerſe fayne wryte fayned othes wordes whyte cheris coulde fayne conclude quene heleyne durynge treate vpon ſame daye ¶delyuered kynge menelaye payde raunſowne graunted tofore gathered towne golde ſyluer alſo floure ſhyppes diligent laboure full great haſte euery thyng brought citie came nought ¶and grekes ſymulacyon makynge colour deuocion holyneſſe vnder ypocriſye falſly fayned fraude flaterye kynge haue prayed haue lybertye frely entre cytye make aſſete oblacyon thefte palladyon offer vp riche ſtede braſſe goddeſſe called pallas ¶what kynge pryam lyketh aſſygne ſhe wyllinge beninge repeyre ſaylynge ſea home grece towarde countre ſhe quemed large ſtede whiche ala pryam toke hede ¶the treaſon hyd coulde aduerte graunted hole herte lyke bringe towne falſe entyſinge ſuggeſtiowne anthenor alſo enee hauynge drede ambyguite entent ſuſpection nother fayninge falſe treaſon right frendely lyke beheſte condeſcendeth vnto requeſte auowes myght obſerue offer vp horſe vnto mynerue grekes tho great diligence full great honour huge reuerence haue ſhapen proceſſiowne bringe ſtede troye towne men armes beinge aye therin glad towne ſpecyall troye ¶but ſothe ſayde aye fyne ioye occupyeth men full ofte ſe vnwarely cometh aduerſytye gladneſſe wo myſauenture men beſte wene ſtanden ſure worldly blyſhe none affyaunce dyuers vnhappy chaunce full deceyte euer meynt trouble truſte varyaunt double ſelde one abydynge throwe worldly luſte though blowe pompe pride boſte ſowne anone paſſeth recorde troye towne wende well ryche grounde gynnyng wo rote cauſe alſo ſlaughter many worthy man sythen tyme ſyege fyrſt began wherfore ſayde ſtynte ſtryfe ſure ſaue lyfe beſt ſende ſyght secretely tenedowne nyght thus fayned full falſe gone crafty locke vndoynge euerychone goth gan anone calle within horſe worthy knyghtes ſecretly man myght eſpye trayterouſly gan hym hye vpon walles ſelfe ſame nyght towarde grekes gan ſhewe lyght laye tofore tenedowne redy armed falle vpon towne whan ſodayne light eſpyed horſe backe anone haue hyed towarde troye armed clene went ſame walle whyche horſe late broke mortally wroke knyghtes eke ſtede braſſe haue met full ſterne pace gan anone throughout citye euery halfe kylle ſlea bloudy ſworde vpon euery ſyde made woundes brode large wide whyle ala thinge aduertynge mydnight houre abedde lay ſlepynge full innocent thought good forbathed owne bloude bothe man childe without exception grekes ſparynge condicyon olde yonge woman wyfe mayde ¶that crye pryamus abrayde ſlepe ſodeynely awoke whiche laye nyght hede ne toke ſlaughter murther towne ¶but tho wiſte treaſowne falſely compaſſed vnto cytee anthenor alſo enee whoſe malys doubte venym taken oute galle conſpyracion vnder ſugre ſymulacion hath ſo longe cloſed hyd dede nowe execute kyd nowe fraude fully treaſon caſtes alſo falſe colluſyon raked abrode yblowe auctours openly yknowe ¶now hath enuye contryued hate engyne ſette abrode gate hate deceyte olde conſpyracye fayned othes one allye openly ſhewed theyr falſeneſſe diſcloſed doubleneſſe farre abrode nowe geyne nowe ala wylde fyre ſeyne tower hye wynde yblaſed wherof eyen caſtynge vp whyte vayne wofull caſe wryte maner mortall ſorowe ¶but guydo wryt ſame morowe anthenor falſe euee conueyed haue throughout cyte myghty grekes vnto ilyon royall toure ryche manſyon whylom moſt excellence whiche founde tho dyffence hyghe lowe none eſtate lefte alone deſolate golde rycheſſe towne shet encloſed chyefe dongeowne man withſtode brake locke raught away ye good treaſure anthenor enee ſtode beſyde routhe pytye beholde ſe lye ſtones colde pyteouſly tofore aulter blede wherof ala hecuba toke hede fayre doughter polycene heire rent golde wyer ſhene inly ſuppryſed ſorowe herte began conſider aduerte noble kinge bloudy ſtreames red drowned eyen derke dead pirrhus ſword girte thrugh outher ſide mortall feare durſt abyde inwardly darted ſight rage toke flyghte yet ſo cite wyſte neuer whytherwarde flee reſcuſe none remedye kynne friende none allye grekes ſworde towne ſo ſette flight wofull quene hath met eneas cauſer wrake vnto rebukynge thus ſpake oh thou traytour moſt malycious thou falſe ſerpent adder enuyous croppe roote fynder falſeneſſe soures well vnkyndeneſſe myghteſt thou thy hande fynde vnto thy kynge ſo vnkynde gynner grounde example treaſon fynall cauſe deſtruction myghteſt thou deuoyde pytye beholdynge ala thy cruelte kynge ſhedde ſo bloude euer hath byn ſo gentyll ſo good gracious lorde ſpecially ouermore throughe highe bounte honoured ymagnefyed lyfe may denyed lyeth dead temple ala thou onely traytour caſe death conſpyrynge vnkynde pirrhus conueying ſhuld finde tofore apollo myddes cyte thou ſhuldeſt duetye rather haue byn protection myghty ſhelde ſauacion haſte citie towne ylorne whiche thou foſtred yborne greateſt reputacion lordes dwellinge towne thou haddeſt whilom moſt pleſaūce remembraunce ¶yet thy hert yf drape gentylneſſe mercy pytye deadly rage full tene rewe doughter yonge polycene grekes ſworde youthe ſaue thy herte may routhe haue manly pytye maydenheade defende nowe kepe drede thou canſte fynde weye wyſe ſhe maye deye ¶that hereafter men ſe rede falſe treaſon foule dede thou haſte done vnto troye towne maye partye protectiowne thy fame venym allye treaſon men wyll aſſaye iuſte reporte thy name accuſe dede may helpe excuſe agaynſt tonges ſpeake enee wyll ſaye thou haddeſt yet pytye polycene onely gentilneſſe therwith ſugre bytterneſſe thy deſerte blowe forth fame reherſayle foule blame ſhal worlde borne ſklaūder infect whē thou art al torne thou ne ſhalte ſhame mowe ſuſtene ſhall doughter fayre polycene thy defence agayne ſuche famous ſtryfe ſo thou ſaue lyfe force though thou make blyue ſworde grekes herte ryue ¶and ſo prayer wofull quene eneas toke hym polycene whoſe traytour herte cruelte youthe meued pytye onely routhe breſt aroſe ſecretely put vp cloſe leſt grekes founde occaſyon agaynſt hym ayax thelamon toke warde andromecha hector wyfe wyfe caſſandra temple longing mynerue grekes ſworde lyues conſerue ¶and menelaye toke quene heleyne garde ſo great payne bode herte many daye toforne ala cytye lorne ¶and grekes aye buſye yre ſlea kylle crullly fyre euery ſyde beate downe palyce houſe wall towne ſpare nought goth fyre feruent hate brent deſyre olde enuye auenged ne lefte within cyte nothynge vnbrent alſo ylyowne rage tourned vp ſo downe made none exception onely take poſſyons anthenor euyll mote fare eneas grekes ſpare th • bounde othe thus grekes furyous wrothe haue daye robbed ybrent ¶tyll kynge agamenon hath ſent lordes aſſemble yfeare pallas temple onely wyſe aduyſe vpon thynges twayne fyrſte wolde holde fayne hooly hope without exceptiowne thē wonne fyrſt towne ¶and ouer axed alſo touchynge goddes wolde golde treaſour poſſeſſyowne haue thrugh hie renown ¶and anſwered without taryinge wolde faith kepe euery thynge ſworne heſtes holde ouer ſayde howe wolde golde treaſour good cyte ryght requietrh alſo equitye iuſtly parted deuyſion euery wyght made diſtribucyon lyke meryt hygh lowe degree kynge eke reaſon ſe eche rewarde labour longeth conquerour man haue matter compleyne ſo felle ſpeakynge heleyne eueryche opynyon tofore ayax thelamon shortly ſayde ſhe hath deſerued death ſo many haue yelde vp brethe playnely affyrmynge parlement ryghtwyſeneſſe trewe iudgement ſhulde eſcape lyfe gynnyng cauſe ſtrife rote grounde ſorowe wo ſo ſayde eke many mo noyſe great affraye ¶agamenon kinge menelaye ne durſt worde partye meue ſaue ye quene leſt grekes wold greue agaynſt ſo great rumour tyll vlixes chiefely ſocour wyt eloquence deuer dyd dylygence haue life fully purchace grekes gette grace ¶and guydo alſo doth v lere agamenon grekes gan requere graunt hym chiefe guerdon caſſandra haue poſſeſſion lyfe hym abyde eke eneas anthenor beſyde helenus grekes tolde werre neuer aſſente wolde prudennt vertuous counſaylyng contrarious tho hygh lowe eſtate troye firſt began debate atwyxe grekes myghty towne eke helpe medyatiowne achylles buryed ygraue deade corp houndes ſaue whan ſlayne full cruell wyſe nyght tyme ye haue herde deuyſe ſothly caſſandra murder herte full wrothe ſory eke many thynge wrought towne wtout wyttynge ¶and malyce innocent grekes haue fully aſſent graunted prerogatyfe parlement haue theyr lyfe helenus firſt teares drowned tofore kynge pyteouſly hath ſowned abraydynge deadly face humble wyſe beſought hym grace knyghtly pytye haue aduertence ſpare ſworde fro bloud innocence mercy diſdayne graunt lyfe ſonnes twayne ¶of worthy hector brother moſt entere eke rewe mother dere onely grace ſhe dead wydowe lefte lone reade ſo kynge ameued herte wote whither ſhe maye diuerte wordes wofull chere benygnely graunted prayer gaue eke lyfe fredom go mother chyldren two ¶and ladyes gentyll woman mercy grace calle graunted eke compaſſyon ſafe conduite fre pardon lyſte towne abyde countre adiacent beſyde put hole electiowne ¶and thanking fell knee many teare dewed face ¶and ſo kynge parteth fro place grekes ryght anone fully purpoſe ſhyp gone haſte ſayle towarde countre ſuche tempeſt roſe vp ſea wawe wynde alſo cloudes blacke moneth dare take water ſalte drede neptunus ¶of ire alſo golus vnto euery thynge contrary londe made longe tarye ſea aye ſo fell boylynge ¶tyll grekes calchas enquyryng one aſſent myght euer one ſo dyuers ſea rage eue morowe ¶and anſwered god gyue euyl ſorow olde ſhrewe prophecye ſo well hym lyſte lye tempeſt cauſed goddes furyes infernall neuer wolde appeaſe ſtylle tyll number platly achylle auenged ſhedynge bloud ¶for whiche ſayde apollo eke wood temple conſecrate death troye violate bloude agayne made ſatiſfaction wherfore muſte throughe redempcyon roote ſpeciall beautye orygynall cauſe death yonge polycene gynnynge fyrſt mortall tene therfore apollo ſhe might vp offred ſacrafyce pleaſe deyte death agayne make recompence right death fyrſt offence grekes muſt vtterly fulfyll deſyre haue wyll large ſea ſayle quiet ¶and pirrhus tho furious hete gan enquire euery man policene wyght tell worde ſhortely ſhe saufe ſome ſayde howe eneas anthenor hyd pryuely wherof roſe amonge ſodeynly suche agrutchynge grekes aboute lyfe doubte inwardly thinges toke grefe ¶till anthenor god geue hym euyll prefe may treaſon wardeyn bere ye keye ſhewe malys euery waye longe hath ſought till chamber olde hath founde grekes tolde brought forth vnto preſence cruell force hatefull vyolence without pytye compaſſyon delyuered agamenon ¶and ala haſtye iudgement without reſpyte auyſemente shortely hath dempte ſhe ſhall deade flourynge maydenhead ¶and excepcyon ¶she aſſygned agamenon vnto pirrhus tirannye ladde forth faſt gan hym hye place ſhe ſhulde dye ¶great preaſe weye gan croude ſhoue beholde ſene yonge mayde fayre pollycene beautye ſemlyneſſe womanhede excellent fayreneſſe yfere toke hede routhe ſhe ſhalbe deade without gylte treſpace men may ſe vpon many face ſalte teares faſte falle downe pytye compaſſyowne man childe none ſo harde hert felte ſake ſome ſmert goodly face whan beholde ſe fayne wolde might haue delyuered force anone fro pirrus hande wende echone without death neuer haue repeire grece wether fayre calchas made ſuggeſtion brought opynyon ¶and laſte whan policene dede wyll mayde clene graue achylles brought kneleth downe wt humble thought caſte vp eye gan ſyghe ofte goddes humbly ſofte dredfull herte deuocion made wyſe lamentacion oh ye myghty yt worlde gouerne euery thinge conſyder diſerne world ſo huge large rounde ayre ſea heauen eke ye grounde deuyſe worde wrought ſothfaſtly knowe euery thought right euery maner wyght without lettynge ſo perſynge ſyght nothinge conceyled ywrye beholdynge eternall eye euery thinge maye attones ſe vpon ſoule haue mercy pyte grace beninge cure vpon wo pyteous auenture haue ſome routhe nowe ſhall deye wofull ſpyryte lede conueye lyſt ſhall pace vnto ſelfe place confeſſe humilyte hytherto haue chaſtyte ladde lyfe kept maydēhead ſeruyce thought dede porte chere countenaunce feture daliaunce one miſloke neuer yet abrayde ſothe dye ſhall maide ye well knowe ſynne innocent though nowe dempt iudgement dead without gilte witneſſe immortall clene entente accuſed yet ala maye excuſed ſwerde vengeaunce muſt byte routheles nothinge wite ſtande cleare pure offence diſcharged conſcience dare affirme fully giltles touchinge murdre worthy achilles ſlewe brother loued nowe cauſe mine aduerſyte yet dede worde thought vnto death aſſentaunt right nought therof right ſory im herte albe maye aſterte dead onely ſake alone vengeaunce ſhalbe take without mercy full cruell wiſe bloud make ſacrafiſe goddes wrathe queme oh people blinde ſothe amiſſe ye deme agaynſt herte ſo cruell mercyles yrous fell without routhe mikel indurate ſley mayde alone deſolate herte ala pitye gone harder trouthe ſtocke ſtone cruell opinion lacke pitye tigre lion certis ye greatly blame ought therof haue great ſhame aſſent ſo foule dede ſley maide quakinge dread graunte none oportunitye wepe virginyte ¶that cruell piteous wreche bloude gylte hereafter ſhall apeche accuſe alſo great enuye goddes ſhall iuſtyfye euery vnright bothe hygh lowe full egally make knowe trouthe plainly ſpare degree make open ſecree ſaye ſelfe complayne haue redres fatall payne death welcome vnto lyfe take gree sithen brother moſt worthy renowne ſlayne buryed towne father dead vnweldy age alone leſte rage haue abyde pyteouſely ſe fynally ruyne cytye whiche herte ſytteth ſo ſore leuer haue wepe dye attones releſſe wo sith kynne paſſed ago longer lyue death better yelde vp breth led cyte amonge ſtraungers lyue pouertee oh death welcome longer lette thy dredefull darte fyle whette tender herte therwith ryue agayne thy myght wyll neuer ſtryue ¶now tyme keth power wyll herte entere clene mayde ſo began without touche maner man lyfe ſame daye lyttle auaunte yet make maye myne ende goddes whoſe helpe clyppe calle mercy mekely commende woful ſpirite pray ſende euery mayde better happe grace haue nowe longer ſpace hertye ioye honour contune without aſſaulte infortune leade lyfe proſperitye maydens remembreth vpon take enſample ye ſhall kepe ye wolde fewe teares wepe ye thynke vpon fayre pollyne age yeres grene whan ſhe ſlayne cruell auenture goddes haue cure dredfull goſte holely betake eternally thus ende make ¶and yt word head ſhe gan enclyne full humbly ſhe ſhulde fyne eyen helde lede downe ¶and pirrhus wodder lyon diſmembred hath ſherpe ſworde yonge made dredefull aferde ouer cruelte ſhewe peces ſmale hath hewe endelonge father ſepulture ala myght cruell herte endure mercyles ſo foule dede aſtoned ſothly reade death hym good lyke tiraunt caſte abrode bloude tygre routhe haue rounde enuyrowne father graue ſprent hate cruelte oh thou pyrrhus thou mayſte well ybe achylles ſonne lyneall diſcent lyke hym herte entente thou ſoth deuoyde pytye worſe yet one degree thy father lyuinge ne radde neuer yet ſo foule thynge though wolde hatred abrayde rancour euer ſlewe amayde fynde well parte whylom loue cupydes darte made ſore lyue ſmerte wounded herte caſtynge onely eye wenynge therby wyſtly dye myght ſodeyne ſtroke eſcape afterwarde fate hath ſhape ¶he murdred loue pollicene thou haſte ſlayne cruell tene furyouſly without routh ſhame whiche thynge foule hatefull fame al world hereafter ſhalbe ſpred ſtory reherſed red ſhalbe ſayd pirrhus routhleſſe slewe yre mayde gylteleſſe woryed ſhall thy name moſt odyble dede paſſyngly horryble loue onely fayre pollycene death hecuba quene hath ſene ala ſhe beſyde ſtode wo gan wood ſorowe wyt ſhe went clothes heire ſhe rent rage wot ſhe doth gan anone handes tothe furye ſcrache eke byte stone caſtes fyſtes ſmyte ſhe mette tyll grekes made bynde ſente forth alſo fynde yle troye partment ſhe ſlayne onely iudgement grekes ſtoned death whan ſhe yelde vp breth wofull quene cruell auenture grekes dyd make ſepulture ceryouſly metall ſtone toke corp buryed anone great honour ſolempnitee longe men might ſe ryche toumbe coſtfull royall ſet made memoryall hecuba whylom great fame gaue place name called longe mynde ¶locus feſtus guydo fynde thus quene onely ſorowe wood whan doughter ſhad bloud grekes ſtones dyd ende make ye haue herde plainly ſake policene whylom calchas vnto apollo falſly offred pyrrhus ſworde achylles auengyng make ſea calme blandyſſhydg goddes take vengeaunce vpon grekes euyll chaunce come falſe goddes euerychone ſtatues ſtockes ſtone whiche ſerpent olde ſnake sathan hym ſelfe gan dwellyng make fraudently folkes yllude full ſuttyll hym ſelfe illude ymages make holde forged ſyluer golde errour falſe illuſyon hath ybrought confuſyon miſchance worthy kinde man syth tyme alder fyrſte began falſe honour ydolatrye worſhyp vnto maumetrye ſacrafyce beaſtes bloud appeaſe wood queme bothe eue morowe praye god giue ſorowe ſo within without none excepte falſe route saturne mar pallas iuno iubyter mercurius pluto nother flora doth floures ſprede nother bachus grape white read cupydo eyen blynde nother daphne cloſed vnder rinde tellus might laurer tree thou dyane thy chaſtitee myghtye venus citherea thy dartes proſerpyna lady arte depe downe helle bellides draweth well ixyon thou zezyphus thyne appyll thou cruell tantalus fury infernall ye ſpynne lyues threde fatall vpon rocke euery maner man muſes ſo ſynge atwene coppys nyſus cira vpon hylle beſyde cyrrea cybele cere thy corne golus dredefull horne herde ſo ferre thou lyſte blowe ianus byfrons backe corbed low pryapes genyus preſt curſed aye candylles feſte echone frowarde kynde ymeneus whoſe power bynde hertes knit maryage tyll goddeſſe diſcorde rage diſſeuereth theim diuiſion nother maues haue manſyon myd erthe derkeneſſe wo elues wont go vndyrmeles phebus moſt ſhene nother fawny tender greues grene water nymphes naydes satyrye nother driades goddes wood wilderneſſe goddes nother leſſe morpheus god ſlepe holde hym wood taketh kepe obſeruaunce may fayle haue myſchaunce ende playnely mede ſuche feyned falſeneſſe drede roſe deuyll fyrſt engyne ſleyghty treynes ſerpentyne onely mankynde whan made loute falſe ydoles whiche doubte deuylles dauyd beareth wytneſſe ſaulter wryt expreſſe confyrmeth endites howe goddes paganiſme rytes one excepteth none made golde ſyluer ſtone forged braſſe metall tree eyen haue yet may ſe fendes ſo dauyd ſayth haueth fayth hope credence delyte drede wyll hym quyte ſuche guerdon ſoule ſleeth perpetually ſo fyne death ſeruyce men henſe pace lyfe vnhap euell grace miſchyefe wo confuſyowne men may ſe example towne wende well aſſured haue haue ſtande longe proſperitye agayne foen helpe apollo venus eke fauour iuno pallas might dyane mynerue wonte honour ſerue cerimonyes ſacrafyce ye tofore haue herde deuyſe haue brought ruyne cruell death bed fyne may ye ſe venym byte ende ſuche olde rytes euydence noble towne may auayle palladyowne may helpe frauded fantaſye olde falſe ydolatrye ala ala bought ſore farewell troye farewell euermore farewell ala cruell thy fall wryte ſhall thy ſake forſoth whan take hede inwarde wo herte fele blede remembre thought ruine thou arte brought noughte whylom ſo noble ſo ryche worlde trowe none liche perygall ſpeake fayreneſſe ſpeake knyghthode worthyneſſe clerkes ſay thy byldynge knewe worlde ought rewe thy piteous waſte walles wilde whylom ſo royall men gan bylde thy towres hye kynge pryamus fyrſt began moſt ryche gloryous ſette ſee noble ilyon oh wryte lamentacion conuenient oh troye thy ſake thy great myſchiefe complayne crye ¶certes trowe olde ieremye ſo wepte captiuitye thylke noble royall chyefe cyte ieruſalem deſtruction hole tranſmygracion ¶of iewes thou ezechyell tyme miſchiefe fell vnto kynge ycalled sedeclye babylon thy propheſye ſtones cruelly yſlawe departed ſawe ye bothe two colde ſo complaine danyell felte ſo great peyne kynges tranſmutaſyon beaſt tyll oryſon danyell reſtored mynde agayne eate graſſe ¶yet veryly though ye thre wepynge gan aliue preſent eke deſtructiowne noble worthy royall towne haue bewayled miſchiefe wo ſlaughter ſyege outher partye full cruell wyſe teares might ſuffyce haue bewepte ſorowes euerychone treaſon wrought aſwell foen ¶hereof may auayle lyke gynneth ſayle agayne wynde maſte ryue ryght ſo vayne ſtryue agayne face bytter galle vengeaunce vpon troye falle preſume furyes ſharpe whette ceryouſly boke ſette great thyng dare vndertake euen pyteous ende make ſyege ſympleſſe though ſtile blotted rudeneſſe metre ruſty vnfyled ¶the fourthe boke haue compyled humble hande drede yt doth quake vnto grace hooly betake ¶of mercy nothynge diſpryre makynge repeyre grekes longer dwelle aduentures ſea telle reſorte home countre receyued onely ſupporte ſo ye deſpyſe fyfthe boke ſhortely ſhall deuyſe ¶thus endeth fourth boke fyfthe boke ¶here begynneth fyfth booke howe grekes retourned grece diſtruction howe peryſſhed almoſte ſea eſcaped dyed myſcheuouſly cap xxxvi eolus whiche dothe wyndes rore appeaſed yt blewe whiche ſtormes gouernoure lorde alſo fully accorde myghty iuno lady ayre make ſkye wether fayre cloude none heauen dyd appere neptunus blaundyſhynge chere aſſent ſtory ſayeth ſoth make ſea fro tempeſt calme ſmoth without boyling trouble wawe mighty grekꝭ ſhipward gan thē draw repeyre home countre wonnen citye put fomen fully werſe fortune aye frowarde peruerſe hath mirth meynt aduerſyte wende full aſſured haue ſtande ſtedfaſte quyete blynde lady falſly made flete ſugred galle diſcordaunce amonge ſelfe brynge varyaunce hertes rancour pryde contagyouſly ſeueryne deuyde ſat hygheſt glorye palme conqueſt victorye fully reioyſynge hye renowne crowne laurer poſſeſſyowne alſo luſt wonne bryghteſt ſhone luſtye freſhe ſonne eaſt weſt worthyneſſe cloudye ſkye vnwarely derkeneſſe eclypſed hath partye light eke diffaced holſome beames bryght welfare proſperitie enuyous falſe contagyoſytie ſerpent pompouſe ellate amonge ſelfe make debate induſynge rancour diſcorde entre within ſhyppes borde agayne vlyxes worthy thelamon preſence kynge agamenon purpoſed hath playnely mattere tofore grekes anone ye ſhall sire quod ſo greue ſemeth iuſtly reaſon may meue touchyng ye winning getting towne golde richeſſe poſſeſſyowne fully delyuered taken hande treaſour founde londe whiche thincketh inward ſight ne hath ben departed halfe ryght amonge v iuſte deuyſyon ne egall dyſtribucion conſydered fyrſt tytle equyte euery wyght eſtate dignitie remembred eke howe ſharpe ſhoure worthyeſt meryte labour deſertes mortall ſtryfe grauntynge eueryche prerogatyfe lyke fortune hath deſerued ordre hath obſerued amonges v without excepcyon delyueraunce palladyon whiche vlyxes ſaye without drede tofore vniuſtly doth poſſede hym vſurpynge falſe opynyon merytorye retrybucyon apparence tytle grounde vnder pretenſe colour falſely founde relyke reioyſe ſhulde ryght ſleyght wonne rather myght vſurpeth maner vaunt gyuen vnto hym graunt echone chyefe guerdon wyll make replycation relyke hym mete whiche ſhall reioyſe quyete maye diſturbe hym lette cleyme duely dette guerdon conuenyent ye lyſte indifferent reaſon onely doth ſeme atwene v two egally deme iuſtly fyrſt euery circumſtaunce outher meryte weyed balaunce firſte conſydered forth fro day daye longe whyle ſyege laye ye ſhulde plentye vitayle ſyde fro myſchyefe fayle ¶and ſhall without auaunt breke armes knyghthode ſpeke fyelde longe continuaunce manly force perſeueraunce vpon foen ſo felle kene day daye armed clene nedeth make mencyon right hand ſlewe phylomene ye well knowe whiche kepynge yonge ſonne pryamus kynge freſhe luſty great fayreneſſe hym infynyte rycheſſe treaſoure golde paſſyngly plentye euery dele brought ye remembre lyſte take hede ye quyet indygence nede occaſyon great good manhode ſhed ye blode mercyles full cruell wyſe ſake kynge fryſe treaſour cofers ſought yfeare ſyege ybrought knyghthode ſyth go full yore haue eke augmented made grekes lande poſſeſſyons conqueſt onely two regyons prudence laboure sythen ye ſyege fyrſt begonne prouynces troye adiacent encreaſe ſo dyligent ¶and achylles worthy warryour ye experte full well laboure wrought auauntage ſythen ye ſo prudent ſage foryetell fully remembrynge nedeth reherſen euery thynge ¶and ſo diſpreue manly knyght tytle cleyme hath ryght dome cōmyttynge opynyons reherſayle condycyons nother hath manhode proweſſe force knyghthode nother hardyneſſe poynt haue rewarde darynge preued cowarde experyence hath ſhewed dede cometh nede worde wynde ſleyghty cōpaſſyng falſhode euer ymagynynge neuer yet daye preued thynge hym acheued whiche might entitled laude ende medlyd fraude vnder colour cure pretende fayre lyke paynted walle dyuerſe hewed nother hye lowe may man plaine mening know ¶and ſuche ſleyght cōpaſſed treaſon troye gat palladyon whiche great ſhame ſclaunder v conqueſt thus befalle treaſon haue cytye wonne knyghthode men reporte koune crop rote yf reherſe ſhall vlyxes grounde cauſe gynnynge fyrſte vnhappy fame reboundeth alder ſhame ſyth trouthe platly knowen wiſte tale ended demyth ye lyſte vlyxes aduertence conceyued hath great inpacyence thelamon great enuye feruent rancour melancolye ¶forbare fyrſt full great aduyſe full prudent ryght wiſe thought wolde make therof iape worde haſte ſhulde eſcape nother none vnbrydled countenaunce outwarde conceyued regardaunce ¶and abraydynge ſtable face syres quod ſo may haue grace vnder ſupporte hyghe preſence tale maye haue audyence nother doubte drede equytye ſhall poſſede palladyon durynge lyues daye maugre myght ſay naye yf ye lyſt reaſon ſe ſyege layde fyrſt cyte haue ſelfe double wiſe acquyt well knyghthod ſothly wyt counſell buſy cure ofre cauſe theyr diſcomfiture aye dylygent auauntage wrought compaſſed vnto theyr domage daye ſothe ne floured theyr felycytye theyr force contuned welfare trouth ſhall ſpare dempt loked reaſon moſt cauſe theyr confuſyon ſo euer agaynſt replye ¶how ofte went imbaſſadrye importable charge dyſpenſe treate aye concludynge ſentence forthrynge entenciowne diſencreaſe hindringe towne ſawe meane none myne aduyſe wittes euerichone force cyte win yt relyke within therupon ſo ſotylly wrought vnto palladyon brought thelamon malyce ſtriueth olde hatred vnto gilt aſcriueth hooly thinge yt haue wrought ¶but ye ſo prudent thought aduerteth wyſely ende maketh hande quarell fully taketh palladion iuſtly prouyde fauour let layde aſyde sith thinge ye platly vnderſtande let v demynge ſtande one aſſent ſo matter wende lo tale ende ¶then thelamon ire full feruent rancoure made inpacient enuye inwardely ameued vlyxes hath diſpyteouſly repreued onely malys hyghe diſdaine vlixes rebukyng agayne full bytterly without abode anone ſo twayne made full mortall foen preſence agamenon ¶but furyouſly ayax thelamon melancolye pale nothynge red thrette vlyxes ſhall dead handes ſhulde eſchewe grekes tho rancour remewe quarell put arbytration menclaye agamenon cauſed full mortall ſtryfe ſentence anone dyffynytyfe put vlixes poſſeſſyon perpetually thilke palladyon hym confyrmynge abyde ſtable cauſe fauourable vlyxes lyke guydo wryte ſo goodly hath hym quyte vnto heleyne gettynge towne beynge cauſe ſauaciowne diſpeyred lyfe drede grekes willynge haue dead prudent mediacyon maugre myght thelamon hath quene fro death preſerued albe ſhe ſame well deſerued grekes ſayde opynyon thus defrauded palladyon ye haue harde worthy knyght manhode great myght gan herte brede paſſynge enuye full great hatrede thought wolde auenged ſome day vpon vlixes menelay eke alſo vppon agamenon brake lyke wood lyon knightes yt ſtronge ſayd playnly great wronge dead woulde auenged ſpecyally ilke three therwithall furious wrothe tournyng backe anone goeth herte fret full mortall tene many greke quarell ſuſtene herte ſore gan dyſdayne agayne vlixes tother twayne full ware ſo euer falle knightes made aboute call gret ſtuffe wake ſlepe awayte manly kepe full good watche enuyron cloſe ¶but full erely ſonne aroſe worthy ayax bed vpryght ymurdred ſelfe ſame nyght albe blede morowe founde peces hewe many mortall wounde thyng cruell horryble god man lothſome odyble full many greke wofull morowe wepe ſe knyght ſo murdred ſlepe crye noyſe ran throughout hooſte anone fro man mā conſtreynt foule deede eueryche felte herte blede full deſyrous make ordynaunce murdre vengeaunce hauynge therof great ſuſpection menelay agamenon ¶but vlixes moſt ſpecyall comon voyce hym arrettynge foule fame myght aſterte ¶but pyrrhus moſt toke thyng hert makyng vowe furyous wood venged playnely bloud thelamon vpon vlixes heade hym manaſynge ſhalbe deade ſore hym frettynge ſorowe ¶but vlixes erly morowe dread pirrhus taken hath ſea ſhyppes faſte gan flee ¶but wente platly reade palladyon toke dyomede hauynge herte therof full great remorſe ¶and pirrhus taken hath corſe thelamon loue ſpecyall dyd make flawme funerall large great cole hote red amyddes feruent fyry glede full many greke ſtondynge beholde lette brenne aſhes colde ſtorye tolde cloſed vrne golde full reuerently hath ſhette thervpon hath prynte yſette armes curyouſly ygraue myſchyefe aſſhes ſaue ſent home great affection conſerued regyon kyng whyle lyue euery thynge perfourmed blyue rytes tho dayes vſed ¶ euer one pyrrhus hath ymuſed vpon murdre trayterouſly ywrought caſte ſhulde full dere abought pyteous death thelamon hauynge aye hate agamenon eke ſuſpecte olde menelay wayte eche laye makyng thē ſelfe knightꝭ ſtronge trye hath ryght wronge pyrrhus ne wolde let lyghtly gone thus made mortall fone ylke three platly death falſe enuy hertes ſleeth amonge thē ſelfe vntrue stryfe vpon ſtryfe gan euery day renewe debate multiplye tyll anthenor gan thynge eſpye wyſedome ſtynten diſdayne reconſyled vnto peace agayne cauſed accorde made ſolempne feaſt royall beſechynge full lowely al thre graunt hym therat gentylneſſe grekes myghte echone outwarde conceyue al alone feaſt goodly made calle writ guydo worthy grekes hye ne lowe none excepcion yf ſhulde make deſcrypcion howe lordes eſtates ſette ſundrye courſes gyftes great anthenor gaue euery ſyde longe abyde plente ſo great ſuffyſaunce ¶and fynde fell dalyaunce syttyng meate ſpeken enee brought hate enmite diſdaye ſhortely ſentence put hym many great offence ſpecyally haſty tene whylom concealed polycene ſleyght made withdrawe whiche cauſe achylles yſlawe shortly concludyng one opynyon fynall exyle troye towne notwithſtandyng graunt lyberte gyuen hym abyde cyte alſo longe hym lyſte deuyſe grekes haue adnulled fraunchyſe fro loweſt vp vnto meſte preſent hye feſte ¶but doubteleſſe well eſpye brought conſpyracye troye boke fynde saue hym ſelfe wytte anthenor ylyche falſe bothe one degre ye haue herde betrayſhynge cytye lyke ſpronge one roote whē knew ther none boote eneas dome modefye prayed courteſye leaſt graunten grace foure monthes myght haue ſpace make ſtuffe apparayle hym ſelfe puruey vytayle eke graunt hym wolde aſſent thylke ſhyppes parys went cytheron vnto temple olde nombre two twenty tolde full graunt petycyowne retourned home troye towne tryſte heuy ſe beholde waſte cytye walles olde ſorowe felte herte blede within hym ſelfe taketh hede remembred aduertence falſe treaſon great offence hym compaſſed towne aforne ſo ſodeynely hath lorne grace grekes ſtode diſconſolate whylom ſo great eſtate herte fully diſpeyred vnwarely ſo euyll apayred vnto grekes beyonde backe beynge vngylty without lacke whome coulde well deme saue ſygnes ſhulde ſeme anthenor moſte wyte caſte playnely wolde hym quyte towne made ſende blyue thilke fewe lefte alyue commynge anone commaundemente euerychone preſent sire quod ye ſe howe fortune towardes gynneth diſcontune aye vnſtable eyen blynde ye experte ſelfe fynde whilom frowarde tourned werſe clerkes called aduerſe lyſt cruelte ſhewe ſo ſtandeth ye fewe muſt parte ye ſtyll abyde ſo ye prouyde standynge alone deuoyde ſuccoure amonge ſelfe make gouernoure ſe beaute ſhalbe acloyed euery parte fynally deſtroyed ſely ſhepe ne reade diſparkled man doth thē leade wherfore beſt dredefull thynge one aſſent choſen kynge moſte able eſtate occupye aſſaulte manly guye anthenor knyghthode renowne accorde opynyowne wherfore haſte vnto entent without abode lette hym ſent comynge plainely towne vpon heade lette ſette crowne grauntynge ſcepter regalye wyſedome maye guye aſſaulte parturbaunce knyghthode prudent gouernaunce aſſent makyng delaye neuer one lyketh ſaye nay ryght gladde maner thynge ye haue herde make hym kynge ¶but full lyttle ſothly ſonde eneas meanyng vnderſtande ne mente treaſon falſehede howe entrynge ſhalbe dead full trayterouſly awayte lying ſlea hym falſely commynge anthenor nothyng ware dyſarmed came weapen bare eneas huge route ſwordes drawe ſet hym rounde aboute tyll troye yonge olde ran atwene manly hym holde knee fell mekely downe beſechynge hym haue compaſſyowne worthyneſſe alſo manlyhead lyke knyght taken hede howe lefte people bare beſechynge hym dredfull ſworde ſpare rancoure yre leue leſt ſlaughter wolde greue commō beſought rewe ſayth myne auctour miſchiefe ye londe founde ſonde almoſt death without remedye hym mynerua hath ſo great enuye ſo woodly temple wente caſſandra autur hente cruell force hatefull vyolence ¶lo peryll offence hye dyſpyte holy place doubte ſhall fayle grace ſo euer vſeth deede laſte god wyll quyte mede rewarde lyke dyſſerueth ſuch thyng many greke ſtriueth bycauſe onely ſuche occaſyon exemplefye preſumpcyon folyly attaine haue tolde agayne god ſo bolde shall repent ſooner weneth many man harme ne meneth suffreth vengeaunce treſpaſſe one fyrſte auctour goth quyte alone many offence abayth ceryouſly guydo wryt ſayth suynge ordre wofull auenture euery greke homewarde dyd endure hygh lowe ſparynge none eſtate holſome welfull ſome infortunate woo welfare ryght fell ſtorye ſhall declare grece whylom worthy kyng manly ryche prudent lyuynge ſoth lyke wryte guydo tyme worthy ſonnes two pallamydes eldeſt brother oetes called tother bothe twayne one mother borne ſtorye reherſed hath toforne pallamydes noble knyght full famous eke power myght fer ſpoke many ſundrye coſte alſo grekes hooſte wyſedome whylom gouernayle ¶but ala ſlayne battayle vnhap martys cruell tene whan ſonne ſhone moſt bright ſhene knighthode worthyneſſe lyke tofore ſtory beareth witneſſe death doth playnely ſpecyfye ¶but nowe malyce hatrede enuye ſuch haue tunges infortunate make onely kinge naulus debate grekes contriued haue newe hye treaſon falſe full vntrewe ī ſoth neuer wrought effecte ymagined thought falſe thinge yfeyned malyce ¶that kinge ſo manly ſo wyſe ſo prudent pallamides shulde enuye god wot cauſeles ſiege troye cyte vpon night falſly murdred ſlaughter lothſome dede vlixes diomede fully wrought ye haue herde deuiſe whiche euery herte ought agryſe ¶this falſe alſo tale haue fayned king naulus haue traiterouſly cōplained albe dede neuer mente grekes alſo aſſent murdre conſpyration menelay agamenon albe ſoth euery dele falſe hanged hye halfe tale ſo forge contryue make frendes cauſeles ſtryue fraude falſe colluſyon kynge naulus put ſuſpection grekes conſpyred doubtles vpon murdre pallamydes makyng ground fayne fro troye ſent letter twayne pallamydes immediatly directe whiche concluded treaſon effecte howe hyghe eſtate falſely allyed confederate troye ſumme golde haue fayned ytolde howe cytye good receyued huge quantite fyne onely grekes betraye prolonge platly delaye ſyege gettynge towne engyne medyacygwne confirme ſentence make naulus gyue full credence ſayd playnely confuſyowne letter yt ſent fro towne yfounde encloſed ſhielde vpon knyght yſlayne fyelde comprehendynge hole trecherye treaſon full confederacye ¶atwene towne pallamydes veryly though gyltles gyue open euydence make prefe great offence ¶they ſayde vlyxes affyrmyng certayne accorded chaumberleyne offyce pallamydes wonder ſecrete nothynge reckeles aſſente conſpyracye wrongly compaſſed brennynge hote enuye behotynge guerdon great mede lyke deuiſe execute dede take treaſour ſumme good full ſecretly knit hode hid voyded preſe vnder bedde pallamides put grekes ſuerte treaſour ſame quantyte ne might denyed lyke letter ſpecyfyed ¶and founde knowe throughout hooſt noiſed yblowe letter golde alſo fro poynt poynt accordynge two kinge aſſentinge treſowne receyued troye towne aſſented ye haue herde tell grekes tho longer would dwell ſhope theym forth one entente haſte came vnto tente kinge full innocent clene litell knewe would mene ¶but vpon full knightly ſtode theyr yre furyouſly wood venged loude gan crye maye man theyr malice modefye ſo merciles finde moſt ſpecyall kinge menelay agamenon onely meued indignacion would haue proceded vnto iudgemtnt haſty rancour without auyſement treaſon auenged notwithſtandinge al hie degre ſothneſſe worthy kinge conceyued hath malice workinge firſt aſtoned inwarde ſyght ſodaynly ſtert vplike knight wiſe worthy pallamides hardy lyon amid preſe nothinge agaſte knightly gan expreſſe playnly ſayde would refuſe acquite ſelfe mortall caſe acceptynge ſo worthy byrth bloud hye kinred al deuoyding knighthod māhed gaue life death forſe tofore theim ieoparde corſe within felde theim liſt ordeyne like knight quarel dareyne liſt durſt vndertake exception liked none make hye lowe ſo bolde proue reaſon haue tolde beſechynge make delaye prolonge ſame daye manly requiringe maye haſte yt falſly thinge compaſte aunſwere ſtoned echone hooſt one hardy ſhal fayne chaump cloſe quarell dareyne nother vlixes yet dyomede chefe worker foule dede vlixes cuſtomabe euery thynge deceyuable double worke aye full deceyt lyke ſerpent lyeth awayte vnder floures gan ſo glide trace right ſo vlixes fayned face yt ſawe knightly hye proweſſe manly cheare hardineſſe high renowne pallamides anone falſhed put ſelfe preſe like frende mente wele brotyll glaſſe pretendinge outwarde ſtele one fyrſt gan excuſe theim counſaylinge longer muſe matter theyr alder eaſe crafte gan ſo appeaſe touchinge rumoure hye treaſon hath voyded ſuſpection theyr hertes concludinge certayne accuſynge made vayne conſpyred onely hatrede albe ſelfe roote dede ¶but ſawe myght acheue ye haue herde worthy kinge greue ſpot treaſon laye hath anone founde waye aſſente fully dyomede vnder pretence playnly frendlyhed comynge hym agayne certayne nyght vnder ſuraunce true knyght counſayle kepe either ſote ſoure enfourmynge great treaſoure golde good infynite rycheſſe diſcured vnder ſecretnes whyche ſothly man dyd knowe hyd incloſed well lowe within felde litell beſyde hym lyſt fro hym hyde truſte vnto hym dyſcure would buſy cure ſame nyght wyth go vnto well thre mo fette away great ſumme good ſothe nothynge vnderſtode mente aſſented anone ſo thre togyther gone vnto well lyke haue tolde moſt manly bolde pallamydes lyke telle deſcended lowe well suppoſynge haue treaſour founde ala hym falſly confounde haue murdred wt ſtones great huge botome hauynge refuge whē accomplyſhed theyr entēt repeyred eueryche tent tale ſtory telleth v feyned kinge naulus touchinge death pallamides theim deſclaunder giltles vlixes wyth dyomede innocent platly reade grekes nigh ferre ſlayne knightly werre durynge ſiege parys arowe falſe fayne ful narowe finde tale neuer yet thought treaſon yt ſhould haue wrought touchinge letter ſent towne ſuch conſpyracyowne grekes wrought fable vnſothe falſly feyned make naulus wroth vlyxes dyomede alſo agamenon grekes mo lette theym homewarde theyr waye hyndre alſo ſaye repayre theyr regyons naulus occaſyons oetes ſonne manly man accorded maye one aſſente auenge mercyles cruell murdre pallamides ordayne theyr home paſſage worke fully theyr domage grekes muſt neceſſitye homewarde ſale foreby countre wherfore kinge ſhapen hath wyle hylles hye lytell yle winter ſeaſon euery maner nyght make fyres ſette vp lyght cauſe theim ſea erre grekes ſawe fyre ferre vnware harme caſt theim lande could peryll vnderſtande ſhope theyr ful myght ariue faſt lyght wherwith ij hundred ſhippes brake amonge rockes fully go wrake drowned many worthy mā thus vengeaunce alderfyrſt began kinge naulus hath grekes take deadly hate ſonnes ſake great miſchiefe confuſyon grekes nauye agamenon great perill death eſcaped almoſt amonge beiaped erles duke worthy kinges crowned trayne ſea drowned menelay alſo dyomede eſcaped miſchefe reade daunger gone oetes wood ire anone herte ſhope wile thought would agamenon begile compaſſynge ful mortall ſtryfe let ſende letter anone wife mighty great agamenon whych chere included falſe treaſon euen lyke yf ſhall lye thus effecte dyd ſpecyfye ¶fyrſt lorde agamenon kinge ſyege wrought wonder thynge preiudyce ſlaundre name albe maner blame lyke wrote platly treſpace knyghtly honour folly difface ¶this ſaye guydo telleth thus loued doughter kynge pryamus beaute wyfe take herte fynally forſake worthy quene whilom great fame clemeſtra ſothly name wonder ſemely ryght fayre dyſcent borne ſtocke royall cellynge eke excellence albe ſhe neuer dyd offence yet lorde newfangilneſſe toke letter expreſſe fully purpoſe anone repayre though clemeſtra good fayre ſodaynly exyle lande many thouſande myle warning ſhe prudente ſubſtaunce ſentemente oetes wrote vnto quene albe kynge innocente clene fore liuinge louyng true maner thinge pleaſe paſſyng ententyfe worde dede durynge lyfe fer oughte reſon deſyred letter falſly conſpyred haue put parcaſe innocence gyue haſty credence ¶thankynge firſte oetes trouthe ſo goodly hym lyſt haue routhe vpon wronge hygh compaſſyon yet ſtorye maketh mencion afterwarde ſhall deſcriue ſhe faleſt one alyue vnto lorde longe abſence haſte ſhe made ſtronge diffence agayne thinge gan purueye ſuche fraude ſhe ne deye worke ſothe ſhe wyte whych ala muſt anone endyte ſtory platly doth lere whych doleful mortall heare oh vnſure truſte worldly glorye wt ſodayn chaunge put memorye oh ioye vnſtable vayne ambycyon vnware tourne reuerſed vp ſo downe oh ydell fame blowe vp ſkye ouer whelmed twincklinge eye oh pompe oh boſte tryumphe victorye lyke ſhadowe waſte tranſytorye oh fortune falſe vnaſſured man maye fully lured hygh lowe maner eſtate bonde fayth conferate agayne whoſe myght mā may diffēd tourne ſhall diſcende ſyt hyeſt thyne vnſtable whele thy brotyll fauour forged ſtele meynt allyed mutabylytye welfulneſſe falſe felicitye ſodayn ſweygh frowarde yu canſt auale freſhe chere anger pale hygh diſdayne thou ſpareſt degree prince duke higheſt ſee mighty kinges worthy emperours richeſt reygne theyr royal floures sceptre crowne yu canſt pul downe ¶i take wytneſſe agamenowne ſo noble myghty lyue ſondry auctours hie renowne deſriue ſothfaſtly excellence might make diffence knightes baner ſewe conſpyred murdre voyde eſchewe reſcuſe none could make ala fele pen quake doth mine inke blotte boke oh mighty god wt thine inwarde loke seeſt euery thing thrugh thy eternal might wilt thou equit ryght puniſhe chaſtice ſo horrible thinge ſpecyally murdre kinge ala payne ixion hell mane sathan dwell egall equipolent venge murdre ſufficient excedeth compariſon al felonye falſhed treaſon wherfore oh lord ſeeſt knoweſt thy power eternall suffre ſuche liue vpon grounde worſe tygre cerberus hounde chayned lyeth bounde hel gate whych malyce playnly though hate berketh fyrſt offence murdre gladly wrought ſylence men aduerte take kepe ¶alas prince ſley ſlepe pyllowe ſlepeth ſofte cryeth wreche hye god alofte axeth vengeaunce take faſt though abyde wyll laſte ala kynge ſpoken ſo ferre ſo worthy outwarde werre cruell fate paſſynge odyous dyſpoſed hath owne houſe mortall ende execute agaynſt whych refute ryght ſhyp lande ſette quene clemeſtra ye ſtrond mette humble cheare loke full beninge ſhewed full many faythful ſygne wyſely trouthe countenaunce albe herte varyaunce perceyued playnly face kynge goodly embrace ſothe trouth mente paleys hye waye wente aduertynge treaſon ſhape whych ala might eſcape falſhede could nothinke fele ne maye longer conſele agayne lorde clemeſtra wrought bond wedlocke ſhe ne thought trewe loke ſothly ſpouſayle agayne malyce lytell myght auayle vnto lorde trouthe conſerue newfangilneſſe cauſed ſterue olde fayth aſſuraunce loue abode fykell chaunce longe abſence herte apalled loued one egiſtus called afore grace ſtode nother byrth bloud lytell nought reputacyowne renowmed manhode renowne knyghthod hygh proweſſe laboure buſyneſſe good awayte vpon nyght therfore beſt furthred ſyght dread ſhe lyue alone sorowles ſo well ſhe could grone ſaye life ſhe ladde except ſhe doughter exyona guydo ſayth ſhe hight vnto clemeſtra behyght aſſuringe vpon payne head ſhulde raygne lorde dead enhaſte concluſyon worthy lorde kynge agamenon next nyght murdred yſlayne falſe egiſtus quene full fayne longer bode ſtorye lere haſte wedded yfere falſe ſleyghty compaſſynge meſſene ſhe made crowned kynge put full poſſeſſyon ¶alas ſynne hath dominacion wronge abate ryght worlde falſhed hath ryghte full ofte ſyth hath ryghtwiſeneſſe eſtate ſette worthyneſſe lo ſynne auoutrye brought murdre conſpyracye synne vpon ſynne lynked twayne embraced fendes chayne perpetually hell endure ala ſhall ſelfe full aſſure fro cruell murdre body withdrawe kinges theyr bedde ſlawe whiche bringeth alyenacyon extorte tytle falſe ſucceſſyon maye coloure pretenſe ſeme full ſtreyghtly god ſhall deme iuſtly venge due recompence intruſyon brought violence felly quyte ſuche horryble thinges ſodayne ſlaughter ſpecially kinges greatly dread euery regyon ¶and fynde agamenon clemeſtra falſe double quene ſonne paſſynge faire ſene right gracious euery mannes ſyght horeſtus boke ſayth hyghte wonder ſemely yonge age great feare mortall rage leſt ſlayne dread anul tytle ſuccede preſerue ſhent kinge taltibus power hath ſente ful ſecretly countree vnto kinge called ydume helde ſceptre royall ſete full mightely lande crete carkaſis named quene doughter called eke climene borne heyre regyon made eke mencyon horeſtes reken thynge quene alſo kinge cheriſhed well ſtorye lere climena theyr owne doughter deare eke kepte cherte fro poynt poynt lyke degre attendaunce conuenyent dewe eſtate euer vpon ſewe ſuch moſt experte ſage gouerne tyll came age reioyce god gaue might heritage whych right clere diſcent happy chaunce thus leue vnder gouernaunce yonge ſonne agamenon muſt make dygreſſyon fro matter tell diomede auentures guydo rede wofull fate paynes ſmerte whych ala might aſterte remembred playnly writynge oetes ſonne riche kinge called naulus ye haue herde toforne heuyneſſe herte hath borne vnto grekes repeyringe home fro troye luſt inwarde ioye hyndre high lowe cauſe vnknowe ſo paſſynge enuyous thought ylyke deſyrous might ſothly le death venge pallamides lyke tofore ſtorye deuyſe ſo prudent ſo wyſe oetes malice wrought trayterouſly new meane ſought might maner waye diomedes vnwarely deſtroye thinge caſt fayle ceryouſly make reherſayle grece kingedome wide large coniunct one calidonye arge full habundaunt rycheſſe rente kinge called pollente worthy man noble fame ſonne aſſandrus name doughter paſſinge fayre ſyght ſothly egra finde ſhe hyght father like wryte guydo mo theſe child two hath wiſedome ſo prouided mighty reygne deuyded atwene theim two deceaſe eche parte lyue peace exclude fro indigence nede ſhe wyfe vnto diomede albe tofore ſtorye ſayde whilom loued one cryſayde ſaye doubilneſſe well wote guydo beareth wytneſſe boke ſothly ſayth none aſſandrus owne wiues brother full luſty freſhe ful manlyhead troye went dyomede ſea fordriuen vp ſo downe riued vp regyon called boece diſconſolate tempeſt driue wery full mate refreſhe none thinge lande thelephus kinge whoſe riuayle whan herde ſayne herte high diſdayne bolde ſo great offence entre grounde hauinge licence yet ſothe domage high lowe maner age toke nought might diſauayle vnto lande vytayle payde iuſtly fine fleſhe fyſhe bread wine yet indignaciowne kinge thelaphus deſcended downe great array harme thē might ſo gan bicker fight aſſandrus full high proweſſe like lion fomen gan oppreſſe wonder knyghtly felde vpen thē wā ſlewe daye many worthy man hygh courage manly pryde kinge whiche ſtode aſyde sawe men ſlayne euery parte hygh dyſdayne hent anone darte caſte hym ala mortall fate perced hathe mayles plate aſſandrus fel downe dead ſoyle bloud redde deadly wounde ſo began blede wood tygre tho came dyomede hym auenge bare hym lyke knyght sleeth kylleth put vnto flight ſuch ſorowe gan make knyghtly routh brother ſake ne wyſt beſt finde myd wo beaſt foule dead corp ſaue like eſtate let make graue buryed hym rite olde ¶but oetes ſyſter tolde ſlayne fraude dyomede fyne myght full poſſede reygne arge hole without ſtryfe wyth purpartye annexed hys wyfe death myght ſeaſon take tolde eke ſhe forſake fayre egra womanhead lorde callled dyomede tolde hell chayned ouermore forged hath fained enuye aſſandrus loſt lyfe lorde hath take wyfe dyſhonour ſhame paſſyngly great ſclaunder name preiudyce ydone eſtate tolde make debate lyke wrote concluſyon clemeſtra agamenon whych herte made ſore greue put fully byleue treaſon ye haue herde tolde yre ſhe pale colde vnkyndneſſe ſo herte ſleeth heuyneſſe brother death neuer yet guydo doth aſſure woman loued better creature ſhe loued hym maner age fyrſt nought ſhe ſet herytage comparyſon brother lyfe lo oetes made newe ſtryfe ye haue herde ſtorye rede gyltles worthy dyomede hath longe ſyege layne kingdom would haue come agayn migyhty hande worthy quene lyeges aſſented bene exyled regyon may made medyacyon thus ſelfe mate dyſpeyred dyſconſolate agayne repeyred salerne londe great rycheſſe tenter worthyneſſe wyth crowne sceptre reygned longe wyth hys lyeges hys knyghtes ſtronge brother ayax thelamon murdred tofore made mencyon dyomede pore deſtytute maye salerne fynde refute whan tenter firſt gan eſpye ſewed hym full great enuye hauynge hym aye ſuſpection touchynge death kynge thelamon ¶but dyomede certayne nyghte full ſecretely hath taken flyght fro salerne faſt gan hym hye hope fynde better remedye helpe ſocour ſome place fortune wolde graunte hym grace hym ſelfe aſhamed confuſe man forſake abiecte refuſe ryght ſo fared wandrynge fro ne wyſt beſt bvt fynde troyan eneas ſtill troye onely routh compaſſyowne ſupport thē left towne beynge alway theyr life doubte theyr fomen rounde beſet aboute lyued lacke hede contynually myſchyefe dread knowing refute cōfort caſe tyll counſell eneas ſupporte theym great nede ſent haſte dyomede knowynge full well deſolacyon proſcrypt fro regyon beſechynge hym manhode routhe enhaſte wythout ſlouthe ſtuffe get ſouldyers alſo manly euery man without abode troye lede ſuccoure great nede ¶and dyomede came taryed nought theyr requeſt beſought releue ſharpe ſhoure wyth hym brought many ſouldeour eneas waye mette frendly wyſe towne hym fette made paſſyngly great chere gan commune yfere theyr auentures lande ſea entermedled great aduerſyte man maye deuoyde eſchewe take parte dewe ſorte hap doth brydell lede ſtorye ſhortly procede cely troyans almoſt ſhent theyr fomen yles adiacent theim beſette aboute enuyrowne manhod hye renowne dyomede ſouldeours knyghtes noble werreours reſkued holpen vtterly foure dayes fought knyghtly wyſe defendynge cytee proweſſe alſo enee ſlewe toke withſtode diffence troyanyſhe bloud suche fonde cytye falſe hange vp hye halſe punyſhed theyr great wronge ¶and dyomede thus gan wexe ſtronge longe proceſſe made mencyon chiefe protectour troye towne enuye none large ſpace durſt abyde grace lygeaunce ſo made loute thus name ſprede gan aboute fame great opynyon dylated vnto regyon ſwifte reporte calydonye arge quene greatly gan charge aſtoned taketh hede power gan might dreade leſt would lande vpon wynne knighthod werre newe begynne ſecretly gan muſe thinge lorde myghty kynge late exyled yput flyght hath grace founde fortune ſyght remonuted high eſtate wherof ſhe ſelfe checke mate wayes caſte prudent hole aduyſe parliament without grutchynge rebellyon reuoke regyon ¶and therupon lowly ſente letter meſſager forth went cauſe annullyng exiled fully reconſyled hole aſſent lyeges ful lowly euerychone call theyr offence theyr treſpace without rygour grace anone like manly knyght mercy ſothly ryght hath theyr ſonde well conceyued theyr meninge fully apparceyued ſtynte ſtrife thought beſt goodly wiſe graunt theyr requeſte reigne within certayne daye repeyred full riche arraye whoſe comynge full glad liege bene reconſiled quene rancour olde offence onely wiſedome put ſuſpenſe one herte bliſful life lede troye booke hym reade let liue felycytee agayne reſortynge tell ene hath tyme ſpent fro troye wt many troyan went ſhippes ſtuffed meyne ſayled forth many ſtraunge ſea many daunger many ſtrayte paſſage tofore aryued cartage ledinge father anchiſes waye finde le wife crewſa fatall auenture wo dyd endure ſo liſt ceryouſly ſene falſhede quene meane dido womanhead floure gaue rycheſſe treaſoure iewelles golde al yt mighte pleaſe euery thing might eaſe ¶but vnkinde reade eneydos ye ſhall fynde howe falſly ſtale awaye nyghte tyme ſhe bedde laye conqueſt alſo ytayle hadde many ſtronge battayle auentures workes fyne fall ye maye ſe ſoueraygne ſtyle fro poynt poynt compyled virgile wryte made ſythen go full yore troye boke ſpeaketh ¶but procedeth ſhall endyte horeſtes caſte quyte father death playnly ſpare ye lyſt heare guydo doth declare requyred equit right iudge moſt myght egally holdeth balaunce death conſpyred vengeaunce voyce bloud doth ſo aye contune crye wreche clamour importune ſothe iniuſtly ſhede murdre wrought wil haue egall mede guerdon hath deſerued maye fle iudgement reſerued ſit higheſt trone beholdeth ſelfe alone full rightfully noble mighty kinge though ſuffer forget nothinge conſydreth inſpectyon murdre agamenon mighty lorde yt moſt ſoueraygne good made mynyſtre ſame bloud yonge horeſtes full high proweſſe execute dome ryghtwiſeneſſe gaue grace power might anone toke ordre knyght ydumeus like tolde foure twentye wynter olde freſhe luſtye wonderly prudent inwardly deſyrous intente fortune would ſayne heritage recure agayne ¶which egiſtas falſly hym denyeth crowne vniuſtly occupyeth falſe tytle wife ¶but horeſts ieoparde lyfe auenture laſteth breth fyrſt venged father death vpon tho treaſon wrought alderfyrſt full lowly beſought ¶kinge ydinne goodlyhead great nede ¶and kinge benignely anone aſſigned hath gone thouſand knightes manly right ſtrōge redreſſe great horrible wronge egiſtus wrought violence wiſdome dyligence horeſtes gan ſo purueye within ſeye gat ſtorye lye thouſande companye worthy knightes one accorde go wt theyr ſoueraygne lorde euery thinge biddinge obeye ye haue herde egiſtus werrey ¶and thus horeſtes full riche arraye gan hooſte made delaye lodginge alderfyrſt gan cheſe citye called troyeſe receyued great reuernece kinge named forence manly knyght bookes ſpecifye bare herte paſſinge great enuye egiſtus double occaſion fyrſte death agamenon eke doughter deare inwardly entere good fayre yonge age whilom giuen mariage egiſtus doubilneſſe falſe treſon newfangilneſſe kinges doughter hath vtterly forſake haſte libell make forge writ repulſyon albe hadde trewe occaſyon egiſtus forſoke saue falſſy wiue toke quene clemeſtra agayne al right law aſſent murdred haue ſlawe agamenon afore tolde whylom ſo myghty ſo bolde hatefull falſe conſpyraſye well murther auoutrye venge bothe dewe recompence worthy knyght ye mighty kyng forence offred horeſtes make hym ſtronge go hym helpe venge wronge hym ladde armed bryght ſtele foure hundred knightes horſed wonder wele takynge fyelde manly chere ſo horeſtes kynge yfeare ryden forthe many manly man ¶but horeſtes werre gan bryght phebus bole ſhone temple full lowly gone goddes moſt beſt wyſe humble herte dyd ſacryfyce fully hope better fare bode lyfe deth ſpare without mercy remyſſyon death venge agamenon ¶on clemeſtra moſte wyte make fyrſte ſworde byte mother handes twayne ouermore buſy payne without pytye mercye ſhewe ſmale peces tyll ſhe hewe diſmembred ſonder ioynt fro ioynt eke yet poynt iuſtly punyſhe rycoure ryght ¶egiſtus eke falſe vntrewe knyght ſlowe neclygent execute commaundement goddes lyſte falle ¶and horeſtes knyghtes ¶and forenſes mighty kynge alſo one herte ſyege go cyte called methene within whiche falſe quene clemeſtra god gyue herde grace horeſtes ſyeged hath place knyghtes ſet rounde aboute ¶falſe egiſtus yryden gather men wreke falle vpon ſyege breke ¶if myght maner ſyde great ſtuffe thus gan ryde takynge vp men fro euery coſte tyll hym made full myghtye hooſte ¶but horeſte whiche ſyege laye gouernaunce eſpyeth daye daye ſent men full ſage ſtoppe wayes lette paſſage made knyghtes full huge route purſue hym euery coſte aboute ſyege manfully begonne aſſaute hath towne ywonne entred nyght full late ſette wardes ſtronge euery gate doungeon moſt ſtronge princypall buildyng myghty royall horeſtes fyrſte mother fonde ¶the quene clemeſtra lady lande whiche drede ſore gan quake mercyles anone made take put chaynes tyll next morowe ¶and egiſtus god gyue hym euyll ſorowe ſtuffe myght accroche towarde towne faſte gan aproche ¶in purpoſe full horeſtes greue within ſodeynely releue ſothe myght auayle cytye myght abayle horeſtes knightes vnwarely haue mette attones proudely hym ſette fyrſte ſlewe men put flyght ¶and taken hym maugre myght chaynes lyke hym fynde mercyles full faſt bynde ſhet hym vp fetryd pryſowne falſe founde towne aſſented wyllinge helpynge murdre worthy kynge grekes worker conſpyratours agayne lorde ryfynge traytours take bounde rycour ſame nyghte ſhet vp toure tyll morowe lyke lot drawe eueryche vnder fonge lawe lyke decerte excepcion none nyght paſſed gone phebus roſe eſtwarde ſphere toures ſhone full bryght clere ¶when clemeſtra rote falſehede brought forth quakyng drede ¶before horeſtes iudgement yfet ſworde ſharpe kene ywhet like goddes charged toforne peces ſmale hath ſhorne made bere townes boūdes voured beaſtes houndes pytye none breſte reſerued quit fully ſhe hath deſerued fro poynt poynt forgat right nought thē chayned egiſtus furth brought iuſtly dempt rigour lawe herdell naked drawe towne might ſe hye hanged tre rot drye agaynſt ſonne lo murdre hath guerdon wonne lo falſhed mayſter awake ¶and traytours towne ytake galowes enhanged euerychone tyll ſeuered aſonder bone fro bone hye hill agayne ſterres ſhene thus ye towne fro treaſon purged clene trouth augmented ymored reygne horreſtes full reſtored ſtorye ſewinge ſhall expowne daye toke crowne myſt euery cloudy ſkye falſe treaſon conſpyracye tried vpon euery ſyde falſhed hadde place abyde ſtorye ſayth ordre reherſynge ſame time menelay kinge ſea ful wawes wete fro troyewarde yriued crete frely eſcaped many dread peyne quene goodly freſhe heleyne cauſe ſhe ſo famous fayre great pres meruaylous repaire fro euery parte beaute beholde troye walles ful olde deſtroyed noble royall towne many man ful worthy renowne hath loſt life may man ſay naye heleyne wife menelay thinge done may none kinge knewe fully brother agamenon murdre euerydele full triſt liked nothinge wele inwardly felte ful great ſmerte ¶and neuewe alſo herte meane horreſtes ſo mercyles like tyraunt graceles mother ſlewe pytye mortall yre crueltye fully caſte would bline ſceptre crowne platly depriue full afferminge mortall caſe lawe vnworthy father reygne heyre poſſede iuſtly conſydred horrible dede one furyous wroth without abode vnto ſhip goth melancolike great tene crete ſaylinge athene toke lande ſhippes borde duke neſtor gouernour lord receyueth like gentyll knyghte power diligence myght menelay rancour great heat gan duke ſecretly trete fynde meane inward ſyght ¶for depriue horreſtes right therupon haue iudgement athene holde parliament lordes regyon giue theron diffinicion whych ſhewed openly ynough horreſtes owne mother ſlough maner great offence ſelfe tho beynge preſence thinge fully eſpye partye gan agayne replye felte frely large alledginge charge goddes ſhortly declare mortall ſworde ne ſpare vpon clemeſtra roote falſe treaſon ſlewe lorde kinge agamenon murdre malice wrought wherfore horreſtes humbly beſought lordes manly herte equit conſydre aduerte malice rancour rage depriue heritage sith ſonne agamenon borne heyre regyon ye haue herde called methene albe mother clemeſtra quene compaſſed deſtruction ¶but duke neſtor ymeued reaſon ſuſtaynynge horeſtes ryght roſe vp anone lyke manly knyght offrynge hym ſelfe proudely ſake hye quarell vndertake body death darreyne lyſt tytle withſeyne ¶but none companye durſte worde agayne hym replye hoole ſtode opynion knyghtly mediacyon bare hym ſo feynynge nothynge horeſtes ycrowned kyng meneſte beynge aſſent whan diſſolued parlement horeſtes lyeges trewe receyued crowne newe treate lordes many one kyng menelay made attone gan ire rancour lete ¶and ydume worthy kynge crete prudently gouerneth mattere hermyone yonge doughter dere ¶of menelay quene heleyne yonge ſo freſhe beaute ſouerayne ywedded without taryinge horeſtes yonge luſty kynge bycauſe allyaunce deuoyded rancour diſtraunce atwene kynges menelay olde horeſtes ryght nowe tolde thus leue beſte eche reygne lyue peace reſte ſtryfe ceaſed caſe ¶but erygona doughter egiſtus ye haue herde telle ſorowe drede lyſte longer dwelle toke rope lyſt nothynge ſpare therwithall gan ſelfe gnare ſtorye ſayth hye vpon tree fyne ye gette wyll forth ceryouſly entreate ſtorye telle great oh vlixes ordre wrytynge thyne auentures come rynge full wonderfull londe ſea entermedlyd great aduerſytye guydo fyrſte deſcryuynge thy repayre saith thou founde wether foule fayre nowe agreable thonder ſowne ſtyll ſmoth wt cloudes frowne ſayth alſo thou dyddeſt ordeyne thy paſſage myghty ſhyppes twayne apparayled marchandyſe thou myghteſt moſt ſecrete wyſe euery myſchyefe ſea eſcape ¶but thou haddeſt felle iape auctour thy reſorte doth wryte ſayth vlyxes wordes whyte yrobbed rycheſſe good contraryous wynde ſo agayne hym ſtode dryue confuſyon myghty ſtronge regyon thelamon reygned lyue hent take blyue ¶by myghtye hande ſeaſed breſt mercyles put vnder areſt hym ſuſpecte workynge touchynge murther ſame kynge ſo wrought ſleyghty wyle tale ſette ſuche ſtyle playnly hath iaped fro hande frely eſcaped excepte queynt fare treaſour ymade full bare paſſage hym vnkouth fell agayne wolfe mouthe veryly ſpecyfyed kynge naulus men haue hym efte eſpyed take bounde chayned mercyles murther kynge pallamydes ¶but ſtorye reherſeth certayne prudence ſcaped agayne expert wyſe olde although maner fully tolde eſcape buſy peyne daunger theſe kynges twayne tyll fortune came fro miſchefe fre preſence kyng ydume ſymple arraye torne apparayle wherof kynge greatly gan meruayle ſe pouert ſo lowe manere made hym good chere though tyme ye infortunate hym receyueth lyke eſtate twayne alone complayninge vlixes made mone vnto kinge ful ſage ceryouſly ſorte paſſage face ſad ſobre cheare fro poynt poynt anone ye ſhall heare ¶my lorde quod ſhortly expreſſe truſte haue gentylneſſe ſhall auentures reherſe ryght fall firſte troye lande forſoke water wyth ſhippes toke anone winde peceably blowe yle vnknowe ¶called mirma great habundaunce thynge pleaſaunce maye ſiluer golde bought redy founde wanted ryght nought abode full longe ioye treaſour gat troye ſhyppes ſtuffed men ſafe ſounde commodyte ylke grounde lyked ſo countre enuyron diſporte recreacyon taryinge thought ful lōge man dyd vnto v wronge tyll daye eyer ſtyll winde alſo fully wyll ſayled quyete peace vnto porte called clauſtafages wherwyth meyne longe many daye founde thinge accordynge paye wether luſty agreable fayre maye truſte winde ayre vpon fayth ſmothe ſkye agayne ſhyppe faſte gan hye taryed nought toke anone ſea smothe calme enduringe dayes three wether founde lacke ſodaynly heauen tourneth blacke hidous tempeſt wawes grene hope haue dyſpeyred clene troubled ſpyrite made ſo penſife without refute eſcape lyfe toſſed driuen many ſundrye yle tyll laſte caſte vp cecyle recuringe lande great annoye payne tyme reygned kynges twayne remembre doubtles tone theim called sorygines whiche vnto full contrarious ¶and tother named coclopas brother byrthe concluſion ylike cruell condycyon though ſorte ſhape none ¶both twayne fell attones oppreſſinge full great dyſtreſſe spoyled ſhippes treaſour richeſſe pyte liked ſpare till lefte deſtitute bare good ala mortall chaunce moſt greuaunce whē golde may reſtrayne ſent downe mighty ſones twayne ¶alipham ful large longe ¶and polipheme ye mighty gianut ſtronge mē auenge thē wereful fame haue hundred ſlayne diſarayed ſtande diffence malice ſodayne violence toke miſchiefe almoſt lorne ¶and alphenor mine owne brother ſworne hatefully haue v founde chaynes caſte ſtockes bounde ylocked priſon make platly mencyon mighty man great polypheme ſyſter ſhortly deme one fayreſt euer yet borne might beaute ſo ſet aforne nature gaue ſuche prerogatife cleane mayde ſothly wyfe flouringe fayreneſſe bounte alphenor ſe albe fetred priſon loue loſte wit eke reaſon wex al mad ſo narowe ſhe binde saue vpon alway minde cloſed aye perillous wounde ſixe monethes thus laye bounde ¶both ſaye platte trouthe til polipheme vpon v routhe grace mediacion quit v fre pryſon ſhewed v mercy pite ſorowe great humanite ¶but alphenor ylike one entente bronde cupide brent felte parte many mortall fit till ſo wrought ſotyll wit night leef lothe ſtale mayde waye gothe helpe men hym time ¶but morowe houre prime ¶poliphemus gan v ſewe whoſe mighty hande might eſchewe ſuche aſſaulte v gan make force haue mayde take ¶from alphenor mauger rage polipheme vnto domage knightes ſo ſore vpon laye might vnneth ſcape awaye ſaue ſelfe compaſſed enuyron death purſewed champyon ſawe gayne fle death ſhortly ſayne giaunt moſt fierſly ſet ſworde eye ſmet vnto ſhip companye fled haſte man might eſpye ¶where became alphenor fere wawes gan clere gracious winde gan v awake countre haue anone forſake holſome v abyde man like write ouide ¶poliphemus giaunt dread eye amid forhead vlixes ſmote ſtroke like browes branched oke heyre longe berde loke child aferde loſt ſyght amonge hilles runneth daye night rage finde ſome refuge caſte rockes great ſtones huge euery parte enuyron countre vlixes auenged thus ſayth ouide concluſion boke tranſformacion metamorphoſeos ye maye ſe ſo euer leyſer ceriouſly ſtorye reade writinge forth procede vlixes face dead pale ydume tolde forth tale reherſinge thus ſuppriſed awaked fro polipheme eſcaped vnhappe infelicyte yle middes ſea driue gan night elidiū litell kingedome hight circe great enchauntreſſe thilke time lady goddeſſe could crafte ſo wonderly ꝑfourme ſodaynly man tranſforme haue likneſſe leſe reaſon horſe bere tygre lyon wolfe liſt deuiſe dreadful crafte ſhapen ſuch wiſe mighty ſtraunge pocions letuaries confection ſhe alſo ſo fayre vpon ſe tho power man might fle worke ſorcereſſe ſo founced vpon fayreneſſe fynally thus ſtode yeare abode paynly power none myght deparie neyther daye night luſty life ladde whych time childe ſhe right inly fayre goodly ſyght thelagonius ſothneſſe hight afterwarde wel reherſe proceſſe wexe manly man ſubtyll ſecret prouidence crafte experyence maugre enchauntementes olde ſtale awaye ſhe might holde fynally fate conclude connynge crafte delude men ſcaped fro hande went large fre lande thinge litell auayle waye gan ſayle ſleyght litell whyle yblowe vp yle ¶where calipha ſyſter circe crowned quene held ſceptre ī peace whoſe craftes ſo mighty ſo ſtrong maugre ſhe held ful longe ſhe ſothe ſpeake womanhede bounte fredome goodlyhead surely ſo ſoueraygne excellence mine abode none offence ſoeuer therat crye clappe laſte ſcaped fro trappe came yle ryght lyne ſpecyally high power diuine ordayned yore myracle ſpirituall oracle man haue temple sodayne anſwere liſt enquere queſtions demaundes ſoules ſhall eke befall men dead grauen vnder ſtone gan axe temple anone mine auentures ſhould ſewe man might fate eſchewe like mine entent aunſwere full conuenient saue befalleth ſoule gone diffinicion vnto none thinge aſſoyle accordeth right reſerued vnto goddes myght excedeth reaſon wyt man fro thenſe forth ſayle gan driuen wynde parte ſuccoured lyke haue deuoured ¶of karibdes profounde well syrines meremaydens dwell fro breſt ſcales ſiluer ſhene theyr ſhape fiſhes freſhe clene ouermore kinde doth compaſſe appeare feminine face like virgin nature without ſpot vndefouled pure cuſtome wawes flete ſonge ſo heauenly ſwete aungelike full armonye veryly ſugred melodye rauiſhe would man alyue inly ioye almoſt herte ryue make man ſodayne high pleaſaunce forget ſelfe leſe remembraunce deuoyde clene owne thought tyl vnwarely miſchiefe brought theyr ſonge take kepe ſhall brought mortall ſlepe anone yt maye withdrawe wil drenche ſhippe lowe vnder wawe thus ſweteneſſe theyr heauenly ſowne bringeth man confuſyon ſo euer theyr bondes paſſe ¶but lyfe ſcaped grace mine eares waxe gommes clere ſtopped ſo ne might heare touche werble theyr inſtrumentes wherby reaſon man blinded fynally ſubtyltee men eſcaped free saylinge forth mate werineſſe till came vp full great diſtreſſe ¶at phenice toke anone lande caſte anker ſhippes bande ſothly fell v full vnfayre ¶for people cruell contrayre onely malice fell anone ſlewe men almoſt euerychone treaſour good litell berafte thē ladde fewe theim lefte alone toke theim put priſon bliue thus hath fortune lad daunce litell ioye plentye miſchaunce whoſe daunger learned experte fall miſchiefe pouerte great dole ſorowe full breſt ſea land south eaſt come vnto preſence haue declared playnly ſentence min auentures worthineſſe truſte onely faythfulneſſe haue ſpecyall haue reherſed tolde hyghneſſe beſt wyſe without doth ſuffyſe though herte conſtrayned ſore thilke time vlixes ſpake helde peace ful heuy lokinge ¶and ydumeus like gentyll kinge comforted euer might buſy herte light beſought heuineſſe lete longe hym lyſt crete abide made ſuerte ſhould fare alſo wel wante maye eaſe ſorowe ſome gan apeaſe rage drewe vnto ende leue toke ſayde would wende lande home countre ¶but fyrſt kinge fredome bounte gaue vnto hym great rycheſſe arraye ſoeuer paye golde treaſour many thinges partynge theſe two kynges ſhippes liſt ſayle redy ſtuffed meyne vitayle thus vlixes gan redy make hath leue fully take haſted toke anone ſea gan ſayle towarde countre fyrſte wente kinge alphenon whych paſſingly affeccion ſe vlixes home comynge deſyrous ouer thynge haue newly acqueyntaunce vnto inly great pleſaunce heare talke eloquence wiſedome high prudence ſmerte receyued playnly glad herte euer yet maner man sithen tyme worlde began ¶and encreaſe felycyte herde firſt penolopee trewe wife without ſpot blame yet grene noble fame lorde longe abſēce thought dede neuer offence ſothly chere dede throughout grece example womanhede yet ſhe bokes lyſt expreſſe throughout ye world myrrour fayreneſſe amonge grekes borne hyeſt blode called auctours fayre good yet ſaye bokes doubtles neuer none ſo great preſe ſhe kepte chaunginge newe vnto lorde euer ylyke trewe herte aye one parted twayne ſhe called quene ſoueraygne wifely trouthe bokes olde ofte finde herte would colde tourne pale fro lorde ſo ferre cloſet heare werre dread ſhe feare eke quake fantaſyes lordes ſake abſence eue morowe death vnto importable ſorowe aye ſothe ioye game fell ſhe herde hector name place anone ſhe fell ſwowne gan ſelfe teares drowne womanhead ſo ſhe aferde heare ſlaughter mortall ſwerde leſt lorde knyghtly ſurquedrye fortune fall ieopardye ſorte mette worthy knight ſeld neuer ſhe felte herte lyght many dreame nightes gaſte ſiege laſte euery playe venym ſyght ſhe owne knight worlde ioye ſhe none high lowe playnly one whoſe ſake myrth ſhe refuſeth ſo herte muſeth woman thinge good melancolye meued bloud let aduerte wyſedome yſee remembre penolope deſerte leſt blamed oh guido thou ſhouldeſt aſhamed ſaye wiues thinge wele good fayth ferre fele though one two amonge offence good prouidence therof nothinge wite though guydo bokes endite ¶the varyaunce heleyne criſeyde ¶or medea ſorowe deyde let agayne ryght equyte wifely trouth penolope maydenhode yonge polycene goodneſſe hecuba quene caſſandra eke ſtedfaſtneſſe take vnkindneſſe pantaſyll withoute variaunce put togyther balaunce ye ſhal
